Nehemiah 5 13 [D] . . . . jah qaþ alla gamainþs: amen. jah hazidedun fraujan jah gatawidedun þata waurd alla so managei.
Nehemiah 5 14 [D] jah fram þamma daga ei anabauþ mis ei weisjau fauramaþleis ize in Iudaia, fram jera ·k· und jer ·l· jah anþar Arta[r]ksairksaus þiudanis ·ib· jera, ik jah broþrjus meinai hlaif fauramaþleis meinis ni matidedum.
Nehemiah 5 15 [D] iþ fauramaþljos þaiei weisun faura mis kauridedun þo managein jah nemun at im hlaibans jah wein jah nauhþanuh silubris sikle ·m·, jah skalkos ize fraujinodedun þizai managein; iþ ik ni tawida swa faura andwairþja agisis gudis.
Nehemiah 5 16 [D] jah waurstw þizos baurgswaddjaus inswinþida, jah þaurp ni gastaistald, jah þiwos meinai jah allai þai galisanans du þamma waurstwa.
Nehemiah 5 17 [D] jah Iudaieis jah þai fauramaþljos ·r· jah ·n· gumane jah þai qimandans at unsis us þiudom þaim bisunjane unsis ana biuda meinamma andnumanai weisun.
Nehemiah 5 18 [D] jah was fraquman dagis hvizuh stiur ·a· lamba gawalida ·q· jah gaits [·a·] gamanwida was mis; jah bi ·i· dagans gaf wein allai þizai filusnai jah allai þizai managein; jah ana þo alla hlaif fauramaþleis meinis ni sokida, in þis ei ni kauridedjau þo managein in þaim waurstwam . . . .

Nehemiah 6 14 [D] . . . . (praufe)te, þaiei þrafstidedun mik.
Nehemiah 6 15 [D] jah ustauhana warþ so baurgswaddjus ·e· jah ·k· daga men(oþis) (Alulis), ·n· dage jah ·b·
Nehemiah 6 16 [D] jah warþ, swe hausidedun fiands unsarai allai, jah ohtedun allos þiudos þos bisunjane unsis, jah atdraus agis in au(g)ona ize abraba; jah ufkunþedun þatei fram guda unsaramma warþ usfulliþ þata waurstw.
Nehemiah 6 17 [D] jah in dagam jainaim managai weisun þize reikjane Iudaie, þaiei sandidedun aipistulans du Tobeiin, jah Tobeias du im.
Nehemiah 6 18 [D] managai auk in Iudaia ufaiþjai weisun imma, unte megs was Saixaineiins, sunaus Aieirins, jah Ioanan sunus is nam dauhtar Maisaullamis, sunaus Barakeiins, du qenai.
Nehemiah 6 19 [D] jah rodidedun du imma wai(la) in andwairþja meinamma, jah waurda meina spillodedun imma, jah aipistulans insandida Tobeias ogjan mik.

Matthew 5 15 [CA] . . . . ak ana lukarnastaþin, jah liuteiþ allaim þaim in þamma garda.
Matthew 5 16 [CA] swa liuhtjai liuhaþ izwar in andwairþja manne, ei gasaihvaina izwara goda waurstwa jah hauhjaina attan izwarana þana in himinam.
Matthew 5 17 [CA] ni hugjaiþ ei qemjau gatairan witoþ aiþþau praufetuns; ni qam gatairan, ak usfulljan.
Matthew 5 18 [CA] amen auk qiþa izwis: und þatei usleiþiþ himins jah airþa, jota ains aiþþau ains striks ni usleiþiþ af witoda, unte allata wairþiþ.
Matthew 5 19 [CA] iþ saei nu gatairiþ aina anabusne þizo minnistono jah laisjai swa mans, minnista haitada in þiudangardjai himine; iþ saei taujiþ jah laisjai swa, sah mikils haitada in þiudangardjai himine.
Matthew 5 20 [CA] qiþa auk izwis þatei nibai managizo wairþiþ izwaraizos garaihteins þau þize bokarje jah Fareisaie, ni þau qimiþ in þiudangardjai himine.
Matthew 5 21 [CA] hausideduþ þatei qiþan ist þaim airizam: ni maurþrjais; iþ saei maurþreiþ skula wairþiþ stauai.
Matthew 5 22 [CA] aþþan ik qiþa izwis þatei hvazuh modags broþr seinamma sware, skula wairþiþ stauai; iþ saei qiþiþ broþr seinamma raka, skula wairþiþ gaqumþai; aþþan saei qiþiþ dwala, skula wairþiþ in gaiainnan funins.
Matthew 5 23 [CA] jabai nu bairais aibr þein du hunslastada jah jainar gamuneis þatei broþar þeins habaiþ hva bi þuk,
Matthew 5 24 [CA] aflet jainar þo giba þeina in andwairþja hunslastadis jah gagg faurþis gasibjon broþr þeinamma, jah biþe atgaggands atbair þo giba þeina.
Matthew 5 25 [CA] sijais waila hugjands andastauin þeinamma sprauto, und þatei is in wiga miþ imma, ibai hvan atgibai þuk sa andastaua stauin, jah sa staua þuk atgibai andbahta, jah in karkara galagjaza.
Matthew 5 26 [CA] amen qiþa þus: ni usgaggis jainþro, unte usgibis þana minnistan kintu.
Matthew 5 27 [CA] hausideduþ þatei qiþan ist: ni horinos.
Matthew 5 28 [CA] aþþan ik qiþa izwis, þatei hvazuh saei saihviþ qinon du luston izos, ju gahorinoda izai in hairtin seinamma.
Matthew 5 29 [CA] iþ jabai augo þein þata taihswo marzjai þuk, usstagg ita jah wairp af þus; batizo ist auk þus ei fraqistnai ains liþiwe þeinaize, jah ni allata leik þein gadriusai in gaiainnan.
Matthew 5 30 [CA] jah jabai taihswo þeina handus marzjai þuk, afmait þo jah wairp af þus; batizo ist auk þus ei fraqistnai ains liþiwe þeinaize, jah ni allata leik þein gadriusai in gaiainnan.
Matthew 5 31 [CA] qiþanuh þan ist þatei hvazuh saei afletai qen, gibai izai afstassais bokos.
Matthew 5 32 [CA] iþ ik qiþa izwis þatei hvazuh saei afletiþ qen seina, inuh fairina kalkinassaus, taujiþ þo horinon; jah sa ize afsatida liugaiþ, horinoþ.
Matthew 5 33 [CA] aftra hausideduþ þatei qiþan ist þaim airizam: ni ufarswarais, iþ usgibais fraujin aiþans þeinans.
Matthew 5 34 [CA] aþþan ik qiþa izwis ni swaran allis, ni bi himina, unte stols ist gudis;
Matthew 5 35 [CA] nih bi airþai, unte fotubaurd ist fotiwe is; nih bi Iairusaulwmai, unte baurgs ist þis mikilins þiudanis;
Matthew 5 36 [CA] nih bi haubida þeinamma swarais, unte ni magt ain tagl hveit aiþþau swart gataujan.
Matthew 5 37 [CA] sijaiþ~þan waurd izwar: ja, ja; ne, ne; iþ þata managizo þaim us þamma ubilin ist.
Matthew 5 38 [CA] hausideduþ þatei qiþan ist: augo und augin, jah tunþu und tunþau.
Matthew 5 39 [CA] iþ ik qiþa izwis ni andstandan allis þamma unseljin; ak jabai hvas þuk stautai bi taihswon þeina kinnu, wandei imma jah þo anþara.
Matthew 5 40 [CA] jah þamma wiljandin miþ þus staua jah paida þeina niman, aflet imma jah wastja.
Matthew 5 41 [CA] jah jabai hvas þuk ananauþjai rasta aina, gaggais miþ imma twos.
Matthew 5 42 [CA] þamma bidjandin þuk gibais, jah þamma wiljandin af þus leihvan sis ni uswandjais.
Matthew 5 43 [CA] hausideduþ þatei qiþan ist: frijos nehvundjan þeinana, jah fiais fiand þeinana.
Matthew 5 44 [CA] aþþan ik qiþa izwis: frijoþ fijands izwarans, þiuþjaiþ þans wrikandans izwis, waila taujaiþ þaim hatjandam izwis, jah bidjaiþ bi þans usþriutandans izwis,
Matthew 5 45 [CA] ei wairþaiþ sunjus attins izwaris þis in himinam, unte sunnon seina urranneiþ ana ubilans jah godans, jah rigneiþ ana garaihtans jah ana inwindans.
Matthew 5 46 [CA] jabai auk frijoþ þans frijondans izwis ainans, hvo mizdono habaiþ? niu jah þai þiudo þata samo taujand?
Matthew 5 47 [CA] jah jabai goleiþ þans frijonds izwarans þatainei, hve managizo taujiþ? niu jah motarjos þata samo taujand?
Matthew 5 48 [CA] sijaiþ nu jus fullatojai, swaswe atta izwar sa in himinam fullatojis ist.
Matthew 6 1 [CA] Atsaihviþ armaion izwara ni taujan in andwairþja manne du saihvan im; aiþþau laun ni habaiþ fram attin izwaramma þamma in himinam.
Matthew 6 2 [CA] þan nu taujais armaion, ni haurnjais faura þus, swaswe þai liutans taujand in gaqumþim jah in garunsim, ei hauhjaindau fram mannam; amen qiþa izwis: andnemun mizdon seina.
Matthew 6 3 [CA] iþ þuk taujandan armaion ni witi hleidumei þeina, hva taujiþ taihswo þeina,
Matthew 6 4 [CA] ei sijai so armahairtiþa þeina in fulhsnja, jah atta þeins saei saihviþ in fulhsnja, usgibiþ þus in bairhtein.
Matthew 6 5 [CA] jah þan bidjaiþ, ni sijaiþ swaswe þai liutans, unte frijond in gaqumþim jah waihstam plapjo standandans bidjan, ei gaumjaindau mannam. Amen, qiþa izwis þatei haband mizdon seina.
Matthew 6 6 [CA] iþ þu þan bidjais, gagg in heþjon þeina jah galukands haurdai þeinai bidei du attin þeinamma þamma in fulhsnja, jah atta þeins saei saihviþ in fulhsnja, usgibiþ þus in bairhtein.
Matthew 6 7 [CA] bidjandansuþ~þan ni filuwaurdjaiþ, swaswe þai þiudo; þugkeiþ im auk ei in filuwaurdein seinai andhausjaindau.

Matthew 6 12 [CA] jah aflet uns þatei skulans sijaima, swaswe jah weis afletam þaim skulam unsaraim.
Matthew 6 13 [CA] jah ni briggais uns in fraistubnjai, ak lausei uns af þamma ubilin; unte þeina ist þiudangardi jah mahts jah wulþus in aiwins. amen.

Matthew 6 19 [CA] ni huzdjaiþ izwis huzda ana airþai, þarei malo jah nidwa frawardeiþ, jah þarei þiubos ufgraband jah hlifand.

Matthew 10 41 [CA] sa andnimands praufetu in namin praufetaus mizdon praufetaus nimiþ, jah sa andnimands garaihtana in namin garaihtis mizdon garaihtis nimiþ.
Matthew 10 42 [CA] jah saei gadragkeiþ ainana þize minnistane stikla kaldis watins þatainei in namin siponeis, amen qiþa izwis, ei ni fraqisteiþ mizdon seinai.
Matthew 11 1 [CA] Jah warþ, biþe usfullida Iesus anabiudands þaim twalif siponjam seinaim, ushof sik jainþro du laisjan jah merjan and baurgs ize.
Matthew 11 2 [CA] iþ Iohannes gahausjands in karkarai waurstwa Xristaus, insandjands bi siponjam seinaim qaþ du imma:
Matthew 11 3 [CA] þû is sa qimanda þau anþarizuh beidaima?
Matthew 11 4 [CA] jah andhafjands Iesus qaþ du im: gaggandans gateihiþ Iohanne þatei gahauseiþ jah gasaihviþ.
Matthew 11 5 [CA] blindai ussaihvand, jah haltai gaggand, þrutsfillai hrainjai wairþand, jah baudai gahausjand, jah dauþai urreisand, jah unledai wailamerjanda:
Matthew 11 6 [CA] jah audags ist hvazuh saei ni gamarzjada in mis.
Matthew 11 7 [CA] at þaim þan afgaggandam, dugann Iesus qiþan þaim manageim bi Iohannen: hva usiddjeduþ ana auþida saihvan? raus fram winda wagidata?
Matthew 11 8 [CA] akei hva usiddjeduþ saihvan? mannan hnasqjaim wastjom gawasidana? sai, þaiei hnasqjaim wasidai sind, in gardim þiudane sind.
Matthew 11 9 [CA] akei hva usiddjeduþ saihvan? praufetu? jai, qiþa izwis: jah managizo praufetau.
Matthew 11 10 [CA] sa ist auk bi þanei gameliþ ist: sai, ik insandja aggilu meinana faura þus, saei gamanweiþ wig þeinana faura þus.
Matthew 11 11 [CA] amen, qiþa izwis: ni urrais in baurim qinono maiza Iohanne þamma daupjandin; iþ sa minniza in þiudangardjai himine maiza imma ist.
Matthew 11 12 [CA] framuh þan þaim dagam Iohannis þis daupjandins und hita þiudangardi himine anamahtjada, jah anamahtjandans frawilwand þo.
Matthew 11 13 [CA] allai auk praufeteis jah witoþ und Iohanne fauraqeþun;
Matthew 11 14 [CA] jah jabai wildedeiþ miþniman, sa ist Helias, saei skulda qiman.
Matthew 11 15 [CA] saei habai au(sona) (hausjandona), (ga)hausja(i).
Matthew 11 16 [CA] (hve) (nu) (galeiko) þata ku(ni)? (Galeik) (ist) (barnam) sitandam (in) (garunsim) (jah) (wopjan)dam anþar anþa(ris),
Matthew 11 17 [CA] (jah) (qiþan)dam: swiglodedum izw(is) (jah) ni plinsideduþ; huf(um) (jah) ni qainodeduþ.
Matthew 11 18 [CA] qam raihtis Iohan(nes) (nih) (mat)jands nih drigkan(ds) (jah) (qi)þand: unhulþ(on) (habaiþ).
Matthew 11 19 [CA] (qam) sa sunus mans (matjands) (jah) drigkands j(ah) (qiþand): (sai), (man)na afetja jah af(drug)kja, (mo)tarje frijonds jah frawaurhtaize. jah uswaurhta gadomida warþ handugei fram barnam seinaim.
Matthew 11 20 [CA] þanuh dugann idweitjan baurgim, in þaimei waurþun þos managistons mahteis is, (þatei) (ni) (idreigodedun) sik.
Matthew 11 21 [CA] (wai) (þus) (Kaurazein), (wai) (þ)us Beþ(saïdan); (unte) (iþ) (wa)urþeina (in) (Twre) (jah) (Seidon)e landa mah(teis) (þos) (waur)þanons in izwis, (airis) (þ)au in sakkau jah azgon (idreig)odedeina.
Matthew 11 22 [CA] sweþauh qi(þa) (izwis): Twrim jah Seidonim (sutizo) (wa)irþiþ in daga stau(os) (þau) (izwis).
Matthew 11 23 [CA] jah þu Kafarna(um), (þu) (und) (hi)min ushauhida, (dalaþ) (und) (halj)a galeiþis: (unte) (jabai) (in) (S)audaumjam (waur)þe(ina) (m)ahteis þos waurþanons in izwis, aiþþau eis weseina und hina dag.
Matthew 11 24 [CA] sweþauh qiþa izwis þatei airþai Saudaumje sutizo wairþiþ in daga stauos þau þus.

Matthew 25 38 [C] hvanuh þan þuk sehvum gast jah galaþodedum? aiþþau naqadana jah wasidedum?

Matthew 25 40 [C] jah andhafjands sa þiudans qiþiþ du im: amen, qiþa izwis: jah þanei tawideduþ ainamma þize minnistane broþre meinaize, mis tawideduþ.
Matthew 25 41 [C] þanuh qiþiþ jah þaim af hleidumein ferai: gaggiþ fairra mis, jus fraqiþanans, in fon þata aiweino, þata manwido unhulþin jah aggilum is.
Matthew 25 42 [C] unte gredags was jan~ni gebuþ mis matjan; afþaursiþs was jan~ni dragkideduþ mik;
Matthew 25 43 [C] gasts <was> jan~ni galaþ(ode)duþ mik; naqaþs jan~ni waside(duþ) mik; siuks jah in karkarai jan~ni gaweisodeduþ meina.
Matthew 25 44 [C] þanuh andhafjand jah þai qiþandans: frauja, hvan þuk sehvum gredagana aiþþau afþaursidana aiþþau gast aiþþau naqadana aiþþau siukana aiþþau in karkarai jan~ni andbahtidedeima þus?
Matthew 25 45 [C] þanuh andhafjiþ im qiþands: amen, qiþa izwis, jah þanei ni tawideduþ ainamma þize leitilane, mis ni tawideduþ.
Matthew 25 46 [C] jah galeiþand þai in balwein aiweinon, iþ þai garaihtans in libain aiweinon.

Matthew 27 1 [C] At maurgin þan waurþanana, garuni nemun allai þai gudjans jah þai . . . .
Matthew 27 2 [CA] jah gabindandans ina gatauhun jah anafulhun ina Pauntiau Peilatau kindina.
Matthew 27 3 [CA] þanuh gasaihvands Iudas sa galewjands ina þatei du stauai gatauhans warþ, idreigonds gawandida þans þrins tiguns silubrinaize gudjam jah sinistam
Matthew 27 4 [CA] qiþands: frawaurhta mis galewjands bloþ swikn. iþ eis qeþun: hva kara unsis? þu witeis.
Matthew 27 5 [CA] jah atwairpands þaim silubr<ein>am in alh aflaiþ, jah galeiþands ushaihah sik.
Matthew 27 6 [CA] iþ þai gudjans nimandans þans skattans qeþun: ni skuld ist lagjan þans in kaurbaunan, unte andawairþi bloþis ist.
Matthew 27 7 [CA] garuni þan nimandans usbauhtedun us þaim þana akr kasjins, du usfilhan ana gastim.
Matthew 27 8 [CA] duþþe haitans warþ akrs jains akrs bloþis und hina dag.
Matthew 27 9 [CA] þanuh usfullnoda þata qiþano þairh Iairaimian praufetu qiþandan: jah usnemun þrins tiguns silubreinaize andawairþi þis wairþodins, þatei garahnidedun fram sunum Israelis,
Matthew 27 10 [CA] jah atgebun ins und akra kasjins, swaswe anabauþ mis frauja.
Matthew 27 11 [CA] iþ Iesus stoþ faura kindina, jah frah ina sa kindins qiþands: þu is þiudans Iudaie? iþ Iesus qaþ du imma: þu qiþis.
Matthew 27 12 [CA] jah miþþanei wrohiþs was fram þaim gudjam jah sinistam, ni waiht andhof.
Matthew 27 13 [CA] þanuh qaþ du imma Peilatus: niu hauseis hvan filu ana þuk weitwodjand?
Matthew 27 14 [CA] jah ni andhof imma wiþra ni ainhun waurde, swaswe sildaleikida sa kindins filu.
Matthew 27 15 [CA] and dulþ þan hvarjoh biuhts was sa kindins fraletan ainana þizai managein bandjan, þanei wildedun.
Matthew 27 16 [CA] habaidedunuh þan bandjan gatarhidana <haitanana> Barabban.
Matthew 27 17 [CA] gaqumanaim þan im, qaþ im Peilatus: hvana wileiþ ei fraletau izwis? Barabban þau Iesu, saei haitada Xristus?
Matthew 27 18 [CA] wissa auk þatei in neiþis atgebun ina.

Matthew 27 42 [CA] . . . . Israelis ist, atsteigadau nu af þamma galgin [ei gasaihvaima] jah galaubjam imma.
Matthew 27 43 [CA] trauaida du guda; lausjadau nu ina, jabai wili ina; qaþ auk þatei gudis im sunus.
Matthew 27 44 [CA] þatuh samo jah þai waidedjans þai miþushramidans imma idweitidedun imma.
Matthew 27 45 [CA] fram saihston þan hveilai warþ riqis ufar allai airþai und hveila niundon.
Matthew 27 46 [CA] iþ þan bi hveila niundon ufhropida Iesus stibnai mikilai qiþands: helei, helei, lima sibakþani, þatei ist: guþ meins, guþ meins, duhve mis bilaist?
Matthew 27 47 [CA] iþ sumai þize jainar standandane gahausjandans qeþun þatei Helian wopeiþ sa.
Matthew 27 48 [CA] jah suns þragida ains us im jah nam swamm fulljands aketis, jah lagjands ana raus draggkida ina.
Matthew 27 49 [CA] iþ þai anþarai qeþun: let, ei saihvam, qimaiu Helias nasjan ina.
Matthew 27 50 [CA] iþ Iesus aftra hropjands stibnai mikilai aflailot ahman.
Matthew 27 51 [CA] jah þan faurhah alhs diskritnoda in twa, iupaþro und dalaþ, jah airþa inreiraida, jah stainos disskritnodedun,
Matthew 27 52 [CA] jah hlaiwasnos usluknodedun, jah managa leika þize ligandane weihaize urrisun.
Matthew 27 53 [CA] jah usgaggandans us hlaiwasnom afar urrist is innatgaggandans in þo weihon baurg jah ataugidedun sik managaim.
Matthew 27 54 [CA] iþ hundafaþs jah þai miþ imma witandans Iesua, gasaihvandans þo reiron jah þo waurþanona, ohtedun abraba, qiþandans: bi sunjai gudis sunus ist sa.
Matthew 27 55 [CA] wesunuh þan jainar qinons managos fairraþro saihvandeins, þozei laistidedun afar Iesua fram Galeilaia, andbahtjandeins imma,
Matthew 27 56 [CA] in þaimei was Marja so Magdalene, jah Marja so Iakobis jah Iosezis aiþei, jah aiþei suniwe Zaibaidaiaus.
Matthew 27 57 [CA] iþ þan seiþu warþ, qam manna gabigs af Areimaþaias þizuh namo Iosef, saei jah silba siponida Iesua.
Matthew 27 58 [CA] sah atgaggands du Peilatau baþ þis leikis Iesuis. þanuh Peilatus uslaubida giban þata leik.
Matthew 27 59 [CA] jah nimands þata leik Iosef biwand ita sabana hrainjamma
Matthew 27 60 [CA] jah galagida ita in niujamma seinamma hlaiwa þatei ushuloda ana staina jah faurwalwjands staina mikilamma daurons þis hlaiwis galaiþ.
Matthew 27 61 [CA] wasuh þan jainar Marja Magdalene jah so anþara Marja sitandeins andwairþis þamma hlaiwa.
Matthew 27 62 [CA] iftumin þan daga, saei ist afar paraskaiwein, gaqemun auhumistans gudjans jah Fareisaieis du Peilatau

Mark 1 1 [CA] Anastodeins aiwaggeljons Iesuis Xristaus sunaus gudis.
Mark 1 2 [CA] swe gameliþ ist in Esaïin praufetau: sai, ik insandja aggilu meinana faura þus, saei gamanweiþ wig þeinana faura þus.
Mark 1 3 [CA] Stibna wopjandins in auþidai: manweiþ wig fraujins, raihtos waurkeiþ staigos gudis unsaris.
Mark 1 4 [CA] was Iohannes daupjands in auþidai jah merjands daupein idreigos du aflageinai frawaurhte.
Mark 1 5 [CA] jah usiddjedun du imma all Iudaialand jah Iairusaulwmeis, jah daupidai wesun allai in Iaurdane ahvai fram imma, andhaitandans frawaurhtim seinaim.

Mark 1 27 [CA] jah afslauþnodedun allai sildaleikjandans, swaei sokidedun miþ sis misso qiþandans: hva sijai þata? hvo so laiseino so niujo, ei miþ waldufnja jah ahmam þaim unhrainjam anabiudiþ jah ufhausjand imma?

Mark 1 31 [CA] jah duatgaggands urraisida þo undgreipands handu izos, jah aflailot þo so brinno suns, jah andbahtida im.

Mark 2 1 [CA] Jah galaiþ aftra in Kafarnaum afar dagans, jah gafrehun þatei in garda ist.

Mark 2 3 [CA] jah qemun at imma usliþan bairandans, hafanana fram fidworim.
Mark 2 4 [CA] jah ni magandans nehva qiman imma faura manageim, andhulidedun hrot þarei was Iesus jah usgrabandans insailidedun þata badi [jah fralailotun] ana þammei lag sa usliþa.
Mark 2 5 [CA] gasaihvands þan Iesus galaubein ize qaþ du þamma usliþin: barnilo, afletanda þus frawaurhteis þeinos.
Mark 2 6 [CA] wesunuh þan sumai þize bokarje jainar sitandans jah þagkjandans sis in hairtam seinaim:
Mark 2 7 [CA] hva sa swa rodeiþ naiteinins? hvas mag afletan frawaurhtins, niba ains guþ?
Mark 2 8 [CA] jah suns ufkunnands Iesus ahmin seinamma þatei swa þai mitodedun sis, qaþ du im: duhve mitoþ þata in hairtam izwaraim?
Mark 2 9 [CA] hvaþar ist azetizo du qiþan þamma usliþin: afletanda þus frawaurhteis þeinos, þau qiþan: urreis jah nim þata badi þeinata jah gagg?
Mark 2 10 [CA] aþþan ei witeiþ þatei waldufni habaiþ sunus mans ana airþai afletan frawaurhtins, qaþ du þamma usliþin:
Mark 2 11 [CA] þus qiþa: urreis nimuh þata badi þein jah gagg du garda þeinamma.
Mark 2 12 [CA] jah urrais suns jah ushafjands badi usiddja faura andwairþja allaize, swaswe usgeisnodedun allai jah hauhidedun mikiljandans guþ, qiþandans þatei aiw swa ni gasehvun.
Mark 2 13 [CA] jah galaiþ aftra faur marein, jah all manageins iddjedun du imma, jah laisida ins.
Mark 2 14 [CA] jah hvarbonds gasahv Laiwwi þana Alfaiaus sitandan at motai jah qaþ du imma: gagg afar mis. Jah usstandands iddja afar imma.
Mark 2 15 [CA] jah warþ, biþe is anakumbida in garda is, jah managai motarjos jah frawaurhtai miþanakumbidedun Iesua jah siponjam is; wesun auk managai jah iddjedun afar imma.
Mark 2 16 [CA] jah þai bokarjos jah Fareisaieis gasaihvandans ina matjandan miþ þaim motarjam jah frawaurhtaim, qeþun du þaim siponjam is: hva ist þatei miþ motarjam jah frawaurhtaim matjiþ jah driggkiþ?
Mark 2 17 [CA] jah gahausjands Iesus qaþ du im: ni þaurbun swinþai lekeis, ak þai ubilaba habandans; ni qam laþon uswaurhtans, ak frawaurhtans.
Mark 2 18 [CA] jah wesun siponjos Iohannis jah Fareisaieis fastandans; jah atiddjedun jah qeþun du imma: duhve siponjos Iohannes jah Fareisaieis fastand, iþ þai þeinai siponjos ni fastand?
Mark 2 19 [CA] jah qaþ im Iesus: ibai magun sunjus bruþfadis, und þatei miþ im ist bruþfaþs, fastan? swa lagga hveila swe miþ sis haband bruþfad, ni magun fastan.
Mark 2 20 [CA] aþþan atgaggand dagos þan afnimada af im sa bruþfaþs, jah þan fastand in jainamma daga.
Mark 2 21 [CA] ni manna plat fanins niujis siujiþ ana snagan fairnjana; ibai afnimai fullon af þamma sa niuja þamma fairnjin, jah wairsiza gataura wairþiþ.
Mark 2 22 [CA] ni manna giutiþ wein juggata in balgins fairnjans; ibai aufto distairai wein þata niujo þans balgins, jah wein usgutniþ, jah þai balgeis fraqistnand; ak wein juggata in balgins niujans giutand.
Mark 2 23 [CA] jah warþ þairhgaggan imma sabbato daga þairh atisk, jah dugunnun siponjos is skewjandans raupjan ahsa.
Mark 2 24 [CA] jah Fareisaieis qeþun du imma: sai, hva taujand siponjos þeinai sabbatim þatei ni skuld ist?
Mark 2 25 [CA] jah is qaþ du im: niu ussuggwuþ aiw hva gatawida Daweid, þan þaurfta jah gredags was, is jah þai miþ imma?
Mark 2 26 [CA] hvaiwa galaiþ in gard gudis uf Abiaþara gudjin jah hlaibans faurlageinais matida, þanzei ni skuld ist matjan niba ainaim gudjam, jah gaf jah þaim miþ sis wisandam?

Mark 3 5 [CA] jah ussaihvands ins miþ moda, gaurs in daubiþos hairtins ize qaþ du þamma mann: ufrakei þo handu þeina! jah ufrakida, jah gastoþ aftra so handus is.

Mark 3 9 [CA] jah qaþ þaim siponjam seinaim ei skip habaiþ wesi at imma in þizos manageins, ei ni þraiheina ina.

Mark 3 11 [CA] jah ahmans unhrainjans, þaih þan ina gasehvun, drusun du imma jah hropidedun qiþandans þatei þu is sunus gudis.
Mark 3 12 [CA] jah filu andbait ins ei ina ni gaswikunþidedeina.

Mark 3 18 [CA] jah Andraian jah Filippu jah Barþaulaumaiu jah Matþaiu jah Þoman jah Iakobu þana Alfaiaus jah Þaddaiu jah Seimona þana Kananeiten

Mark 3 23 [CA] jah athaitands ins in gajukom qaþ du im: hvaiwa mag Satanas Satanan uswairpan?

Mark 3 26 [CA] jah jabai Satana usstoþ ana sik silban jah gadailiþs warþ, ni mag gastandan, ak andi habaiþ.
Mark 3 27 [CA] ni manna mag kasa swinþis galeiþands in gard is wilwan, niba faurþis þana swinþan gabindiþ; jah <þan> þana gard is diswilwai.
Mark 3 28 [CA] amen, qiþa izwis, þatei allata afletada þata frawaurhte sunum manne, jah naiteinos swa managos swaswe wajamerjand;
Mark 3 29 [CA] aþþan saei wajamereiþ ahman weihana ni habaiþ fralet aiw, ak skula ist aiweinaizos frawaurhtais.
Mark 3 30 [CA] unte qeþun: ahman unhrainjana habaiþ.
Mark 3 31 [CA] jah qemun þan aiþei is jah broþrjus is jah uta standandona insandidedun du imma, haitandona ina.
Mark 3 32 [CA] jah setun bi ina managei; qeþun þan du imma: sai, aiþei þeina jah broþrjus þeinai jah swistrjus þeinos uta sokjand þuk.
Mark 3 33 [CA] jah andhof im qiþands: hvo ist so aiþei meina aiþþau þai broþrjus meinai?
Mark 3 34 [CA] jah bisaihvands bisunjane þans bi sik sitandans qaþ: sai, aiþei meina jah þai broþrjus meinai.

Mark 4 1 [CA] Jah aftra [Iesus] dugann laisjan at marein, jah galesun sik du imma manageins filu, swaswe ina galeiþan<dan> in skip gasitan in marein; jah alla so managei wiþra marein ana staþa was.
Mark 4 2 [CA] jah laisida ins in gajukom manag jah qaþ im in laiseinai seinai:
Mark 4 3 [CA] hauseiþ! sai, urrann sa saiands du saian fraiwa seinamma.
Mark 4 4 [CA] jah warþ, miþþanei saiso, sum raihtis gadraus faur wig, jah qemun fuglos jah fretun þata.
Mark 4 5 [CA] anþaruþ~þan gadraus ana stainahamma, þarei ni habaida airþa managa, jah suns urrann, in þizei ni habaida diupaizos airþos;
Mark 4 6 [CA] at sunnin þan urrinnandin ufbrann, jah unte ni habaida waurtins, gaþaursnoda.
Mark 4 7 [CA] jah sum gadraus in þaurnuns; jah ufarstigun þai þaurnjus jah afhvapidedun þata, jah akran ni gaf.
Mark 4 8 [CA] jah sum gadraus in airþa goda jah gaf akran urrinnando jah wahsjando, jah bar ain ·l· jah ain ·j· jah ain ·r·
Mark 4 9 [CA] jah qaþ: saei habai ausona hausjandona, gahausjai.
Mark 4 10 [CA] iþ biþe warþ sundro, frehun ina þai bi ina miþ þaim twalibim þizos gajukons.
Mark 4 11 [CA] jah qaþ im: izwis atgiban ist kunnan runa þiudangardjos gudis, iþ jainaim þaim uta in gajukom allata wairþiþ,
Mark 4 12 [CA] ei saihvandans saihvaina jah ni gaumjaina, jah hausjandans hausjaina jah ni fraþjaina, ibai hvan gawandjaina sik jah afletaindau im frawaurhteis.
Mark 4 13 [CA] jah qaþ du im: ni wituþ þo gajukon, jah hvaiwa allos þos gajukons kunneiþ?
Mark 4 14 [CA] sa saijands waurd saijiþ.
Mark 4 15 [CA] aþþan þai wiþra wig sind, þarei saiada þata waurd, jah þan gahausjand unkarjans, suns qimiþ Satanas jah usnimiþ waurd þata insaiano in hairtam ize.
Mark 4 16 [CA] jah <þai> sind samaleiko þai ana stainahamma saianans, þaiei þan hausjand þata waurd, suns miþ fahedai nimand ita
Mark 4 17 [CA] jah ni haband waurtins in sis, ak hveilahvairbai sind; þaþroh, biþe qimiþ aglo aiþþau wrakja in þis waurdis, suns gamarzjanda.
Mark 4 18 [CA] jah þai sind þai in þaurnuns saianans, þai waurd hausjandans,
Mark 4 19 [CA] jah saurgos þizos libainais jah afmarzeins gabeins jah þai bi þata anþar lustjus innatgaggandans afhvapjand þata waurd, jah akranalaus wairþiþ.
Mark 4 20 [CA] jah þai sind þai ana airþai þizai godon saianans, þaiei hausjand þata waurd jah andnimand jah akran bairand, ain ·l· jah ain ·j· jah ain ·r·
Mark 4 21 [CA] jah qaþ du im: ibai lukarn qimiþ duþe ei uf melan satjaidau aiþþau undar ligr? niu ei ana lukarnastaþan satjaidau?
Mark 4 22 [CA] nih allis ist hva fulginis þatei ni gabairhtjaidau: nih warþ analaugn, ak ei swikunþ wairþai.
Mark 4 23 [CA] jabai hvas habai ausona hausjandona, gahausjai.
Mark 4 24 [CA] jah qaþ du im: saihviþ, hva hauseiþ! in þizaiei mitaþ mitiþ, mitada izwis jah biaukada izwis þaim galaubjandam.
Mark 4 25 [CA] unte þishvammeh saei habaiþ gibada imma; jah saei ni habaiþ jah þatei habaiþ afnimada imma.
Mark 4 26 [CA] jah qaþ: swa ist þiudangardi gudis, swaswe jabai manna wairpiþ fraiwa ana airþa.
Mark 4 27 [CA] jah slepiþ jah urreisiþ naht jah daga, jah þata fraiw keiniþ jah liudiþ swe ni wait is.
Mark 4 28 [CA] silbo auk airþa akran bairiþ: frumist gras, þaþroh ahs, þaþroh fulliþ kaurnis in þamma ahsa.
Mark 4 29 [CA] þanuh biþe atgibada akran, suns insandeiþ gilþa, unte atist asans.
Mark 4 30 [CA] jah qaþ: hve galeikom þiudangardja gudis, aiþþau in hvileikai gajukon gabairam þo?
Mark 4 31 [CA] swe kaurno sinapis, þatei þan saiada ana airþa, minnist allaize fraiwe ist þize ana airþai;
Mark 4 32 [CA] jah þan saiada, urrinniþ jah wairþiþ allaize grase maist jah gataujiþ astans mikilans, swaswe magun uf skadau is fuglos himinis gabauan.

Mark 12 1 [CA] Jah dugann im in gajukom qiþan: weinagard ussatida manna jah bisatida ina faþom jah usgrof dal uf mesa jah gatimrida kelikn jah anafalh ina waurstwjam jah aflaiþ aljaþ.

Mark 15 1 [CA] Jah sunsaiw in maurgin garuni taujandans þai auhumistans gudjans miþ þaim sinistam jah bokarjam, jah alla so gafaurds gabindandans Iesu brahtedun ina at Peilatau.
Mark 15 2 [CA] jah frah ina Peilatus: þu is þiudans Iudaie? iþ is andhafjands qaþ du imma: þu qiþis.
Mark 15 3 [CA] jah wrohidedun ina þai auhumistans gudjans filu.
Mark 15 4 [CA] iþ Peilatus aftra frah ina qiþands: niu andhafjis ni waiht? sai, hvan filu ana þuk weitwodjand.
Mark 15 5 [CA] iþ Iesus þanamais <waiht> ni andhof, swaswe sildaleikida Peilatus.
Mark 15 6 [CA] iþ and dulþ hvarjoh fralailot im ainana bandjan þanei bedun.
Mark 15 7 [CA] wasuh þan sa haitana Barabbas miþ þaim miþ imma drobjandam gabundans, þaiei in auhjodau maurþr gatawidedun.

Mark 15 9 [CA] iþ Peilatus andhof im qiþands: wileidu fraleitan izwis þana þiudan Iudaie?
Mark 15 10 [CA] wissa auk þatei in neiþis atgebun ina þai auhumistans gudjans.
Mark 15 11 [CA] iþ þai auhumistans gudjans inwagidedun þo managein ei mais Barabban fralailoti im.
Mark 15 12 [CA] iþ Peilatus aftra andhafjands qaþ du im: hva nu wileiþ ei taujau þammei qiþiþ þiudan Iudaie?
Mark 15 13 [CA] iþ eis aftra hropidedun: ushramei ina.
Mark 15 14 [CA] iþ Peilatus qaþ du im: hva allis ubilis gatawida? iþ eis mais hropidedun: ushramei ina.
Mark 15 15 [CA] iþ Peilatus wiljands þizai managein fullafahjan, fralailot im þana Barabban, iþ Iesu atgaf usbliggwands, ei ushramiþs wesi.

Mark 15 18 [CA] jah dugunnun goljan ina: hails, þiudan Iudaie!

Mark 15 20 [CA] jah biþe bilailaikun ina andwasidedun ina þizai paurpurai jah gawasidedun ina wastjom swesaim. jah ustauhun ina ei ushramidedeina ina.
Mark 15 21 [CA] jah undgripun sumana manne, Seimona Kwreinaiu, qimandan af akra, attan Alaiksandraus jah Rufaus, ei nemi galgan is.

Mark 15 23 [CA] jah gebun imma drigkan wein miþ smwrna; iþ is ni nam.
Mark 15 24 [CA] jah ushramjandans ina disdailjand wastjos is wairpandans hlauta ana þos, hvarjizuh hva nemi.
Mark 15 25 [CA] wasuh þan hveila þridjo, jah ushramidedun ina.
Mark 15 26 [CA] jah was ufarmeli fairinos is ufarmeliþ: sa þiudans Iudaie.
Mark 15 27 [CA] jah miþ imma ushramidedun twans waidedjans, ainana af taihswon jah ainana af hleidumein is.
Mark 15 28 [CA] jah usfullnoda þata gamelido þata qiþando: jah miþ unsibjaim rahniþs was.
Mark 15 29 [CA] jah þai faurgaggandans wajameridedun ina, wiþondans haubida seina jah qiþandans: o sa gatairands þo alh jah bi þrins dagans gatimrjands þo,
Mark 15 30 [CA] nasei þuk silban jah atsteig af þamma galgin!
Mark 15 31 [CA] samaleiko jah þai auhumistans gudjans bilaikandans ina miþ sis misso miþ þaim bokarjam qeþun: anþarans ganasida, iþ sik silban ni mag ganasjan.
Mark 15 32 [CA] sa Xristus, sa þiudans Israelis, atsteigadau nu af þamma galgin, ei gasaihvaima jah galaubjaima. jah þai miþushramidans imma idweitidedun imma.
Mark 15 33 [CA] jah biþe warþ hveila saihsto, riqis warþ ana allai airþai und hveila niundon.
Mark 15 34 [CA] jah niundon hveilai wopida Iesus stibnai mikilai qiþands: ailoe ailoe, lima sibakþanei, þatei ist gaskeiriþ: guþ meins, guþ meins, duhve mis bilaist?
Mark 15 35 [CA] jah sumai þize atstandandane gahausjandans qeþun: sai, Helian wopeiþ.
Mark 15 36 [CA] þragjands þan ains jah gafulljands swam akeitis, galagjands ana raus, dragkida ina qiþands: let, ei saihvam qimaiu Helias athafjan ina.
Mark 15 37 [CA] iþ Iesus aftra letands stibna mikila uzon.
Mark 15 38 [CA] jah faur[a]hah als disskritnoda in twa iupaþro und dalaþ.
Mark 15 39 [CA] gasaihvands þan sa hundafaþs sa atstandands in andwairþja is þatei swa hropjands uzon, qaþ: bi sunjai, sa manna sa sunus was gudis.
Mark 15 40 [CA] wesunuþ~þan qinons fairraþro saihvandeins, in þaimei was Marja so Magdalene jah Marja Iakobis þis minnizins jah Iosezis aiþei jah Salome.
Mark 15 41 [CA] jah þan was in Galeilaia, jah laistidedun ina jah andbahtidedun imma, jah anþaros managos þozei miþiddjedun imma in Iairusalem.
Mark 15 42 [CA] jah juþan at andanahtja waurþanamma, unte was paraskaiwe, saei ist fruma sabbato,

Mark 15 44 [CA] iþ Peilatus sildaleikida ei is juþan gaswalt; jah athaitands þana hundafaþ frah ina jû~þan gadauþnodedi.

Mark 16 1 [CA] jah inwisandins sabbate dagis Marja so Magdalene jah Marja so Iakobis jah Salome usbauhtedun aromata, ei atgaggandeins gasalbodedeina ina.
Mark 16 2 [CA] jah filu air þis dagis afarsabbate atiddjedun du þamma hlaiwa at urrinnandin sunnin.
Mark 16 3 [CA] jah qeþun du sis misso: hvas afwalwjai unsis þana stain af daurom þis hlaiwis?
Mark 16 4 [CA] jah insaihvandeins gaumidedun þammei afwalwiþs ist sa stains; was auk mikils abraba.
Mark 16 5 [CA] jah atgaggandeins in þata hlaiw gasehvun juggalauþ sitandan in taihswai biwaibidana wastjai hveitai; jah usgeisnodedun.
Mark 16 6 [CA] þaruh qaþ du im: ni faurhteiþ izwis, Iesu sokeiþ Nazoraiu þana ushramidan; nist her, urrais, sai þana staþ þarei galagidedun ina.
Mark 16 7 [CA] akei gaggiþ qiþiduh du siponjam is jah du Paitrau þatei faurbigaggiþ izwis in Galeilaian; þaruh ina gasaihviþ, swaswe qaþ izwis.
Mark 16 8 [CA] jah usgaggandeins af þamma hlaiwa gaþlauhun; dizuh~þan~sat ijos reiro jah usfilmei, jah ni qeþun mannhun waiht; ohtedun sis auk.
Mark 16 9 [CA] usstandands þan in maurgin frumin sabbato ataugida <sik> frumist Marjin þizai Magdalene, af þizaiei uswarp sibun unhulþons.
Mark 16 10 [CA] soh gaggandei gataih þaim miþ imma wisandam, qainondam jah gretandam.
Mark 16 11 [CA] jah eis hausjandans þatei libaiþ jah gasaihvans warþ fram izai, ni galaubidedun.
Mark 16 12 [Speyer] . . . . twaim ize ataugiþs warþ in anþaramma farwa, gaggandam du wehsa:
Mark 16 13 [Speyer] jah jainai galeiþandans gataihun þaim anþaraim; niþ~þaim galaubidedun.
Mark 16 14 [Speyer] bi spedistin þan anakumbjandam þaim ainlibim ataugida, jah idweitida ungalaubein ize jah harduhairtein, unte þaim gasaihvandam ina urrisanana, ni galaubidedun.
Mark 16 15 [Speyer] jah qaþ du im: gaggandans in þo manaseþ alakjo, merjaiþ þo aiwaggeljon allai þizai gaskaftai.
Mark 16 16 [Speyer] jah sa galaubjands ufdaupiþs ganisiþ; iþ saei ni galaubeiþ, afdomjada.
Mark 16 17 [Speyer] aþþan taikns þaim galaubjandam þata afargaggiþ: in namin meinamma unhulþons uswairpand: razdom rodjand niujaim,
Mark 16 18 [Speyer] waurmans nimand, jah jabai ingibe hva drigkaina, ni þauh im agljai; ana unhailans handuns uslagjand, jah waila wairþiþ im.
Mark 16 19 [Speyer] þanuh þan frauja Iesus afar þatei rodida du im, usnumans warþ in himin jah gasat af taihswon gudis.
Mark 16 20 [Speyer] Aiwaggeljo þairh Marku ustauh. wulþus þus weiha guþ. amen.
Luke 1 1 [CA] Unte raihtis managai dugunnun meljan insaht bi þos gafullaweisidons in uns waihtins,
Luke 1 2 [CA] swaswe anafulhun unsis þaiei fram frumistin silbasiunjos jah andbahtos wesun þis waurdis;
Luke 1 3 [CA] galeikaida jah mis [jah ahmin weihamma] fram anastodeinai allaim glaggwuba afarlaistjandin gahahjo þus meljan, batista Þaiaufeilu,
Luke 1 4 [CA] ei gakunnais þize bi þoei galaisiþs is waurde [a]staþ.
Luke 1 5 [CA] was in dagam Herodes þiudanis Iudaias gudja namin Zakarias, us afar<am> Abijins, jah qeins is us dauhtrum Aharons, jah namo izos Aileisabaiþ.
Luke 1 6 [CA] wesunuh þan garaihta ba in andwairþja gudis, gaggandona in allaim anabusnim jah garaihteim fraujins unwaha.
Luke 1 7 [CA] jah ni was im barne, unte was Aileisabaiþ stairo, jah ba framaldra dage seinaize wesun.
Luke 1 8 [CA] warþ þan, miþþanei gudjinoda is in wikon kunjis seinis in andwairþja gudis,
Luke 1 9 [CA] bi biuhtja gudjinassaus hlauts imma urrann du saljan, atgaggands in alh fraujins,
Luke 1 10 [CA] jah alls hiuhma was manageins beidandans uta hveilai þwmiamins.
Luke 1 11 [CA] warþ þan imma in siunai aggilus fraujins standands af taihswon hunslastadis þwmiamins.
Luke 1 12 [CA] jah gadrobnoda Zakarias gasaihvands, jah agis disdraus ina.
Luke 1 13 [CA] qaþ þan du imma sa aggilus: ni ogs þus, Zakaria, duþe ei andhausida ist bida þeina, jah qens þeina Aileisabaiþ gabairid sunu þus, jah haitais namo is Iohannen.
Luke 1 14 [CA] jah wairþiþ þus faheds jah swegniþa, jah managai in gabaurþai is faginond.
Luke 1 15 [CA] wairþiþ auk mikils in andwairþja fraujins jah wein jah leiþu ni drigkid jah ahmins weihis gafulljada nauhþan in wambai aiþeins seinaizos,
Luke 1 16 [CA] jah managans suniwe Israelis gawandeiþ du fraujin guda ize.
Luke 1 17 [CA] jah silba fauraqimid in andwairþja is in ahmin jah mahtai Haileiins gawandjan hairtona attane du barnam jah untalans in frodein garaihtaize, manwjan fraujin managein gafahrida.
Luke 1 18 [CA] jah qaþ Zakarias du þamma aggilau: bihve kunnum þata? ik raihtis im sineigs, jah qens meina framaldrozei in dagam seinaim.
Luke 1 19 [CA] jah andhafjands sa aggilus qaþ du imma: ik im Gabriel sa standands in andwairþja gudis, jah insandiþs im rodjan du þus jah wailamerjan þus þata.
Luke 1 20 [CA] jah <sai> sijais þahands jah ni magands rodjan und þana dag ei wairþai þata, duþe ei ni galaubides waurdam meinaim, þoei usfulljanda in mela seinamma.
Luke 1 21 [CA] jah was managei beidandans Zakariins, jah sildaleikidedun hva latidedi ina in þizai alh.
Luke 1 22 [CA] usgaggands þan ni mahta du im rodjan, jah froþun þammei siun gasahv in alh; jah silba was bandwjands im jah <ga>was dumbs.
Luke 1 23 [CA] jah warþ, biþe usfullnodedun dagos andbahteis is, galaiþ du garda seinamma.
Luke 1 24 [CA] afaruh þan þans dagans inkilþo warþ Aileisabaiþ qens is jah galaugnida sik menoþs fimf, qiþandei:
Luke 1 25 [CA] þatei swa mis gatawida frauja in dagam þaimei insahv afniman idweit mein in mannam.
Luke 1 26 [CA] þanuh þan in menoþ saihstin insandiþs was aggilus Gabriel fram guda in baurg Galeilaias sei haitada Nazaraiþ,
Luke 1 27 [CA] du magaþai in fragibtim abin, þizei namo Iosef, us garda Daweidis, jah namo þizos magaþais Mariam.
Luke 1 28 [CA] jah galeiþands inn sa aggilus du izai qaþ: fagino, anstai audahafta, frauja miþ þus; þiuþido þu in qinom.
Luke 1 29 [CA] iþ si gasaihvandei gaþlahsnoda bi innatgahtai is jah þahta sis hveleika wesi so goleins [þatei swa þiuþida izai].
Luke 1 30 [CA] jah qaþ aggilus du izai: ni ogs þus, Mariam, bigast auk anst fram guda.

Luke 1 36 [CA] jah sai, Aileisabaiþ niþjo þeina, jah so inkilþo sunau in aldomin seinamma, jah sa menoþs saihsta ist izai sei haitada stairo,

Luke 2 41 [CA] jah wratodedun þai birusjos is jera hvammeh in Iairusalem at dulþ paska.

Luke 2 43 [CA] jah ustiuhandam þans dagans, miþþane gawandidedun sik aftra, gastoþ Iesus sa magus in Iairusalem, jah ni wissedun Iosef jah aiþei is.
Luke 2 44 [CA] hugjandona in gasinþjam ina wisan qemun dagis wig jah sokidedun ina in ganiþjam jah in kunþam.
Luke 2 45 [CA] jah ni bigitandona ina gawandidedun sik in Iairusalem sokjandona ina.
Luke 2 46 [CA] jah warþ afar dagans þrins, bigetun ina in alh sitandan in midjaim laisarjam jah hausjandan im jah fraihnandan ins.
Luke 2 47 [CA] usgeisnodedun þan allai þai hausjandans is ana frodein jah andawaurdjam is.
Luke 2 48 [CA] jah gasaihvandans ina sildaleikidedun, jah qaþ du imma so aiþei is: magau, hva gatawides uns swa? sai, sa atta þeins jah ik winnandona sokidedum þuk.
Luke 2 49 [CA] jah qaþ du im: hva þatei sokideduþ mik? niu wisseduþ þatei in þaim attins meinis skulda wisan?
Luke 2 50 [CA] jah ija ni froþun þamma waurda þatei rodida du im.

Luke 3 1 [CA] In jera þan fimftataihundin þiudinassaus Teibairiaus kaisaris, raginondin Puntiau Peilatau Iudaia, jah fidurraginja þis Galeilaias Herodeis, Filippauzuh þan broþrs is fidurraginja þis Ituraias jah Trakauneitidaus landis, jah Lwsaniaus Abeilenes fidurraginja,
Luke 3 2 [CA] at auhmistam gudjam Annin jah Kajafin, warþ waurd gudis at Iohannen, Zaxariins sunau, in auþidai.
Luke 3 3 [CA] jah qam and allans gaujans Iaurdanaus merjands daupein idreigos du fraleta frawaurhte,
Luke 3 4 [CA] swaswe gamelid ist in bokom waurde Esaeiins praufetaus qiþandins: stibna wopjandins in auþidai, manweid wig fraujins, raihtos waurkeiþ staigos is;
Luke 3 5 [CA] all dalei usfulljada jah all fairgunje jah hlaine gahnaiwjada, jah wairþiþ þata wraiqo du raihtamma jah usdrusteis du wigam slaihtaim.
Luke 3 6 [CA] jah gasaihviþ all leike nasein gudis.

Luke 3 8 [CA] waurkjaiþ nu akran wairþata idreigos jah ni duginnaiþ qiþan in izwis: attan aigum Abraham; qiþa auk izwis þatei mag guþ us stainam þaim urraisjan barna Abrahama.
Luke 3 9 [CA] aþþan ju so aqizi at waurtim bagme ligiþ: all nu bagme unbairandane akran god usmaitada jah in fon galagjada.
Luke 3 10 [CA] jah frehun ina manageins qiþandans: an hva taujaima?

Luke 3 12 [CA] qemun þan <jah> motarjos daupjan jah qeþun du imma: laisari, hva taujaima?
Luke 3 13 [CA] þaruh qaþ du im: ni waiht ufar þatei garaid sijai izwis, lausjaiþ.
Luke 3 14 [CA] frehun þan ina jah þai militondans qiþandans: jah weis hva taujaima? jah qaþ du im: ni mannanhun holoþ, ni mannanhun anamahtjaid jah waldaiþ annom izwaraim.
Luke 3 15 [CA] at wenjandein þan allai managein jah þagkjandam allaim in hairtam seinaim bi Iohannein, niu aufto sa wesi Xristus,

Luke 3 17 [CA] habands winþiskauron in handau seinai jah gahraineiþ gaþrask sein jah briggiþ kaurn in bansta seinamma, iþ ahana intandeiþ funin unhvapnandin.
Luke 3 18 [CA] managuþ~þan jah anþar þrafstjands þiuþspilloda managein.

Luke 3 20 [CA] anaaiauk jah þata ana alla jah galauk Iohannen in karkarai.

Luke 4 1 [CA] Iþ Iesus, ahmins weihis fulls, gawandida sik fram Iaurdanau jah tauhans was in ahmin in auþidai
Luke 4 2 [CA] dage fidwor tiguns, fraisans fram diabulau. jah ni matida waiht in dagam jainaim, jah at ustauhanaim þaim dagam, biþe gredags warþ.
Luke 4 3 [CA] jah qaþ du imma diabulus: jabai sunaus sijais gudis, qiþ þamma staina ei wairþai hlaibs.
Luke 4 4 [CA] jah andhof Iesus wiþra ina qiþands: gamelid ist þatei ni bi hlaib ainana libaid manna, ak bi all waurde gudis.
Luke 4 5 [CA] jah ustiuhands ina diabulaus ana fairguni hauhata, ataugida imma allans þiudinassuns þis midjungardis in stika melis.
Luke 4 6 [CA] jah qaþ du imma sa diabulus: þus giba þata waldufni þize allata jah wulþu ize, unte mis atgiban ist, jah þishvammeh þei wiljau, giba þata.
Luke 4 7 [CA] þu nu jabai inweitis mik in andwairþja meinamma, wairþiþ þein all.
Luke 4 8 [CA] jah andhafjands imma Iesus qaþ: gamelid ist, fraujan guþ þeinana inweitais jah imma ainamma fullafahjais.
Luke 4 9 [CA] þaþroh gatauh ina in Iairusalem jah gasatida ina ana giblin alhs jah qaþ du imma: jabai sunus sijais gudis, wairp þuk þaþro dalaþ;
Luke 4 10 [CA] gamelid ist auk þatei aggilum seinaim anabiudiþ bi þuk du gafastan þuk,
Luke 4 11 [CA] jah þatei ana handum þuk ufhaband, ei hvan ni gastagqjais bi staina fotu þeinana.
Luke 4 12 [CA] jah andhafjands qaþ imma Iesus þatei qiþan ist: ni fraisais fraujan guþ þeinana.
Luke 4 13 [CA] jah ustiuhands all fraistobnjo diabulus, afstoþ fairra imma und mel.
Luke 4 14 [CA] jah gawandida sik Iesus in mahtai ahmins in Galeilaian, jah meriþa urrann and all gawi bisitande bi ina.
Luke 4 15 [CA] jah is laisida in gaqumþim ize, mikilids fram allaim.
Luke 4 16 [CA] jah qam in Nazaraiþ, þarei was fodiþs, jah galaiþ inn bi biuhtja seinamma in daga sabbato in swnagogein jah usstoþ siggwan bokos.
Luke 4 17 [CA] jah atgibanos wesun imma bokos Eisaeiins praufetus, jah uslukands þos bokos bigat stad, þarei was gamelid:
Luke 4 18 [CA] ahma fraujins ana mis, in þizei gasalboda mik du wailamerjan unledaim, insandida mik du ganasjan þans gamalwidans hairtin,
Luke 4 19 [CA] merjan frahunþanaim fralet jah blindaim siun, fraletan gamaidans in gaþrafstein, merjan jer fraujins andanem.
Luke 4 20 [CA] jah faifalþ þos bokos jah usgibands andbahta gasat. jah allaim in þizai swnagogein wesun augona fairweitjandona du imma.
Luke 4 21 [CA] dugann þan rodjan du im þatei himma daga usfullnodedun mela þo in ausam izwaraim.
Luke 4 22 [CA] jah allai alakjo weitwodidedun imma jah sildaleikidedun bi þo waurda anstais þo usgaggandona us munþa is jah qeþun: niu sa ist sunus Iosefis?
Luke 4 23 [CA] jah qaþ du im: aufto qiþiþ mis þo gajukon: þu leiki, hailei þuk silban; hvan filu hausidedum waurþan in Kafarnaum, tawei jah her in gabaurþai þeinai.
Luke 4 24 [CA] qaþ þan: amen izwis qiþa, þatei ni ainshun praufete andanems ist in gabaurþai seinai:
Luke 4 25 [CA] aþþan bi sunjai qiþa izwis þatei managos widuwons wesun in dagam Heleiins in Israela, þan galuknoda himins du jeram þrim jah menoþs saihs, swe warþ huhrus mikils and alla airþa:
Luke 4 26 [CA] jah ni du ainaihun þizo insandiþs was Helias, alja in Saraipta Seidonais du qinon widuwon.
Luke 4 27 [CA] jah managai þrutsfillai wesun uf Haileisaiu praufetau in Israela, jah ni ainshun ize gahrainids was, alja Naiman sa Saur.
Luke 4 28 [CA] jah fullai waurþun allai modis in þizai swnagogein hausjandans þata.
Luke 4 29 [CA] jah usstandans uskusun imma ut us baurg jah brahtedun ina und auhmisto þis fairgunjis ana þammei so baurgs ize gatimrida was, du afdrausjan ina þaþro.
Luke 4 30 [CA] iþ is þairhleiþands þairh midjans ins iddja.
Luke 4 31 [CA] jah galaiþ in Kafarnaum, baurg Galeilaias jah was laisjands ins in sabbatim.
Luke 4 32 [CA] jah sildaleikidedun bi þo laisein is, unte in waldufnja was waurd is.
Luke 4 33 [CA] jah in þizai swnagogein was manna habands ahman unhulþons unhrainjana jah ufhropida,
Luke 4 34 [CA] qiþands: let! hva uns jah þus, Iesu Nazorenu? qamt fraqistjan unsis? kann þuk, hvas is, sa weiha gudis.
Luke 4 35 [CA] jah gahvotida imma Iesus qiþands: afdobn jah usgagg us þamma. jah gawairpands ina sa unhulþa in midjaim urrann af imma, ni waihtai gaskaþjands imma.
Luke 4 36 [CA] jah warþ afslauþnan <ana> allans, jah rodidedun du sis misso qiþandans: hva waurde þata, þatei miþ waldufnja jah mahtai anabiudiþ þaim unhrainjam ahmam jah usgaggand?
Luke 4 37 [CA] jah usiddja meriþa fram imma and allans stadins þis bisunjane landis.
Luke 4 38 [CA] usstandands þan us þizai swnagogai galaiþ in gard Seimonis. swaihro þan þis Seimonis was anahabaida brinnon mikilai, jah bedun ina bi þo.
Luke 4 39 [CA] jah atstandands ufar ija gasok þizai brinnon, jah aflailot ija. sunsaiw þan usstandandei andbahtida im.
Luke 4 40 [CA] miþþanei þan sagq sunno, allai swa managai swe habaidedun siukans sauhtim missaleikaim, brahtedun ins at imma: iþ is ainhvarjammeh ize handuns analagjands gahailida ins.
Luke 4 41 [CA] usiddjedun þan jah unhulþons af managaim hropjandeins jah qiþandeins þatei þu is Xristus, sunus gudis. jah gasakands im ni lailot þos rodjan, unte wissedun [silban] Xristu ina wisan.
Luke 4 42 [CA] biþeh þan warþ dags, usgaggands galaiþ ana auþjana stad, jah manageins sokidedun ina jah qemun und ina jah gahabaidedun ina, ei ni afliþi fairra im.
Luke 4 43 [CA] þaruh is qaþ du im þatei jah þaim anþaraim baurgim wailamerjan ik skal bi þiudangardja gudis, unte duþe mik insandida.
Luke 4 44 [CA] jah was merjands in swnagogim Galeilaias.
Luke 5 1 [CA] Jah warþ, miþþanei managei anatramp ina du hausjan waurd gudis, jah is silba was standands nehva saiwa Gainnesaraiþ,
Luke 5 2 [CA] jah gasahv twa skipa standandona at þamma saiwa, iþ fiskjans afgaggandans af im usþwohun natja.
Luke 5 3 [CA] galaiþ þan in ain þize skipe, þatei was Seimonis; haihait ina aftiuhan fairra staþa leitil jah gasitands laisida us þamma skipa manageins.
Luke 5 4 [CA] biþeh þan gaandida rodjands, qaþ du Seimonau: brigg ana diupiþa, jah athahid þo natja izwara du fiskon.
Luke 5 5 [CA] jah andhafjands Seimon qaþ du imma: talzjand, alla naht þairharbaidjandans waiht ni nemum; iþ afar waurda þeinamma wairpam natja.
Luke 5 6 [CA] jah þata taujandans galukun manageins fiske filu, swe natja dishnupnodedun ize.
Luke 5 7 [CA] jah bandwidedun gamanam þoei wesun in anþaramma skipa, ei atiddjedeina hilpan ize. jah qemun jah gafullidedun ba þo skipa, swe sugqun.
Luke 5 8 [CA] gaumjands þan Seimon Paitrus draus du kniwam Iesuis qiþands: [bidja þuk] usgagg fairra mis, unte manna frawaurhts im, frauja.
Luke 5 9 [CA] sildaleik auk dishabaida ina jah allans þans miþ imma in gafahis þize fiske þanzei ganutun;
Luke 5 10 [CA] samaleikoh þan jah Iakobau jah Iohannen, sununs Zaibaidaiaus, þaiei wesun gadailans Seimona. jah qaþ du Seimona Iesus: ni ogs þus, fram himma nu manne sind nutans.
Luke 5 11 [CA] jah gatiuhandans þo skipa ana airþa afleitandans allata laistidedun afar imma.
Luke 5 12 [CA] jah warþ, miþþanei was is in ainai baurge, jah sai, manna fulls þrutsfillis jah gasaihvands Iesu driusands ana andwairþi bad ina qiþands: frauja, jabai wileis, magt mik gahrainjan.
Luke 5 13 [CA] jah ufrakjands handu attaitok imma qiþands: wiljau, wairþ hrains. jah suns þata þrutsfill aflaiþ af imma.
Luke 5 14 [CA] jah is faurbaud imma ei mann ni qeþi; ak gagg jah ataugei þuk silban gudjin jah atbair imma fram þizai gahraineinai þeinai þatei anabaud Moses du weitwodiþai im.
Luke 5 15 [CA] usmernoda þan þata waurd mais bi ina, jah garunnun hiuhmans managai hausjon jah leikinon fram imma sauhte seinaizo.
Luke 5 16 [CA] iþ is was afleiþands ana auþidos jah bidjands.
Luke 5 17 [CA] jah warþ in ainamma dage, jah is was laisjands. jah wesun sitandans Fareisaieis jah witodalaisarjos, þaiei wesun gaqumanai us allamma haimo Galeilaias jah Iudaias jah Iairusaulwmon; jah mahts fraujins was du hailjan ins.
Luke 5 18 [CA] jah sai mans bairandans ana ligra mannan saei was usliþa, jah sokidedun hvaiwa ina innatbereina jah galagidideina in andwairþja is.
Luke 5 19 [CA] jah ni bigitandans hvaiwa innatbereina ina in manageins, ussteigandans ana hrot and skaljos, gasatidedun ina miþ þamma badja in midjaim faura Iesua.
Luke 5 20 [CA] jah gasaihvands galaubein ize qaþ du þamma usliþin: manna, afleitanda þus frawaurhteis þeinos.
Luke 5 21 [CA] jah dugunnun þagkjan þai bokarjos jah Fareisaieis qiþandans: hvas ist sa, saei rodeiþ naiteinins? hvas mag afletan frawaurhtins, alja ains guþ?
Luke 5 22 [CA] ufkunnands þan Iesus mitonins ize andhafjands qaþ du im: hva biþagkeiþ in hairtam izwaraim?
Luke 5 23 [CA] hvaþar ist azetizo qiþan: afletanda þus frawaurhteis, þau qiþan: urreis jah gagg?
Luke 5 24 [CA] aþþan ei witeid þatei waldufni habaid sa sunus mans ana airþai afletan frawaurhtins, qaþ du þamma usliþin: du þus qiþa, urreis jah ushafjands þata badi þeinata gagg in gard þeinana.
Luke 5 25 [CA] jah sunsaiw usstandands in andwairþja ize, ushafjands ana þammei lag, galaiþ in gard seinana mikiljands guþ.
Luke 5 26 [CA] jah usfilmei dissat allans, jah mikilidedun guþ jah fullai waurþun agisis qiþandans þatei gasaihvam wulþaga himma daga.
Luke 5 27 [CA] jah afar þata usiddja jah gasahv motari, namin Laiwwi, sitandan ana motastada, jah qaþ du imma: laistei afar mis.
Luke 5 28 [CA] jah bileiþands allaim, usstandands iddja afar imma.
Luke 5 29 [CA] jah gawaurhta dauht mikila Laiwweis imma in garda seinamma, jah was managei motarje mikila jah anþaraize, þaiei wesun miþ im anakumbjandans.
Luke 5 30 [CA] jah birodidedun bokarjos ize jah Fareisaieis du siponjam is qiþandans: duhve miþ þaim motarjam jah frawaurhtaim matjid jah drigkid?
Luke 5 31 [CA] jah andhafjands Iesus qaþ du im: ni þaurbun hailai leikeis, ak þai unhailans.
Luke 5 32 [CA] ni qam laþon garaihtans, ak frawaurhtans in idreiga.
Luke 5 33 [CA] iþ eis qeþun du imma: duhve siponjos Iohannes fastand ufta jah bidos taujand, samaleiko jah Fareisaiei, iþ þai þeinai siponjos matjand jah drigkand?
Luke 5 34 [CA] þaruh is qaþ du im: ni magud sununs bruþfadis, unte sa bruþfads miþ im ist, gataujan fastan.
Luke 5 35 [CA] aþþan qimand dagos, jah þan afnimada af im sa bruþfads, jah þan fastand in jainaim dagam.
Luke 5 36 [CA] qaþuh þan jah gajukon du im, þatei ainshun plat snagins niujis ni lagjid ana snagan fairnjana, aiþþau jah sa niuja aftaurnid, jah þamma fairnjin ni gatimid þata af þamma niujin.
Luke 5 37 [CA] jah ainshun ni giutid wein niujata in balgins fairnjans, aiþþau distairid þata niujo wein þans balgins jah silbo usgutniþ, jah þai balgeis fraqistnand;
Luke 5 38 [CA] ak wein juggata in balgins niujans giutand, jah bajoþs gafastanda.
Luke 5 39 [CA] jah ainshun drigkandane fairni, ni suns wili jugg; qiþiþ auk: þata fairnjo batizo ist.
Luke 6 1 [CA] Jah warþ in sabbato anþaramma frumin gaggan imma þairh atisk, jah raupidedun ahsa siponjos is jah matidedun bnauandans handum.
Luke 6 2 [CA] iþ sumai Fareisaie qeþun du im: hva taujid þatei ni skuld ist taujan in sabbato dagam?
Luke 6 3 [CA] jah andhafjands wiþra ins Iesus qaþ: ni þata ussuggwud þatei gatawida Daweid, þan gredags was, silba jah þaiei miþ imma wesun?
Luke 6 4 [CA] hvaiwa inngalaiþ in gard gudis jah hlaibans faurlageinais usnam jah matida jah gaf þaim miþ sis wisandam, þanzei ni skuld ist matjan, nibai ainaim gudjam?
Luke 6 5 [CA] jah qaþ du im þatei frauja ist sa sunus mans jah þamma sabbato daga.
Luke 6 6 [CA] jah warþ þan in anþaramma daga sabbato galeiþan imma in swnagogein jah laisjan. jah was jainar manna, jah handus is so taihswo was þaursus.
Luke 6 7 [CA] witaidedunuh þan þai bokarjos jah Fareisaieis, jau in sabbato daga leikinodedi, ei bigeteina til du wrohjan ina.
Luke 6 8 [CA] iþ is wissuh mitonins ize jah qaþ du þamma mann, þamma þaursja habandin handu: urreis jah stand in midjaim. þaruh is urreisands gastoþ.
Luke 6 9 [CA] qaþ þan Iesus du im: fraihna izwis hva skuld ist sabbato dagam, þiuþ taujan þau unþiuþ taujan, saiwala ganasjan þau usqistjan?

Luke 6 37 [CA] jah ni stojid, ei ni stojaindau; ni afdomjaid, jah ni afdomjanda; fraletaid, jah fraletanda.

Luke 6 42 [CA] aiþþau hvaiwa magt qiþan du broþr þeinamma: broþar let, ik uswairpa gramsta þamma in augin þeinamma, silba in augin þeinamma anza ni gaumjands? liuta, uswairp faurþis þamma anza us augin þeinamma, jah þan gaumjais uswairpan gramsta þamma in augin broþrs þeinis.

Luke 6 45 [CA] þiuþeigs manna us þiuþeigamma huzda hairtins seinis usbairid þiuþ, jah ubils manna us ubilamma hairtins seinis usbairid ubil: uzuh allis ufarfullein hairtins rodeid munþs is.

Luke 6 48 [CA] galeiks ist mann timrjandin razn, saei grob jah gadiupida jah gasatida grunduwaddjau ana staina. at garunjon þan waurþanai bistagq ahva bi jainamma razna jah ni mahta gawagjan ita; gasulid auk was ana þamma staina.

Luke 8 37 [CA] jah bedun ina allai gaujans þize Gaddarene galeiþan fairra sis, unte agisa mikilamma dishabaidai wesun. iþ is galeiþands in skip gawandida sik.
Luke 8 38 [CA] baþ þan ina sa wair af þammei þos unhulþons usiddjedun, ei wesi miþ imma; fralailot þan ina Iesus qiþands:
Luke 8 39 [CA] gawandei þuk du garda þeinamma jah usspillo hvan filu gatawida þus guþ. jah galaiþ and baurg alla merjands hvan filu gatawida imma Iesus.
Luke 8 40 [CA] warþ þan, miþþanei gawandida sik Iesus, andnam ina managei; wesun auk allai beidandans is.
Luke 8 41 [CA] jah sai, qam wair þizei namo Iaeirus, sah fauramaþleis swnagogais was, jah driusands faura fotum Iesuis bad ina gaggan in gard seinana;
Luke 8 42 [CA] unte dauhtar ainoho was imma swe wintriwe twalibe, jah so swalt. miþþanei þan iddja is, manageins þraihun ina.
Luke 8 43 [CA] jah qino wisandei in runa bloþis jera twalif, soei in lekjans fraqam allamma aigina seinamma, jah ni mahta was fram ainomehun galeikinon,
Luke 8 44 [CA] atgaggandei du aftaro attaitok skauta wastjos is, jah suns gastoþ sa runs bloþis izos.
Luke 8 45 [CA] jah qaþ Iesus: hvas sa tekands mis? laugnjandam þan allaim qaþ Paitrus jah þai miþ imma: talzjand, manageins bihvairband þuk jah þreihand, jah qiþis: hvas sa tekands mis?
Luke 8 46 [CA] þaruh is qaþ: taitok mis sums; ik auk ufkunþa maht usgaggandein af mis.
Luke 8 47 [CA] gasaihvandei þan so qino þatei ni galaugnida, reirandei <qam> jah atdriusandei du imma, in þizei attaitok imma, gataih imma in andwairþja allaizos manageins jah hvaiwa gahailnoda suns.
Luke 8 48 [CA] iþ Iesus qaþ du izai: þrafstei þuk, dauhtar: galaubeins þeina ganasida þuk; gagg in gawairþja.
Luke 8 49 [CA] nauhþan imma rodjandin gaggiþ sums manne fram þis fauramaþleis swnagogais, qiþands du imma þatei gadauþnoda dauhtar þeina; ni draibei þana laisari.
Luke 8 50 [CA] iþ is gahausjands andhof imma qiþands: ni faurhtei; þatainei galaubei, jah ganasjada.
Luke 8 51 [CA] qimands þan in garda ni fralailot ainohun inngaggan, alja Paitru jah Iakobu jah Iohannen jah þana attan þizos maujos jah aiþein.
Luke 8 52 [CA] gaigrotun þan allai jah faiflokun þo. þaruh qaþ: ni gretiþ, unte ni gaswalt, ak slepiþ.
Luke 8 53 [CA] jah bihlohun ina gasaihvandans þatei gaswalt.
Luke 8 54 [CA] þanuh is usdreibands allans ut jah fairgreipands handu izos wopida qiþands: mawi, urreis!
Luke 8 55 [CA] jah gawandida ahman izos, jah ustoþ suns. jah anabaud izai giban mat.
Luke 8 56 [CA] jah usgeisnodedun fadrein izos; iþ is faurbaud im ei mann ni qiþeina þata waurþano.
Luke 9 1 [CA] Gahaitands þan þans twalif apaustauluns atgaf im maht jah waldufni ufar allaim unhulþom jah sauhtins gahailjan.
Luke 9 2 [CA] jah insandida ins merjan þiudangardja gudis jah gahailjan allans þans unhailans.
Luke 9 3 [CA] jah qaþ du im: ni waiht nimaiþ in wig; nih waluns nih matibalg nih hlaib nih skattans, nih þan tweihnos paidos haban.
Luke 9 4 [CA] jah in þanei gard gaggaiþ, þar saljiþ jah þaþroh usgaggaiþ.
Luke 9 5 [CA] jah swa managai swe ni andnimaina izwis, usgaggandans us þizai baurg jainai jah mulda af fotum izwaraim afhrisjaiþ du weitwodiþai ana ins.
Luke 9 6 [CA] usgaggandans þan þairhiddjedun and haimos wailamerjandans jah leikinondans and all.
Luke 9 7 [CA] gahausida þan Herodis sa taitrarkes þo waurþanona fram imma alla jah þahta, unte qeþun sumai þatei Iohannes urrais us dauþaim.
Luke 9 8 [CA] sumai þan qeþun <þatei> Helias ataugida sik; sumaiuþ~þan þatei praufetus sums þize airizane usstoþ.
Luke 9 9 [CA] jah qaþ Herodes: Iohannau ik haubiþ afmaimait, iþ hvas ist sa, bi þanei ik hausja swaleik? jah sokida ina gasaihvan.
Luke 9 10 [CA] jah gawandjandans sik apaustauleis usspillodedun imma, swa filu swe gatawidedun. jah andnimands ins afiddja sundro ana staþ auþjana baurgs namnidaizos Baidsaiïdan.
Luke 9 11 [CA] iþ þos manageins finþandeins laistidedun afar imma, jah andnimands ins rodida du im þo bi þiudangardja gudis jah þans þarbans leikinassaus gahailida.
Luke 9 12 [CA] þanuh dags juþan dugann hneiwan. atgaggandans þan du imma þai twalif qeþun du imma: fralet þo managein, ei galeiþandans in þos bisunjane haimos jah weihsa saljaina jah bugjaina sis matins, unte her in auþjamma stada sium.
Luke 9 13 [CA] þanuh qaþ du im: gibiþ im jus matjan. iþ eis qeþun du imma: nist hindar uns maizo fimf hlaibam, jah fiskos twai, niba þau þatei weis gaggandans bugjaima allai þizai manaseidai matins.
Luke 9 14 [CA] wesun auk swe fimf þusundjos waire. qaþ þan du siponjam seinaim: gawaurkeiþ im anakumbjan kubituns, ana hvarjanoh fimf tiguns.
Luke 9 15 [CA] jah gatawidedun swa jah gatawidedun anakumbjan allans.
Luke 9 16 [CA] nimands þan þans fimf hlaibans jah twans fiskans, insaihvands du himina gaþiuþida ins jah gabrak jah gaf siponjam du faurlagjan þizai managein.
Luke 9 17 [CA] jah matidedun jah sadai waurþun allai; jah ushafan warþ, þatei aflifnoda im gabruko, tainjons twalif.
Luke 9 18 [CA] jah warþ, miþþanei was is bidjands sundro, gamotidedun imma siponjos is, jah frah ins qiþands: hvana mik qiþand wisan þos manageins?
Luke 9 19 [CA] iþ eis andhafjandans qeþun: Iohannen þana daupjand, anþarai þan Heleian, sumai þan þatei praufetus sums þize airizane usstoþ.
Luke 9 20 [CA] qaþ þan du im: aþþan jus hvana mik qiþiþ wisan? andhafjands þan Paitrus qaþ: þu is Xristus, sunus gudis.
Luke 9 21 [CA] iþ is þan gahvotjands im faurbauþ ei mann ni qiþeina þata;
Luke 9 22 [CA] qiþands þatei skal sunus mans manag winnan jah uskusans fram sinistam wairþan jah gudjam jah bokarjam jah usqiman jah þridjin daga urreisan.
Luke 9 23 [CA] qaþ þan du allaim: jabai hvas wili afar mis gaggan, afaikai sik silban jah nimai galgan seinana dag hvanoh jah laistjai mik.
Luke 9 24 [CA] saei allis wili saiwala seina nasjan, fraqisteiþ izai; aþþan saei fraqisteiþ saiwalai seinai in meina, ganasjiþ þo.
Luke 9 25 [CA] hvo allis þaurfte gataujiþ sis manna, gageigands þo manased alla, iþ sis silbin fraqistjands aiþþau gasleiþjands?
Luke 9 26 [CA] saei allis skamaiþ sik meina aiþþau meinaize waurde, þizuh sunus mans skamaid sik, biþe qimiþ in wulþu seinamma jah attins jah þize weihane aggele.
Luke 9 27 [CA] qiþuh þan izwis sunja: sind sumai þize her standandane, þaiei ni kausjand dauþau, unte gasaihvand þiudinassau gudis.
Luke 9 28 [CA] waurþun þan afar þo waurda swe dagos ahtau, ganimands Paitru jah Iakobu jah Iohannen usiddja in fairguni bidjan.
Luke 9 29 [CA] jah warþ, miþþanei baþ is, siuns andwairþjis is anþara jah gawaseins is hveita skeinandei.
Luke 9 30 [CA] jah sai, wairos twai miþrodidedun imma, þaiei wesun Moses jah Helias;
Luke 9 31 [CA] þai gasaihvanans in wulþau qeþun urruns is, þoei skulda usfulljan in Iairusalem.
Luke 9 32 [CA] iþ Paitrus jah þai miþ imma wesun kauridai slepa: gawaknandans þan gasehvun wulþu is jah þans twans wairans þans miþstandandans imma.
Luke 9 33 [CA] jah warþ, miþþanei afskaiskaidun sik af imma, qaþ Paitrus du Iesua: talzjand, god ist unsis her wisan, jah gawaurkjaima hleiþros þrins, aina þus jah aina Mose jah aina Helijin, ni witands hva qiþiþ.
Luke 9 34 [CA] þata þan imma qiþandin warþ milhma jah ufarskadwida ins; faurhtidedun þan in þammei jainai qemun in þamma milhmin.
Luke 9 35 [CA] jah stibna warþ us þamma milhmin qiþandei: sa ist sunus meins sa liuba, þamma hausjaiþ.
Luke 9 36 [CA] jah miþþanei warþ so stibna, bigitans warþ Iesus ains. jah eis þahaidedun jah mann ni gataihun in jainaim dagam ni waiht þizei gasehvun.
Luke 9 37 [CA] warþ þan in þamma <afar>daga, dalaþ atgaggandam im af fairgunja, gamotida imma manageins filu.
Luke 9 38 [CA] jah sai, manna us þizai managein ufwopida qiþands: laisari, bidja þuk insaihvan du sunu meinamma, unte ainaha mis ist.
Luke 9 39 [CA] jah sai, ahma nimiþ ina unhrains jah anaks hropeiþ jah tahjiþ ina miþ hvaþon jah halisaiw aflinniþ af imma gabrikands ina.
Luke 9 40 [CA] jah baþ siponjans þeinans ei usdribeina imma, jah ni mahtedun.
Luke 9 41 [CA] andhafjands þan Iesus qaþ: o kuni ungalaubjando jah inwindo, und hva siau at izwis jah þulau izwis? attiuh þana sunu þeinana hidrei.
Luke 9 42 [CA] þaruh nauhþan duatgaggandin imma, gabrak ina sa unhulþa jah tahida. gahvotida þan Iesus ahmin þamma unhrainjin jah gahailida þana magu jah atgaf ina attin is.
Luke 9 43 [CA] usfilmans þan waurþun allai ana þizai mikilein gudis. at allaim þan sildaleikjandam bi alla þoei gatawida Iesus [qaþ Paitrus: frauja, duhve weis ni mahtedum usdreiban þamma? iþ Iesus qaþ: þata kuni ni usgaggiþ, nibai in bidom jah in fastubnja.] qaþ þan du siponjam seinaim:
Luke 9 44 [CA] lagjiþ jus in ausona izwara þo waurda, unte sunus mans skulds ist atgiban in handuns manne.
Luke 9 45 [CA] iþ eis ni froþun þamma waurda, jah was gahuliþ faura im, ei ni froþeina imma; jah ohtedun fraihnan ina bi þata waurd.
Luke 9 46 [CA] galaiþ þan mitons in ins, þata hvarjis þau ize maists wesi.
Luke 9 47 [CA] iþ Iesus gasaihvands þo miton hairtins ize, fairgreipands barn gasatida faura sis
Luke 9 48 [CA] jah qaþ du im: sahvazuh saei andnimiþ þata barn ana namin meinamma, mik andnimiþ; jah sahvazuh saei mik andnimiþ, andnimiþ þana sandjandan mik; unte sa minnista wisands in allaim izwis, sa wairþiþ mikils.
Luke 9 49 [CA] andhafjands þan Iohannes qaþ: talzjand, gasehvum sumana ana þeinamma namin usdreibandan unhulþons jah waridedun imma, unte ni laisteiþ miþ unsis.
Luke 9 50 [CA] jah qaþ du im Iesus: ni warjiþ, unte saei nist wiþra izwis, faur izwis ist. [ni ainshun auk ist manne, saei ni gawaurkjai maht in namin meinamma.]
Luke 9 51 [CA] warþ þan in þammei usfulnodedun dagos andanumtais is, jah is andwairþi seinata gatulgida du gaggan in Iairusalem.
Luke 9 52 [CA] jah insandida airuns faura sis, jah gaggandans galiþun in haim Samareite, swe manwjan imma.
Luke 9 53 [CA] jah ni andnemun ina, unte andwairþi is was gaggando du Iairusalem.
Luke 9 54 [CA] gasaihvandans þan siponjos is Iakobus jah Iohannes qeþun: frauja, wileizu ei qiþaima, fon atgaggai us himina jah fraqimai im, swe jah Heleias gatawida?
Luke 9 55 [CA] gawandjands þan gasok im jah qaþ du im: niu wituþ hvis ahmane sijuþ?
Luke 9 56 [CA] unte sunus mans ni qam saiwalom qistjan, ak nasjan. jah iddjedun in anþara haim.
Luke 9 57 [CA] warþ þan gaggandam im in wiga qaþ sums du imma: laistja þuk þishvaduh þadei gaggis, frauja.
Luke 9 58 [CA] jah qaþ du imma Iesus: fauhons grobos aigun jah fuglos himinis sitlans; iþ sunus mans ni habaiþ hvar haubiþ galagjai.
Luke 9 59 [CA] qaþ þan du anþaramma: laistei mik; iþ is qaþ: frauja, uslaubei mis galeiþan faurþis jah usfilhan attan meinana.
Luke 9 60 [CA] qaþ þan du imma Iesus: let þans dauþans usfilhan seinans nawins: iþ þu gagg jah gaspillo þiudangardja gudis.
Luke 9 61 [CA] qaþ þan jah anþar: laistja þuk, frauja; iþ faurþis uslaubei mis andqiþan þaim þaiei sind in garda meinamma.
Luke 9 62 [CA] qaþ þan du imma Iesus: ni manna uslagjands handu seina ana hohan jah saihvands aftra, gatils ist in þiudangardja gudis.
Luke 10 1 [CA] Afaruþ~þan þata ustaiknida frauja jah anþarans sibuntehund jah insandida ins twans hvanzuh faura andwairþja seinamma in all baurge jah stade, þadei munaida is gaggan.
Luke 10 2 [CA] qaþuh þan du im: asans managa, iþ waurstwjans fawai; bidjiþ nu fraujan asanais ei ussatjai waurstwjans in þo asan seina.
Luke 10 3 [CA] gaggiþ, sai ik insandja izwis swe lamba in midumai wulfe.
Luke 10 4 [CA] ni bairaiþ pugg nih matibalg nih gaskohi; ni mannanhun bi wig goljaiþ.
Luke 10 5 [CA] in þane gardei inngaggaiþ, frumist qiþaiþ: gawairþi þamma garda.
Luke 10 6 [CA] jah jabai sijai jainar sunus gawairþjis, gahveilaiþ sik ana imma gawairþi izwar; iþ jabai ni, du izwis gawandjai.
Luke 10 7 [CA] inuh þan þamma garda wisaiþ matjandans jah driggkandans þo at im; wairþs auk ist waurstwja mizdons seinaizos. ni faraiþ us garda in gard.
Luke 10 8 [CA] jah in þoei baurge gaggaiþ jah andnimaina izwis, matjaiþ þata faurlagido izwis.
Luke 10 9 [CA] jah lekinoþ þans in izai siukans jah qiþiþ du im: atnehvida ana izwis þiudangardi gudis.
Luke 10 10 [CA] iþ in þoei baurge inngaggaiþ jah ni andnimaina izwis, usgaggandans ana fauradaurja izos qiþaiþ:
Luke 10 11 [CA] jah stubju þana gahaftnandan unsis us þizai baurg izwarai ana fotuns unsarans afhrisjam izwis; sweþauh þata witeiþ þatei atnehvida sik ana izwis þiudangardi gudis.
Luke 10 12 [CA] qiþa izwis þatei Saudaumjam in jainamma daga sutizo wairþiþ þau þizai baurg jainai.
Luke 10 13 [CA] wai þus Kaurazein, wai þus Baiþsaïdan! Unte iþ in Twrai jah Seidonai waurþeina mahteis þozei waurþun in izwis, airis þau in sakkum jah azgon sitandeins gaïdreigodedeina.
Luke 10 14 [CA] sweþauh Twrai jah Seidonai sutizo wairþiþ in daga stauos þau izwis.
Luke 10 15 [CA] jah þu Kafarnaum, þu und himin ushauhido, und halja gadrausjaza.
Luke 10 16 [CA] saei hauseiþ izwis, mis hauseiþ, jah saei ufbrikiþ izwis, mis ufbrikiþ; iþ saei ufbrikiþ mis, ufbrikiþ þamma sandjandin mik.
Luke 10 17 [CA] gawandidedun þan sik þai sibuntehund miþ fahedai qiþandans: frauja, jah unhulþons ufhausjand unsis in namin þeinamma.
Luke 10 18 [CA] qaþ þan du im: gasahv Satanan swe lauhmunja driusandan us himina.
Luke 10 19 [CA] sai, atgaf izwis waldufni trudan ufaro waurme jah skaurpjono jah ana allai mahtai fijandis, jah waihte ainohun izwis ni gaskaþjiþ.
Luke 10 20 [CA] sweþauh þamma ni faginoþ, ei þai ahmans izwis ufhausjand: iþ faginod in þammei namna izwara gamelida sind in himinam.
Luke 10 21 [CA] inuh þizai hveilai swegnida ahmin Iesus jah qaþ: andhaita þus, atta, frauja himinis jah airþos, unte affalht þo faura snutraim jah frodaim jah andhulides þo niuklahaim. Jai, atta, unte swa warþ galeikaiþ in andwairþja þeinamma. jah gawandiþs du siponjam seinaim qaþ:
Luke 10 22 [CA] all mis atgiban ist fram attin meinamma, jah ni hvashun kann hvas ist sunus, alja atta, jah hvas ist atta, alja sunus, jah þammei wili sunus andhuljan.
Luke 10 23 [CA] jah gawandiþs du siponjam seinaim sundro qaþ: audaga augona, þoei saihvand þoei jus saihviþ.
Luke 10 24 [CA] qiþa auk izwis þatei managai praufeteis jah þiudanos wildedun saihvan þatei jus saihviþ jah ni gasehvun, jah hausjan þatei jus [ga]hauseiþ jah ni <ga>hausidedun.
Luke 10 25 [CA] jah sai, witodafasteis sums ustoþ fraisands ina jah qiþands: laisari, hva taujands libainais aiweinons arbja wairþa?
Luke 10 26 [CA] þaruh qaþ du imma: in witoda hva gameliþ ist? hvaiwa ussiggwis?
Luke 10 27 [CA] iþ is andhafjands qaþ: frijos fraujan guþ þeinana us allamma hairtin þeinamma jah us allai saiwalai þeinai jah us allai mahtai þeinai jah us allai gahugdai þeinai, jah nehvundjan þeinana swe þuk silban.
Luke 10 28 [CA] þanuh qaþ du imma: raihtaba andhoft; þata tawei jah libais.
Luke 10 29 [CA] iþ is wiljands uswaurhtana sik domjan qaþ du Iesua: an hvas ist mis nehvundja?
Luke 10 30 [CA] andhafjands þan Iesus qaþ: manna <sums> galaiþ af Iairusalem in Iaireikon jah in waidedjans frarann, þaiei jah biraubodedun ina jah banjos analag(jandans) . . . .

Luke 18 22 [CA] gahausjands þan þata Iesus qaþ du imma: nauh ainis þus wan ist: all þatei habais frabugei jah gadailei unledaim, jah habais huzd in himina, jah hiri laistjan mik.
Luke 18 23 [CA] iþ is gahausjands þata gaurs warþ; was auk gabeigs filu.
Luke 18 24 [CA] gasaihvands þan ina Iesus gaurana waurþanana qaþ: hvaiwa agluba þai faihu habandans inngaleiþand in þiudangardja gudis!
Luke 18 25 [CA] raþizo allis ist ulbandau þairh þairko neþlos þairhleiþan þau gabigamma in þiudangardja gudis galeiþan.
Luke 18 26 [CA] qeþun þan þai gahausjandans: an hvas mag ganisan?
Luke 18 27 [CA] iþ is qaþ: þata unmahteigo at mannam mahteig ist at guda.
Luke 18 28 [CA] qaþ þan Paitrus: sai, weis aflailotum allata jah laistidedum þuk.
Luke 18 29 [CA] iþ is qaþuh du im: amen, qiþa izwis þatei ni ainshun ist þize afletandane gard aiþþau fadrein aiþþau broþruns aiþþau qen aiþþau barna in þiudangardjos gudis,
Luke 18 30 [CA] saei ni andnimai managfalþ in þamma mela jah in aiwa þamma qimandin libain aiweinon.
Luke 18 31 [CA] ganimands þan þans ·ib· qaþ du im: sai, usgaggam in Iairusalem, jah ustiuhada all þata gamelido þairh praufetuns bi sunu mans.
Luke 18 32 [CA] atgibada auk þiudom jah bilaikada jah anamahtjada jah bispeiwada,
Luke 18 33 [CA] jah usbliggwandans usqimand imma, jah þridjin daga usstandiþ.
Luke 18 34 [CA] jah eis ni waihtai þis froþun, jah was þata waurd gafulgin af im, jah ni wissedun þo qiþanona.
Luke 18 35 [CA] warþ þan, miþþanei nehva was is Iaireikon, blinda sums sat faur wig du aihtron.
Luke 18 36 [CA] gahausjands þan managein faurgaggandein frah hva wesi þata.
Luke 18 37 [CA] gataihun þan imma þatei Iesus Nazoraius þairhgaggiþ.
Luke 18 38 [CA] iþ is ubuhwopida qiþands: Iesu, sunu Daweidis, armai mik!
Luke 18 39 [CA] jah þai faur<a>gaggandans andbitun ina ei þahaidedi: iþ is und filu mais hropida: sunau Daweidis, armai mik!
Luke 18 40 [CA] gastandands þan Iesus haihait ina tiuhan du sis. biþe nehva was þan imma, frah ina
Luke 18 41 [CA] qiþands: hva þus wileis ei taujau? iþ is qaþ: frauja, ei ussaihvau.
Luke 18 42 [CA] jah Iesus qaþ du imma: ussaihv, galaubeins þeina ganasida þuk.
Luke 18 43 [CA] jah suns ussahv jah laistida ina awiliudonds guda. jah alla managei gasaihvandei gaf hazein guda.
Luke 19 1 [CA] Jah inngaleiþands þairhlaiþ Iaireikon.
Luke 19 2 [CA] jah sai, guma namin haitans Zakkaius, sah was fauramaþleis motarje jah was gabigs,
Luke 19 3 [CA] jah sokida gasaihvan Iesu, hvas wesi, jah ni mahta faura managein, unte wahstau leitils was.
Luke 19 4 [CA] jah biþragjands faur usstaig ana smakkabagm, ei gasehvi ina, unte is and þata munaida þairhgaggan.
Luke 19 5 [CA] jah biþe qam ana þamma stada, insaihvands iup Iesus gasahv ina jah qaþ du imma: Zakkaiu, sniumjands dalaþ atsteig: himma daga auk in garda þeinamma skal ik wisan.
Luke 19 6 [CA] jah sniumjands atstaig jah andnam ina faginonds.
Luke 19 7 [CA] jah gasaihvandans allai birodidedun, qiþandans þatei du frawaurhtis mans galaiþ [in gard] ussaljan.
Luke 19 8 [CA] standands þan Zakkaius qaþ du fraujin: sai, halbata aiginis meinis, frauja, gadailja unledaim, jah jabai hvis hva afholoda, fidurfalþ fragilda.
Luke 19 9 [CA] qaþ þan du imma Iesus þatei himma daga naseins þamma garda warþ, unte jah sa sunus Abrahamis ist;
Luke 19 10 [CA] qam auk sunus mans sokjan jah nasjan þans fralusanans.
Luke 19 11 [CA] at gahausjandam þan im þata, biaukands qaþ gajukon, bi þatei nehva Iairusalem was, jah þuhta im ei suns skulda wesi þiudangardi gudis gaswikunþjan.
Luke 19 12 [CA] qaþ þan: manna sums godakunds gaggida landis franiman sis þiudangardja jah gawandida sik.
Luke 19 13 [CA] athaitands þan taihun skalkans seinans atgaf im taihun dailos jah qaþ du im: kaupoþ, unte ik qimau.
Luke 19 14 [CA] iþ baurgjans is fijaidedun ina jah insandidedun airu afar imma qiþandans: ni wileima þana þiudanon ufar unsis.
Luke 19 15 [CA] jah warþ, biþe atwandida sik aftra, andnimands þiudangardja jah haihait wopjan du sis þans skalkans þaimei atgaf þata silubr, ei gakunnaidedi hva hvarjizuh gawaurhtedi.
Luke 19 16 [CA] qam þan sa frumista qiþands: frauja, skatts þeins gawaurhta taihun skattans.
Luke 19 17 [CA] jah qaþ du imma: waila, goda skalk, unte in leitilamma wast triggws, sijais waldufni habands ufar taihun baurgim.
Luke 19 18 [CA] jah qam anþar qiþands: frauja, skatts þeins gawaurhta fimf skattans.
Luke 19 19 [CA] qaþ þan jah du þamma: jah þu sijais ufaro fimf baurgim.
Luke 19 20 [CA] jah sums qam qiþands: frauja, sai, sa skatts þeins þanei habaida galagidana in fanin;
Luke 19 21 [CA] ohta mis auk þuk, unte manna hardus is. nimis þatei ni lagides jah sneiþis þatei ni saisost.
Luke 19 22 [CA] jah qaþ du imma: us munþa þeinamma stoja þuk, unselja skalk jah lata. wisseis þatei ik manna hardus im, nimands þatei ni lagida jah sneiþands þatei ni saiso;
Luke 19 23 [CA] jah duhve ni atlagides þata silubr mein du skattjam? jah <ik> qimands miþ wokra galausidedjau þata.
Luke 19 24 [CA] jah du þaim faurastandandam qaþ: nimiþ af imma þana skatt jah gibiþ þamma þos taihun dailos habandin.
Luke 19 25 [CA] jah qeþun du imma: frauja, habaiþ taihun dailos.
Luke 19 26 [CA] qiþa allis izwis þatei hvarjammeh habandane gibada, iþ af þamma unhabandin jah þatei habaiþ afnimada af imma.
Luke 19 27 [CA] aþþan sweþauh fijands meinans jainans, þaiei ni wildedun mik þiudanon ufar sis, briggiþ her jah usqimiþ faura mis.
Luke 19 28 [CA] jah qiþands þata iddja fram, usgaggands in Iairusaulwma.
Luke 19 29 [CA] jah warþ, biþe nehva was Beþsfagein jah Beþanijin, at fairgunja þatei haitada alewjo, insandida twans siponje seinaize
Luke 19 30 [CA] qiþands: gaggats in þo wiþrawairþon haim, in þizaiei inngaggandans bigitats fulan asilaus gabundanana, ana þammei ni ainshun aiw manne sat; andbindandans ina attiuhiþ.
Luke 19 31 [CA] jah jabai hvas inqis fraihnai: duhve andbindiþ? swa qiþaits du imma þatei frauja þis gairneiþ.
Luke 19 32 [CA] galeiþandans þan þai insandidans bigetun, swaswe qaþ du im.
Luke 19 33 [CA] andbindandam þan im <þana fulan> qeþun þai fraujans þis du im: duhve andbindats þana fulan?
Luke 19 34 [CA] iþ eis qeþun: fraujin þaurfts þis ist.
Luke 19 35 [CA] jah attauhun þana fulan Iesua jah uswairpandans wastjos seinos ana þana fulan ussatidedun Iesu.
Luke 19 36 [CA] gaggandin þan imma ufstrawidedun wastjom seinaim ana wiga.
Luke 19 37 [CA] biþe þan is nehva was, juþan at ibdaljin þis fairgunjis alewabagme, dugunnun alakjo managei siponje faginondans hazjan guþ stibnai mikilai in allaizo þoze sehvun mahte,
Luke 19 38 [CA] qiþandans: þiuþida sa qimanda þiudans in namin fraujins; gawairþi in himina jah wulþus in hauhistjam.
Luke 19 39 [CA] jah sumai Fareisaie us þizai managein qeþun du imma: laisari, sak þaim siponjam þeinaim.
Luke 19 40 [CA] jah andhafjands qaþ du im: qiþa izwis þatei jabai þai slawand, stainos hropjand.
Luke 19 41 [CA] jah sunsei nehva was, gasaihvands þo baurg gaigrot bi þo, qiþands:
Luke 19 42 [CA] þatei iþ wissedeis jah þu in þamma daga þeinamma þo du gawairþja þeinamma! iþ nu gafulgin ist faura augam þeinaim,
Luke 19 43 [CA] þatei qimand dagos ana þus, jah bigraband fijands þeinai grabai þuk jah bistandand þuk jah biwaibjand þuk allaþro.
Luke 19 44 [CA] jah airþai þuk gaïbnjand jah barna þeina in þus jah ni letand in þus stain ana staina, in þizei ni ufkunþes þata mel niuhseinais þeinaizos.
Luke 19 45 [CA] jah galeiþands in alh dugann uswairpan þans frabugjandans in izai jah bugjandans,
Luke 19 46 [CA] qiþands du im: gameliþ ist þatei gards meins gards bido ist; iþ jus ina gatawideduþ du filegrja þiube.
Luke 19 47 [CA] jah was laisjands daga hvammeh in þizai alh: iþ þai auhmistans gudjans jah bokarjos sokidedun ina usqistjan jah þai frumistans manageins.
Luke 19 48 [CA] jah ni bigetun hva gatawidedeina; managei auk alakjo hahaida du hausjan imma.
Luke 20 1 [CA] Jah warþ in sumamma dage jainaize at laisjandin imma þo managein in alh jah wailamerjandin, atstoþun þai gudjans jah bokarjos miþ þaim sinistam
Luke 20 2 [CA] jah qeþun du imma qiþandans: qiþ unsis, in hvamma waldufnje þata taujis, aiþþau hvas ist saei gaf þus þata waldufni?
Luke 20 3 [CA] andhafjands þan qaþ du im: fraihna izwis jah ik ainis waurdis jah qiþiþ mis:
Luke 20 4 [CA] daupeins Iohannis uzuh himina was þau uzuh mannam?
Luke 20 5 [CA] iþ eis þahtedun miþ sis misso qiþandans þatei jabai qiþam: us himina, qiþiþ: aþþan duhve ni galaubideduþ imma?
Luke 20 6 [CA] iþ jabai qiþam: us mannam, alla so managei stainam afwairpiþ unsis; triggwaba galaubjand auk allai Iohannen praufetu wisan.
Luke 20 7 [CA] jah andhofun ei ni wissedeina hvaþro.
Luke 20 8 [CA] jah Iesus qaþ im: ni ik izwis qiþa, in hvamma waldufnje þata tauja.
Luke 20 9 [CA] dugann þan du managein qiþan þo gajukon: manna ussatida weinagard, jah anafalh ina waurstwjam jah aflaiþ jera ganoha.
Luke 20 10 [CA] jah in mela insandida du þaim aurtjam skalk, ei akranis þis weinagardis gebeina imma. iþ þai aurtjans usbliggwandans ina insandidedun lausana.
Luke 20 11 [CA] jah anaaiauk sandjan anþarana skalk; iþ eis jah jainana bliggwandans jah unswerandans insandidedun lausana.
Luke 20 12 [CA] jah anaaiauk sandjan þridjan; iþ eis jah þana gawondondans uswaurpun.
Luke 20 13 [CA] qaþ þan sa frauja þis weinagardis: hva taujau? sandja sunu meinana þana liuban; aufto þana gasaihvandans aistand.
Luke 20 14 [CA] gasaihvandans þan ina þai aurtjans þahtedun miþ sis misso qiþandans, sa ist sa arbinumja; afslaham ina, ei uns wairþai þata arbi.
Luke 20 15 [CA] jah uswairpandans ina ut us þamma weinagarda usqemun. hva nu taujai im frauja þis weinagardis?
Luke 20 16 [CA] qimiþ jah usqisteiþ aurtjam þaim jah gibiþ þana weinagard anþaraim. gahausjandans qeþun þan: nis~sijai.
Luke 20 17 [CA] iþ is insaihvands du im qaþ: aþþan hva ist þata gamelido: stains þammei uskusun timrjans, sah warþ du haubida waihstins?
Luke 20 18 [CA] hvazuh saei driusiþ ana þana stain, gakrotuda; iþ ana þanei driusiþ, diswinþeiþ ina.
Luke 20 19 [CA] jah sokidedun þai bokarjos jah auhumistans gudjans uslagjan ana ina handuns in þizai hveilai jah ohtedun þo managein; froþun auk þatei du im þo gajukon qaþ.
Luke 20 20 [CA] jah afleiþandans insandidedun ferjans, þans us liutein taiknjandans sik garaihtans wisan, ei gafaifaheina is waurdei jah atgebeina ina reikja jah waldufnja kindinis.
Luke 20 21 [CA] jah frehun ina qiþandans: laisari, witum þatei raihtaba rodeis jah laiseis jah ni andsaihvis andwairþi, ak bi sunjai wig gudis laiseis:
Luke 20 22 [CA] skuldu ist unsis kaisara gild giban þau niu?
Luke 20 23 [CA] bisaihvands þan ize unselein Iesus qaþ du im: hva mik fraisiþ?
Luke 20 24 [CA] ataugeiþ mis skatt: hvis habaiþ manleikan jah ufarmeli? andhafjandans þan qeþun: kaisaris.
Luke 20 25 [CA] iþ is qaþuh du im: us~nu~gibiþ þo kaisaris kaisara jah þo gudis guda.
Luke 20 26 [CA] jah ni mahtedun gafahan is waurde in andwairþja manageins jah sildaleikjandans andawaurde is gaþahaidedun.
Luke 20 27 [CA] du atgaggandans þan sumai Saddukaie, þaiei qiþand usstass ni wisan, frehun ina
Luke 20 28 [CA] qiþandans: laisari, Moses gamelida uns, jabai hvis broþar gadauþnai aigands qen, jah sa unbarnahs gadauþnai, ei nimai broþar is þo qen jah urraisjai fraiw broþr seinamma.
Luke 20 29 [CA] sibun nu broþrjus wesun, jah sa frumista nimands qen gadauþnoda unbarnahs.
Luke 20 30 [CA] jah nam anþar þo qen, jah sa gaswalt unbarnahs.
Luke 20 31 [CA] jah þridja nam þo samaleiko; samaleiko þan jah þai sibun, jah ni biliþun barne jah gaswultun.
Luke 20 32 [CA] Spedista allaize gadauþnoda jah so qens.
Luke 20 33 [CA] in þizai usstassai nu, hvarjis þize wairþiþ qens? þai auk sibun aihtedun þo du qenai.
Luke 20 34 [CA] jah andhafjands qaþ du im Iesus: þai sunjus þis aiwis liugand jah liuganda;
Luke 20 35 [CA] iþ þaiei wairþai sind jainis aiwis niutan jah usstassais us dauþaim, ni liugand ni liuganda;
Luke 20 36 [CA] nih allis gaswiltan þanaseiþs magun, ibnans aggilum auk sind jah sunjus sind gudis, usstassais sunjus wisandans.
Luke 20 37 [CA] aþþan þatei urreisand dauþans, jah Moses bandwida ana aihvatundjai, swe qiþiþ: sahv fraujan guþ Abrahamis jah guþ Isakis jah guþ Iakobis.
Luke 20 38 [CA] aþþan guþ nist dauþaize, ak qiwaize; allai auk imma liband.
Luke 20 39 [CA] andhafjandans þan sumai þize bokarje qeþun: laisari, waila qast.
Luke 20 40 [CA] niþ~þan þanaseiþs gadaurstedun fraihnan ina ni waihtais.
Luke 20 41 [CA] qaþ þan du im: hvaiwa qiþand Xristu sunu Daweidis wisan?
Luke 20 42 [CA] jah silba Daweid qiþiþ in bokom psalmo<no>: qaþ frauja du fraujin meinamma: sit af taihswon meinai,
Luke 20 43 [CA] unte ik galagja fijands þeinans fotubaurd fotiwe þeinaize.
