John 5 45 [CA] . . . . þatei ik wrohidedjau izwis du attin; ist saei wrohida izwis, Moses, du þammei jus weneiþ.
John 5 46 [CA] jabai allis Mose galaubidedeiþ, ga~þau~laubidedeiþ mis; bi mik auk jains gamelida.
John 5 47 [CA] þande nu jainis melam ni galaubeiþ, hvaiwa meinaim waurdam galaubjaiþ?
John 6 1 [CA] Afar þata galaiþ Iesus ufar marein þo Galeilaie jah Tibairiade.
John 6 2 [CA] jah laistida ina manageins filu, unte gasehvun taiknins þozei gatawida bi siukaim.
John 6 3 [CA] usiddja þan ana fairguni Iesus jah jainar gasat miþ siponjam seinaim.
John 6 4 [CA] wasuh þan nehva pasxa, so dulþs Iudaie.
John 6 5 [CA] þaruh ushof augona Iesus jah gaumida þammei manageins filu iddja du imma, qaþuh du Filippau: hvaþro bugjam hlaibans, ei matjaina þai?
John 6 6 [CA] þatuh þan qaþ fraisands ina; iþ silba wissa þatei habaida taujan.
John 6 7 [CA] andhof imma Filippus: twaim hundam skatte hlaibos ni ganohai sind þaim, þei nimai hvarjizuh leitil.
John 6 8 [CA] qaþ ains þize siponje is, Andraias, broþar Paitraus Seimonaus:
John 6 9 [CA] ist magula ains her, saei habaiþ ·e· hlaibans barizeinans jah ·b· fiskans; akei þata hva ist du swa managaim?
John 6 10 [CA] iþ Iesus qaþ: waurkeiþ þans mans anakumbjan. wasuh þan hawi manag ana þamma stada. þaruh anakumbidedun wairos raþjon swaswe fimf þusundjos.
John 6 11 [CA] namuh þan þans hlaibans Iesus jah awiliudonds gadailida þaim anakumbjandam; samaleiko jah þize fiske, swa filu swe wildedun.
John 6 12 [CA] þanuh, biþe sadai waurþun, qaþ du siponjam seinaim: galisiþ þos aflifnandeins drauhsnos, þei waihtai ni fraqistnai.
John 6 13 [CA] þanuh galesun jah gafullidedun ·ib· tainjons gabruko us fimf hlaibam þaim barizeinam, þatei aflifnoda þaim matjandam.
John 6 14 [CA] þaruh þai mans gasaihvandans þoei gatawida taikn Iesus, qeþun þatei sa ist bi sunjai praufetus sa qimanda in þo manaseþ.
John 6 15 [CA] iþ Iesus kunnands þatei munaidedun usgaggan jah wilwan <ina> ei tawidedeina ina du þiudana, afiddja aftra in fairguni is ains.
John 6 16 [CA] iþ swe seiþu warþ, atiddjedun siponjos is ana marein,
John 6 17 [CA] jah usstigun in skip, iddjedunuh ufar marein in Kafarnaum. jah riqis juþan warþ jah ni atiddja nauhþan du im Iesus.
John 6 18 [CA] iþ marei winda mikilamma waiandin urraisida was.
John 6 19 [CA] þaruh farjandans swe spaurde ·k· jah ·e· aiþþau ·l· gasaihvand Iesu gaggandan ana marein jah nehva skipa qimandan jah ohtedun sis.
John 6 20 [CA] þaruh is qaþ <im>: ik im, ni ogeiþ izwis.
John 6 21 [CA] þaruh wildedun ina niman in skip, jah sunsaiw þata skip warþ ana airþai ana þoei eis iddjedun.
John 6 22 [CA] iftumin daga managei sei stoþ hindar marein, sehvun þatei skip anþar ni was jainar alja ain, jah þatei miþ~ni~qam siponjam seinaim Iesus in þata skip, ak ainai siponjos is galiþun.
John 6 23 [CA] anþara þan skipa qemun us Tibairiadau nehva þamma stada, þarei matidedun hlaif, ana þammei awiliudoda frauja.
John 6 24 [CA] þaruh þan gasahv managei þatei Iesus nist jainar nih siponjos is, gastigun in skipa jah qemun in Kafarnaum sokjandans Iesu.
John 6 25 [CA] jah bigetun ina hindar marein qeþunuh du imma: rabbei, hvan her qamt?
John 6 26 [CA] andhof im Iesus jah qaþ: amen amen qiþa izwis, sokeiþ mik, ni þatei sehvuþ taiknins jah fauratanja, ak þatei matideduþ þize hlaibe jah sadai waurþuþ.
John 6 27 [CA] waurkjaiþ ni þana mat þana fralusanan, ak mat þana wisandan du libainai aiweinon, þanei sunus mans gibiþ izwis; þanuh auk atta gasiglida guþ.
John 6 28 [CA] þaruh qeþun du imma: hva taujaima, ei waurkjaima waurstwa gudis?
John 6 29 [CA] andhof Iesus jah qaþ du im: þat~ist waurstw gudis, ei galaubjaiþ þammei insandida jains.
John 6 30 [CA] qeþun du imma: aþþan hva taujis þu taikne, ei saihvaima jah galaubjaima þus? hva waurkeis?
John 6 31 [CA] attans unsarai manna matidedun ana auþidai, swaswe ist gameliþ: hlaif us himina gaf im du matjan.
John 6 32 [CA] þaruh qaþ im Iesus: amen amen qiþa izwis, ni Moses gaf izwis hlaif us himina, ak atta meins gaf izwis hlaif us himina þana sunjeinan.
John 6 33 [CA] sa auk hlaifs gudis ist, saei atstaig us himina jah gaf libain þizai manasedai.
John 6 34 [CA] þanuh qeþun du imma: frauja, framwigis gif unsis þana hlaif.
John 6 35 [CA] jah qaþ du im Iesus: ik im sa hlaifs libainais; þana gaggandan du mis ni huggreiþ jah þana galaubjandan du mis ni þaurseiþ hvanhun.
John 6 36 [CA] akei qaþ izwis þatei gasehvuþ mik jah ni galaubeiþ.
John 6 37 [CA] all þatei gaf mis atta, du mis qimiþ, jah þana gaggandan du mis ni uswairpa ut;
John 6 38 [CA] unte atstaig us himina, nih þeei taujau wiljan meinana, ak wiljan þis sandjandins mik.
John 6 39 [CA] . . . .
John 6 40 [CA] þatuh þan ist wilja þis sandjandins mik, ei hvazuh saei saihviþ þana sunu jah galaubeiþ du imma, aigi libain aiweinon, jah urraisja ina ik in spedistin daga.
John 6 41 [CA] birodidedun þan Iudaieis bi ina, unte qaþ: ik im hlaifs sa atsteigands us himina,
John 6 42 [CA] jah qeþun: niu sa ist Iesus sa sunus Iosefis, þizei weis kunþedum attan jah aiþein? hvaiwa nu qiþiþ sa þatei us himina atstaig?
John 6 43 [CA] andhof þan Iesus jah qaþ du im: ni birodeiþ miþ izwis misso.
John 6 44 [CA] ni manna mag qiman at mis, nibai atta saei sandida mik atþinsiþ ina, jah ik urraisja ina in þamma spedistin daga.
John 6 45 [CA] ist gameliþ ana praufetum: jah wairþand allai laisidai gudis. hvazuh nu sa gahausjands at attin jah ganam gaggiþ du mis.
John 6 46 [CA] ni þatei attan sehvi hvas, nibai saei was fram attin, sa sahv attan.
John 6 47 [CA] amen amen qiþa izwis: saei galaubeiþ du mis aih libain aiweinon.
John 6 48 [CA] ik im sa hlaifs libainais.
John 6 49 [CA] attans izwarai matidedun manna in auþidai jah gaswultun.
John 6 50 [CA] sa ist hlaifs saei us himina atstaig, ei saei þis matjai, ni gadauþnai.
John 6 51 [CA] ik im hlaifs sa libanda, sa us himina qumana; jabai hvas matjiþ þis hlaibis, libaiþ in ajukduþ; jah þan sa hlaifs þanei ik giba, leik mein ist þatei ik giba in þizos manasedais libainais.
John 6 52 [CA] þanuh sokun miþ sis misso Iudaieis qiþandans: hvaiwa mag sa unsis leik giban du matjan?
John 6 53 [CA] þaruh qaþ du im Iesus: amen amen qiþa izwis, nibai matjiþ leik þis sunaus mans jah driggkaiþ is bloþ, ni habaiþ libain in izwis silbam.
John 6 54 [CA] saei matjiþ mein leik jah driggkiþ mein bloþ, aih libain aiweinon, jah ik urraisja ina in þamma spedistin daga.
John 6 55 [CA] þata auk leik meinata bi sunjai ist mats, jah þata bloþ mein bi sunjai ist draggk.
John 6 56 [CA] saei matjiþ mein leik jah driggkiþ mein bloþ, in mis wisiþ jah ik in imma.
John 6 57 [CA] swaswe insandida mik libands atta, jah ik liba in attins, jah saei matjiþ mik, jah sa libaiþ in meina.
John 6 58 [CA] sa ist hlaifs saei us himina atstaig, ni swaswe matidedun attans izwarai manna jah gadauþnodedun; iþ saei matjiþ þana hlaif libaiþ in ajukduþ.
John 6 59 [CA] þata qaþ in swnagoge laisjands in Kafarnaum.
John 6 60 [CA] þanuh managai gahausjandans þize siponje is qeþun: hardu ist þata waurd, hvas mag þis hausjon?
John 6 61 [CA] iþ witands Iesus in sis silbin þatei birodidedun þata þai siponjos is, qaþ du im: þata izwis gamarzeiþ?
John 6 62 [CA] jabai nu gasaihviþ sunu mans ussteigan, þadei was faurþis?
John 6 63 [CA] ahma ist saei liban taujiþ, þata leik ni boteiþ waiht. þo waurda þoei ik rodida izwis, ahma ist jah libains ist,
John 6 64 [CA] akei sind izwara sumai, þaiei ni galaubjand. wissuh þan us frumistja Iesus hvarjai sind þai ni galaubjandans, jah hvas ist saei galeiweiþ ina.
John 6 65 [CA] jah qaþ: duþe qaþ izwis þatei ni ainshun mag qiman at mis, nibai ist atgiban imma fram attin meinamma.
John 6 66 [CA] uzuh þamma mela managai galiþun siponje is ibukai jah þanaseiþs miþ imma ni iddjedun.
John 6 67 [CA] þaruh qaþ Iesus du þaim twalibim: ibai jah jus wileiþ galeiþan?
John 6 68 [CA] þanuh andhof imma Seimon Paitrus: frauja, du hvamma galeiþaima? waurda libainais aiweinons habais.
John 6 69 [CA] jah weis galaubidedum jah ufkunþedum þatei þu is Xristus, sunus gudis libandins.
John 6 70 [CA] andhof im Iesus: niu ik izwis ·ib· gawalida jah izwara ains diabaulus ist?
John 6 71 [CA] qaþuh þan þana Iudan Seimonis, Iskariotu, sa auk habaida ina galewjan, ains wisands þize twalibe.
John 7 1 [CA] Jah hvarboda Iesus afar þata in Galeilaia; ni auk wilda in Iudaia gaggan, unte sokidedun ina þai Iudaieis usqiman.
John 7 2 [CA] wasuh þan nehva dulþs Iudaie, so hleþrastakeins.
John 7 3 [CA] þanuh qeþun du imma broþrjus is: usleiþ þaþro jah gagg in Iudaian, ei jah þai siponjos <þeinai> saihvaina waurstwa þeina þoei þu taujis.
John 7 4 [CA] ni manna auk in analaugnein hva taujiþ jah sokeiþ sik uskunþana wisan. jabai þata taujis, bairhtei þuk silban þizai manasedai.
John 7 5 [CA] ni auk þai broþrjus is galaubidedun imma.
John 7 6 [CA] þaruh qaþ im Iesus: mel mein ni nauh ist, iþ mel izwar sinteino ist manwu.
John 7 7 [CA] ni mag so manaseþs fijan izwis, iþ mik fijaiþ; unte ik weitwodja bi ins þatei waurstwa ize ubila sind.
John 7 8 [CA] jus galeiþiþ in dulþ þo, iþ ik ni nauh galeiþa in þo dulþ, unte meinata mel ni nauh usfulliþ ist.
John 7 9 [CA] þatuh þan qaþ du im wisands in Galeilaia.
John 7 10 [CA] iþ biþe galiþun þai broþrjus is, þanuh jah is galaiþ in þo dulþ ni andaugjo, ak swe analaugniba.
John 7 11 [CA] þanuh Iudaieis sokidedun ina in þizai dulþai jah qeþun: hvar ist jains?
John 7 12 [CA] jah birodeins mikila <bi ina> was in managein: sumaih qeþun þatei sunjeins ist; anþarai qeþun: ne, ak airzeiþ þo managein.
John 7 13 [CA] nih þan ainshun sweþauh balþaba rodida bi ina in agisis Iudaie.
John 7 14 [CA] iþ juþan ana midjai dulþ usstaig Iesus in alh jah laisida.
John 7 15 [CA] jah sildaleikidedun manageins qiþandans: hvaiwa sa bokos kann unuslaisiþs?
John 7 16 [CA] andhof þan Iesus jah qaþ: so meina laiseins nist meina, ak þis sandjandins mik.
John 7 17 [CA] jabai hvas wili wiljan is taujan, ufkunnaiþ bi þo laisein framuh guda sijai, þau iku fram mis silbin rodja.
John 7 18 [CA] saei fram sis silbin rodeiþ, hauhiþa seina sokeiþ; iþ saei sokeiþ hauhiþa þis sandjandins sik, sah sunjeins ist jah inwindiþa in imma nist.
John 7 19 [CA] niu Moses gaf izwis witoþ? jah ni ainshun izwara taujiþ þata witoþ; hva mik sokeiþ usqiman?
John 7 20 [CA] andhof so managei jah qeþun: unhulþon habais; hvas þuk sokeiþ usqiman?
John 7 21 [CA] andhof Iesus jah qaþ du im: ain waurstw gatawida, jah allai sildaleikeiþ.
John 7 22 [CA] duþþe Moses atgaf izwis bimait, ni þatei fram Mose sijai, ak us attam, jah in sabbato bimaitiþ mannan.
John 7 23 [CA] jabai bimait nimiþ manna in sabbato, ei ni gatairaidau witoþ þata Mosezis; iþ mis hatizoþ, unte allana mannan hailana gatawida in sabbato?
John 7 24 [CA] ni stojaiþ bi siunai, ak þo garaihton staua stojaiþ.
John 7 25 [CA] qeþunuh þan sumai þize Iairusaulwmeite: niu sa ist þammei sokjand usqiman?
John 7 26 [CA] jah sai, andaugiba rodeiþ jah waiht du imma ni qiþand; ibai aufto bi sunjai ufkunþedun þai reiks þatei sa ist bi sunjai Xristus?
John 7 27 [CA] akei þana kunnum, hvaþro ist; iþ Xristus, biþe qimiþ, ni manna wait hvaþro ist.
John 7 28 [CA] hropida þan in alh laisjands Iesus jah qiþands: jah mik kunnuþ jah wituþ hvaþro im; jah af mis silbin ni qam, ak ist sunjeins saei sandida mik, þanei jus ni kunnuþ.
John 7 29 [CA] iþ ik kann ina, unte fram imma im, jah is mik insandida.
John 7 30 [CA] sokidedun þan ina gafahan, jah ni ainshun uslagida ana ina handu, unte nauhþanuh ni atiddja hveila is.
John 7 31 [CA] iþ managai þizos manageins galaubidedun imma jah qeþun: <ei> Xristus, þan qimiþ, ibai [ei] managizeins taiknins taujai þaimei sa tawida?
John 7 32 [CA] hausidedun þan Fareisaieis þo managein birodjandein bi ina þata. inuhsandidedun andbahtans þai Fareisaieis jah þai auhumistans gudjans, ei gafaifaheina ina.
John 7 33 [CA] þanuh qaþ Iesus: nauh leitila hveila miþ izwis im, jah þan gagga du þamma sandjandin mik.
John 7 34 [CA] sokeiþ mik jah ni bigitiþ, jah þarei im ik, jus ni maguþ qiman.
John 7 35 [CA] þaruh qeþun þai Iudaieis du sis misso: hvadre sa skuli gaggan, þei weis ni bigitaima ina? nibai in distahein þiudo skuli gaggan jah laisjan þiudos?
John 7 36 [CA] hva sijai þata waurd, þatei qaþ: sokeiþ mik jah ni bigitiþ, jah þarei im ik, jus ni maguþ qiman?
John 7 37 [CA] iþ in spedistin daga þamma mikilin dulþais stoþ Iesus jah hropida qiþands: jabai hvana þaursjai, gaggai du mis jah driggkai.
John 7 38 [CA] saei galaubeiþ du mis, swaswe qaþ gameleins, ahvos us wambai is rinnand watins libandins.
John 7 39 [CA] þatuh þan qaþ bi ahman þanei skuldedun niman þai galaubjandans du imma; unte ni nauhþanuh was ahma sa weiha ana im, unte Iesus nauhþanuh ni hauhiþs was.
John 7 40 [CA] managai þan þizos manageins hausjandans þize waurde qeþun: sa ist bi sunjai sa praufetes.
John 7 41 [CA] sumaih qeþun: sa ist Xristus. sumaih qeþun: ibai þau us Galeilaia Xristus qimiþ?
John 7 42 [CA] niu gameleins qaþ þatei us fraiwa Daweidis jah us Beþlaihaim weihsa, þarei was Daweid, Xristus qimiþ?
John 7 43 [CA] þanuh missaqiss in þizai managein warþ bi ina.
John 7 44 [CA] sumaih þan ize wildedun fahan ina; akei ni ainshun uslagida ana ina handuns.
John 7 45 [CA] galiþun þan þai andbahtos du þaim auhumistam gudjam jah Fareisaium; þaruh qeþun du im jainai: duhve ni attauhuþ ina?
John 7 46 [CA] andhofun þai andbahtos: ni hvanhun aiw rodida manna, swaswe sa manna.
John 7 47 [CA] andhofun þan im þai Fareisaieis: ibai jah jus afairzidai sijuþ?
John 7 48 [CA] sai, jau ainshun þize reike galaubidedi imma aiþþau Fareisaie?
John 7 49 [CA] alja so managei, þaiei ni kunnun witoþ, fraqiþanai sind.
John 7 50 [CA] qaþ Nikaudemus du im, saei atiddja du imma in naht, sums wisands izei:
John 7 51 [CA] ibai witoþ unsar stojiþ mannan, nibai faurþis hauseiþ fram imma jah ufkunnaiþ hva taujai?
John 7 52 [CA] andhofun jah qeþun du imma: ibai jah þu us Galeilaia is? ussokei jah saihv þatei praufetus us Galeilaia ni urreisiþ.

John 8 12 [CA] Aftra du im Iesus rodida qaþuh: ik im liuhaþ manasedais; saei laisteiþ mik ni gaggiþ in riqiza, ak habaiþ liuhaþ libainais.
John 8 13 [CA] þanuh qeþun du imma þai Fareisaieis: þu bi þuk silban weitwodeis; so weitwodiþa þeina nist sunjeina.
John 8 14 [CA] andhof Iesus jah qaþ du im: jah jabai ik weitwodja bi mik silban, sunja ist so weitwodiþa meina, unte wait hvaþro qam jah hvaþ galeiþa, iþ jus ni wituþ hvaþro qima, aiþþau hvaþ galeiþa.
John 8 15 [CA] jus bi leika stojiþ, iþ ik ni stoja ainnohun.
John 8 16 [CA] jaþ~þan jabai stoja ik, staua meina sunjeina ist, unte ains ni im, ak ik jah saei sandida mik atta.
John 8 17 [CA] jah þan in witoda izwaramma gameliþ ist þatei twaddje manne weitwodiþa sunja ist.
John 8 18 [CA] ik im saei weitwodja bi mik silban, jah weitwodeiþ bi mik saei sandida mik atta.
John 8 19 [CA] qeþun þan du imma: hvar ist sa atta þeins? andhof Iesus: ni mik kunnuþ nih attan meinana; iþ mik kunþedeiþ, jah þau attan meinana kunþedeiþ.
John 8 20 [CA] þo waurda rodida in gazaufwlakio, laisjands in alh; jah ainshun ni faifah ina, unte nauhþanuh ni qam hveila is.
John 8 21 [CA] þanuh qaþ aftra du im Iesus: ik galeiþa, jah sokeiþ mik, jah in frawaurhtai izwarai gadauþniþ. þadei ik gagga, jus ni maguþ qiman.
John 8 22 [CA] qeþun þan Iudaieis: nibai usqimai sis silbin, ei qiþiþ: þadei ik gagga, jus ni maguþ qiman?
John 8 23 [CA] jah qaþ du im Iesus: jus us þaim dalaþro sijuþ, iþ ik us þaim iupaþro im; jus us þamma fairhvau sijuþ, iþ ik ni im us þamma fairhvau.
John 8 24 [CA] qaþ nu izwis þatei gadauþniþ in frawaurhtim izwaraim; jabai auk ni galaubeiþ þatei ik im, gadauþniþ in frawaurhtim izwaraim.
John 8 25 [CA] þaruh qeþun du imma: þu hvas is? jah qaþ du im Iesus: anastodeins, þatei jah rodja du izwis.
John 8 26 [CA] manag skal bi izwis rodjan jah stojan; akei saei sandida mik sunjeins ist; jah ik þatei hausida at imma þata rodja in þamma fairhvau.
John 8 27 [CA] ni froþun þatei attan im qaþ.
John 8 28 [CA] qaþuh þan du im Iesus: þan ushauheiþ þana sunu mans, þanuh ufkunnaiþ þatei ik im, jah af mis silbin tauja ni waiht, ak swaswe laisida mik atta meins, þata rodja.
John 8 29 [CA] jah saei sandida mik miþ mis ist; ni bilaiþ mis ainamma atta, unte ik þatei leikaiþ imma tauja sinteino.
John 8 30 [CA] þata imma rodjandin managai galaubidedun imma.
John 8 31 [CA] þanuh qaþ Iesus du þaim galaubjandam sis Iudaium: jabai jus gastandiþ in waurda meinamma, bi sunjai siponjos meinai sijuþ,
John 8 32 [CA] jah ufkunnaiþ sunja, jah so sunja frijans izwis briggiþ.
John 8 33 [CA] andhofun imma: fraiw Abrahamis sijum jah ni mannhun skalkinodedum aiw hvanhun; hvaiwa þu qiþis þatei frijai wairþiþ?
John 8 34 [CA] andhof im Iesus: amen amen, qiþa izwis þatei hvazuh saei taujiþ frawaurht, skalks ist frawaurhtai.
John 8 35 [CA] sah þan skalks ni wisiþ in garda du aiwa, sunus wisiþ du aiwa.
John 8 36 [CA] jabai nu sunus izwis frijans briggiþ, bi sunjai frijai sijuþ.
John 8 37 [CA] wait þatei fraiw Abrahamis sijuþ; akei sokeiþ mis usqiman, unte waurd mein ni gamot in izwis.
John 8 38 [CA] ik þatei gasahv at attin meinamma rodja, jah jus þatei hausideduþ fram attin izwaramma taujiþ.
John 8 39 [CA] andhofun jah qeþun du imma: atta unsar Abraham ist. qaþ im Iesus: iþ barna Abrahamis weseiþ, waurstwa Abrahamis tawidedeiþ.
John 8 40 [CA] iþ nu sokeiþ mik usqiman, mannan izei sunja izwis rodida, þoei hausida fram guda; þatuh Abraham ni tawida.
John 8 41 [CA] jus taujiþ toja attins izwaris. þanuh qeþun imma: weis us horinassau ni sijum gabauranai; ainana attan aigum, guþ.
John 8 42 [CA] qaþ du im Iesus: jabai guþ atta izwar wesi, friodedeiþ þau mik, unte ik fram guda urrann jah qam; nih þan auk fram mis silbin ni qam, ak is mik insandida.
John 8 43 [CA] duhve maþlein meina ni kunnuþ? unte ni maguþ hausjan waurd mein.
John 8 44 [CA] jus us attin diabaulau sijuþ jah lustuns þis attins izwaris wileiþ taujan. jains manamaurþrja was fram frumistja jah in sunjai ni gastoþ; unte nist sunja in imma. þan rodeiþ liugn, us seinaim rodeiþ, unte liugnja ist jah atta is.
John 8 45 [CA] iþ ik, þatei sunja rodida, ni galaubeiþ mis.
John 8 46 [CA] hvas izwara gasakiþ mik bi frawaurht? þande sunja qiþa, duhve ni galaubeiþ mis?
John 8 47 [CA] sa wisands us guda waurda gudis hauseiþ; duþe jus ni hauseiþ, unte us guda ni sijuþ.
John 8 48 [CA] andhofun þan þai Iudaieis jah qeþun du imma: niu waila qiþam weis þatei Samareites is þu jah unhulþon habais?
John 8 49 [CA] andhof Iesus: ik unhulþon ni haba, ak swera attan meinana, jah jus unsweraiþ mik.
John 8 50 [CA] ik ni sokja hauhein meina; ist saei sokeiþ jah stojiþ.
John 8 51 [CA] amen amen qiþa izwis: jabai hvas waurd mein fastaiþ, dauþu ni gasaihviþ aiwa dage.
John 8 52 [CA] þanuh qeþun du imma þai Iudaieis: nu ufkunþedum þatei unhulþon habais. Abraham gadauþnoda jah praufeteis, jah þu qiþis: jabai hvas mein waurd fastai, ni kausjai dauþau aiwa dage.
John 8 53 [CA] ibai þu maiza is attin unsaramma Abrahama, saei gadauþnoda? jah praufeteis gadauþnodedun. hvana þuk silban taujis þu?
John 8 54 [CA] andhof Iesus: jabai ik hauhja mik silban, so hauheins meina ni waihts ist; ist atta meins saei hauheiþ mik, þanei jus qiþiþ þatei guþ unsar ist.
John 8 55 [CA] jah ni kunnuþ ina; iþ ik kann ina; jah jabai qeþjau þatei ni kunnjau ina, sijau galeiks izwis liugnja; ak kann ina jah waurd is fasta.
John 8 56 [CA] Abraham atta izwar sifaida ei gasehvi dag meinana, jah gasahv jah faginoda.
John 8 57 [CA] þanuh qeþun þai Iudaieis du imma: fimf tiguns jere nauh ni habais jah Abraham sahvt?
John 8 58 [CA] qaþ im Iesus: amen amen qiþa izwis: faurþizei Abraham waurþi, im ik.
John 8 59 [CA] þanuh nemun stainans, ei waurpeina ana ina; iþ Iesus þan gafalh sik jah usiddja us alh usleiþands þairh midjans ins, jah hvarboda swa.
John 9 1 [CA] Jah þairhgaggands gaumida mann blindamma us gabaurþai.
John 9 2 [CA] þaruh frehun ina siponjos is qiþandans: rabbei, hvas frawaurhta, sau þau fadrein is, ei blinds gabaurans warþ?
John 9 3 [CA] andhof Iesus: nih sa frawaurhta nih fadrein is, ak ei bairhta waurþeina waurstwa gudis ana imma.
John 9 4 [CA] ik skal waurkjan waurstwa þis sandjandins mik, unte dags ist; qimiþ nahts, þa(n)ei ni manna mag waurkjan.
John 9 5 [CA] þan in þamma fairhvau im, liuhaþ im þis fairhvaus.
John 9 6 [CA] þata qiþands gaspaiw dalaþ, jah gawaurhta fani us þamma spaiskuldra, jah gasmait imma ana augona þata fani þamma blindin,
John 9 7 [CA] jah qaþ du imma: gagg þwahan in swumsl Siloamis, þatei gaskeirjada insandiþs. galaiþ jah afþwoh jah qam saihvands.
John 9 8 [CA] þanuh garaznans jah þai saihvandans ina faurþis, þatei is bidagwa was, qeþun: niu sa ist saei sat aihtronds?
John 9 9 [CA] sumaih qeþun: þatei sa ist; sumaih þatei galeiks þamma ist; iþ is qaþ: þatei ik im.
John 9 10 [CA] þanuh qeþun du imma: hvaiwa usluknodedun þus þo augona?
John 9 11 [CA] andhof jains jah qaþ: manna haitans Iesus fani gawaurhta jah bismait mis augona jah qaþ mis: gagg afþwahan in þata swumfsl Siloamis; iþ ik galaiþ jah biþwahands ussahv.
John 9 12 [CA] qeþun þan du imma: hvar ist sa? iþ is qaþ: ni wait.
John 9 13 [CA] gatiuhand ina du Fareisaium, þana saei was blinds.
John 9 14 [CA] wasuh þan sabbato, þan þata fani gawaurhta Iesus jah uslauk imma augona.
John 9 15 [CA] aftra þan frehun ina jah þai Fareisaieis hvaiwa ussahv; iþ is qaþ jah þaim: fani galagida mis ana augona jah afþwoh, jah saihva.
John 9 16 [CA] qeþun þan sumai þize Fareisaie: sa manna nist fram guda, þande sabbate daga ni witaiþ. sumaih qeþun: hvaiwa mag manna frawaurhts swaleikos taiknins taujan? jah missaqiss warþ miþ im.
John 9 17 [CA] qeþunuh du þamma faurþis blindin aftra: þu hva qiþis bi þana ei uslauk þus augona? iþ is qaþuh: þatei praufetus ist.
John 9 18 [CA] ni galaubidedun þan Iudaieis bi ina þatei is blinds wesi jah ussehvi, unte atwopidedun þans fadrein is, þis ussaihvandins.
John 9 19 [CA] jah frehun ins qiþandans: sau ist sa sunus izwar þanei jus qiþiþ þatei blinds gabaurans waurþi? hvaiwa nu saihviþ?
John 9 20 [CA] andhofun þan im þai fadrein is jah qeþun: witum þatei sa ist sunus unsar, jah þatei blinds gabaurans warþ;
John 9 21 [CA] iþ hvaiwa nu saihviþ ni witum, aiþþau hvas uslauk imma þo augona weis ni witum; silba uswahsans ist, ina fraihniþ, silba bi sik rodjai.
John 9 22 [CA] þata qeþun þai fadrein is, unte ohtedun sis Iudaiuns; juþan auk gaqeþun sis Iudaieis, ei, jabai hvas ina andhaihaiti Xristu, utana swnagogais wairþai.
John 9 23 [CA] duhþe þai berusjos is qeþun þatei uswahsans ist, silban fraihniþ.
John 9 24 [CA] atwopidedun þan anþaramma sinþa þana mannan saei was blinds, jah qeþun du imma: gif hauhein guda! weis witum þatei sa manna frawaurhts ist.
John 9 25 [CA] þanuh andhof jains: jabai frawaurhts ist, ik ni wait; þat~ain wait ei blinds was, iþ nu saihva.
John 9 26 [CA] þanuh qeþun <du imma> aftra: hva gatawida þus? hvaiwa uslauk þus augona?
John 9 27 [CA] andhof im: qaþ izwis ju jah ni hausideduþ; hva aftra wileiþ hausjan? ibai jah jus wileiþ þamma siponjos wairþan?
John 9 28 [CA] þanuh lailoun imma jah qeþun: þu is siponeis þamma, iþ weis Mose siponjos sijum.
John 9 29 [CA] weis witum þatei du Mose rodida guþ, iþ þana ni kunnum, hvaþro ist.
John 9 30 [CA] andhof sa manna jah qaþ du im: auk in þamma sildaleik ist, þatei jus ni wituþ hvaþro ist, jah uslauk mis augona.
John 9 31 [CA] witumuh þan þatei guþ frawaurhtaim ni andhauseiþ, ak jabai hvas gudblostreis ist jah wiljan is taujiþ, þamma hauseiþ.
John 9 32 [CA] fram aiwa ni gahausiþ was þatei uslukiþ hvas augona blindamma gabauranamma.
John 9 33 [CA] nih wesi sa fram guda, ni mahtedi taujan ni waiht.
John 9 34 [CA] andhofun jah qeþun du imma: in frawaurhtim þu gabaurans warst alls jah þu laiseis unsis? jah uswaurpun imma ut.
John 9 35 [CA] hausida Iesus þatei uswaurpun imma ut, jah bigat ina qaþuh du imma: þu ga~u~laubeis du sunau gudis?
John 9 36 [CA] andhof jains jah qaþ: an hvas ist, frauja, ei galaubjau du imma?
John 9 37 [CA] qaþ þan imma Iesus: jah gasahvt ina jah saei rodeiþ miþ þus, sa ist.
John 9 38 [CA] iþ is qaþuh: galaubja, frauja; jah inwait ina.
John 9 39 [CA] jah qaþ Iesus: du stauai ik in þamma fairhvau qam, ei þai unsaihvandans saihvaina jah þai saihvandans blindai wairþaina.
John 9 40 [CA] jah hausidedun þize Fareisaie sumai þata, þai wisandans miþ imma, jah qeþun du imma: ibai jah weis blindai sijum?
John 9 41 [CA] qaþ im Iesus: iþ blindai weseiþ, ni þau habaidedeiþ frawaurhtais; iþ nu qiþiþ þatei gasaihvam; eiþan frawaurhts izwara þairhwisiþ.
John 10 1 [CA] Amen amen qiþa izwis, saei inn ni atgaggiþ þairh daur in gardan lambe, ak steigiþ aljaþro, sah hliftus ist jah waidedja.
John 10 2 [CA] iþ sa inngaggands þairh daur hairdeis ist lambe.
John 10 3 [CA] þammuh daurawards uslukiþ, jah þo lamba stibnai is hausjand, jah þo swesona lamba haitiþ bi namin jah ustiuhiþ þo.
John 10 4 [CA] jah þan þo swesona <lamba> ustiuhiþ, faura im gaggiþ, jah þo lamba ina laistjand, unte kunnun stibna is.
John 10 5 [CA] iþ framaþjana ni laistjand, ak þliuhand faura imma, unte ni kunnun þize framaþjane stibna.
John 10 6 [CA] þo gajukon qaþ im Iesus: iþ jainai ni froþun hva was, þatei rodida du im.
John 10 7 [CA] þanuh qaþ aftra du im Iesus: amen amen, qiþa izwis þatei ik im daur þize lambe.
John 10 8 [CA] allai swa managai swe qemun, þiubos sind jah waidedjans; akei ni hausidedun im þo lamba.
John 10 9 [CA] ik im þata daur. þairh mik jabai hvas inngaggiþ, ganisiþ, jah inngaggiþ jah utgaggiþ jah winja bigitiþ.
John 10 10 [CA] þiubs ni qimiþ, nibai ei stilai jah ufsneiþai jah fraqistjai; iþ ik qam, ei libain aigeina jah managizo aigeina.
John 10 11 [CA] ik im hairdeis gods. hairdeis sa goda saiwala seina lagjiþ faur lamba.
John 10 12 [CA] iþ asneis jah saei nist hairdeis, þizei ni sind lamba swesa, gasaihviþ wulf qimandan jah bileiþiþ þaim lambam jah þliuhiþ, jah sa wulfs frawilwiþ þo jah distahjiþ þo lamba.
John 10 13 [CA] iþ sa asneis afþliuhiþ, unte asneis ist jah ni kar~ist ina þize lambe.
John 10 14 [CA] ik im hairdeis sa goda jah kann meina jah kunnun mik þo meina,
John 10 15 [CA] swaswe kann mik atta jah ik kann attan, jah saiwala meina lagja faur þo lamba.
John 10 16 [CA] jah anþara lamba aih þoei ni sind þis awistris, jah þo skal briggan, jah stibnos meinaizos hausjand, jah wairþand ain aweþi, ains hairdeis.
John 10 17 [CA] duhþe atta mik frijoþ, unte ik lagja saiwala meina, ei aftra nimau þo.
John 10 18 [CA] ni hvashun nimiþ þo af <mis, akei ik lagja þo af> mis silbin; waldufni haba aflagjan þo, jah waldufni haba aftra niman þo. þo anabusn nam at attin meinamma.
John 10 19 [CA] þanuh missaqiss aftra warþ miþ Iudaium in þize waurde.
John 10 20 [CA] qeþunuh managai ize: unhulþon habaiþ jah dwalmoþ; hva þamma hauseiþ?
John 10 21 [CA] sumaih qeþun: þo waurda ni sind unhulþon habandins; ibai mag unhulþo blindaim augona uslukan?
John 10 22 [CA] warþ þan inniujiþa in Iairusaulwmai, jah wintrus was.
John 10 23 [CA] jah hvarboda Iesus in alh in ubizwai Saulaumonis.
John 10 24 [CA] þanuh birunnun ina Iudaieis jah qeþun du imma: und hva saiwala unsara hahis? jabai þu sijais Xristus, qiþ unsis andaugiba.
John 10 25 [CA] andhof <im> Iesus: qaþ izwis, jah ni galaubeiþ; waurstwa þoei ik tauja in namin attins meinis, þo weitwodjand bi mik;
John 10 26 [CA] akei jus ni galaubeiþ, unte ni sijuþ lambe meinaize, swaswe qaþ izwis.
John 10 27 [CA] lamba meina stibnai meinai hausjand, jah ik kann þo, jah laistjand mik.
John 10 28 [CA] jah ik libain aiweinon giba im, jah ni fraqistnand aiw; jah ni frawilwiþ hvashun þo us handau meinai.
John 10 29 [CA] atta meins þatei fragaf mis, maizo allaim ist, jah ni aiw ainshun mag frawilwan þo us handau attins meinis.
John 10 30 [CA] ik jah atta meins ain siju.
John 10 31 [CA] nemun aftra stainans þai Iudaieis, ei waurpeina ana ina.
John 10 32 [CA] andhof im Iesus: managa goda waurstwa ataugida izwis us attin meinamma, in hvarjis þize waurstwe staineiþ mik?
John 10 33 [CA] andhofun imma þai Iudaieis: in godis waurstwis ni stainjam þuk, ak in wajamereins, jah þatei þu manna wisands taujis þuk silban du guda.
John 10 34 [CA] andhof im Iesus: niu ist gameliþ in witoda izwaramma: ik qaþ, guda sijuþ?
John 10 35 [CA] jabai jainans qaþ guda, du þaimei waurd gudis warþ, jah ni maht ist gatairan þata gamelido;
John 10 36 [CA] þanei atta gaweihaida jah insandida in þana fairhvu, jus qiþiþ þatei wajamerjau, unte qaþ: sunus gudis im?
John 10 37 [CA] niba taujau waurstwa attins meinis, ni galaubeiþ mis;
John 10 38 [CA] iþ jabai taujau, niba mis galaubjaiþ, þaim waurstwam galaubjaiþ, ei ufkunnaiþ jah galaubjaiþ þatei in mis atta jah ik in imma.
John 10 39 [CA] sokidedun ina aftra gafahan, jah usiddja us handum ize.
John 10 40 [CA] jah galaiþ aftra ufar Iaurdanu in þana stad þarei was Iohannes frumist daupjands, jah salida jainar.
John 10 41 [CA] jah managai qemun at imma jah qeþun þatei Iohannes gatawida taikne ni ainohun; iþ allata þatei qaþ Iohannes bi þana, sunja was.
John 10 42 [CA] jah galaubidedun managai du imma jainar.

John 11 3 [CA] insandidedun þan þos swistrjus is du imma qiþandeins: frauja, sai, þanei frijos siuks ist.
John 11 4 [CA] iþ is gahausjands qaþ: so siukei nist du dauþau, ak in hauheinais gudis, ei hauhjaidau sunus gudis þairh þata.
John 11 5 [CA] frijoduh þan Iesus Marþan jah swistar izos jah Lazaru.

John 11 17 [CA] qimands þan Iesus bigat ina juþan fidwor dagans habandan in hlaiwa.

John 11 22 [CA] akei jah nu wait, ei þishvah þei bidjis guþ, gibiþ þus guþ.
John 11 23 [CA] qaþ izai Iesus: usstandiþ broþar þeins.
John 11 24 [CA] qaþ du imma Marþa: wait þatei usstandiþ in usstassai in þamma spedistin daga.
John 11 25 [CA] qaþ þan <izai> Iesus: ik im so usstass jah libains; saei galaubeiþ du mis, þauh ga~ba~dauþniþ, libaid;
John 11 26 [CA] jah hvazuh saei libaiþ jah galaubeiþ du mis, ni gadauþniþ aiw. galaubeis þata?
John 11 27 [CA] qaþ imma: jai, frauja, ik galaubida þatei þu is Xristus, sunus gudis, sa in þana fairhvu qimanda.
John 11 28 [CA] jah þata qiþandei galaiþ jah wopida Marjan, swistar seina, þiubjo qiþandei: laisareis qam jah haitiþ þuk.
John 11 29 [CA] iþ jaina, sunsei hausida, urrais sprauto jah iddja du imma.
John 11 30 [CA] niþ~þan nauhþanuh qam Iesus in weihsa, ak was nauhþanuh in þamma stada þarei gamotida imma Marþa.
John 11 31 [CA] Iudaieis þan þai wisandans miþ izai in garda þrafstjandans ija, gasaihvandans Marjan þatei sprauto usstoþ jah usiddja, iddjedunuh afar izai qiþandans þatei gaggiþ du hlaiwa, ei greitai jainar.
John 11 32 [CA] iþ Marja, sunsei qam þarei was Iesus, gasaihvandei ina draus imma du fotum qiþandei du imma: frauja, iþ weiseis her, ni þauh gaswulti meins broþar.
John 11 33 [CA] þanuh Iesus, sunsei gasahv ija greitandein jah Iudaiuns þaiei qemun miþ izai gretandans, inrauhtida ahmin jah inwagida sik silban.
John 11 34 [CA] jah qaþ: hvar lagideduþ ina? qeþun du imma: frauja, hiri jah saihv.
John 11 35 [CA] jah tagrida Iesus.
John 11 36 [CA] þaruh qeþun þai Iudaieis: sai, hvaiwa frioda ina.
John 11 37 [CA] sumai þan ize qeþun: niu mahta sa izei uslauk augona þamma blindin gataujan ei jah sa ni gadauþnodedi?
John 11 38 [CA] þanuh Iesus aftra inrauhtiþs in sis silbin gaggiþ du þamma hlaiwa. wasuh þan hulundi jah staina ufarlagida was ufaro.
John 11 39 [CA] qaþ Iesus: afnimiþ þana stain. qaþ du imma swistar þis dauþins Marþa: frauja, ju fuls ist; fidurdogs auk ist.

John 14 1 [CA] Ni indrobnai izwar hairto; galaubeiþ du guda jah du mis galaubeiþ.

John 14 3 [CA] jah þan jabai gagga, manwja izwis stad, aftra qima jah franima izwis du mis silbin, ei þarei im ik, þaruh sijuþ jah jus.

John 14 10 [CA] niu galaubeis þatei ik in attin jah atta in mis ist? þo waurda þoei ik rodja izwis, af mis silbin ni rodja, ak atta saei in mis ist, sa taujiþ þo waurstwa.
John 14 11 [CA] Galaubeiþ mis þatei ik in attin jah atta in mis; iþ jabai <ni>, in þize waurstwe [ni] galaubeiþ mis.
John 14 12 [CA] amen amen qiþa izwis, saei galaubeid mis: þo waurstwa þoei ik tauja, jah is taujiþ jah maizona þaim taujiþ; unte ik du attin gagga.
John 14 13 [CA] jah þatei hva bidjiþ in namin meinamma, þata tauja, ei hauhjaidau atta in sunau.
John 14 14 [CA] jabai hvis bidjiþ mik in namin meinamma, ik tauja.
John 14 15 [CA] jabai mik frijoþ, anabusnins meinos fastaid.
John 14 16 [CA] jah ik bidja attan, jah anþarana parakletu gibiþ izwis, ei sijai miþ izwis du aiwa,

John 14 18 [CA] ni leta izwis widuwairnans; qima at izwis.
John 14 19 [CA] nauh leitil, jah so manaseiþs mik ni þanaseiþs saihviþ; iþ jus saihviþ mik, þatei ik liba, jah jus libaiþ.
John 14 20 [CA] in jainamma daga ufkunnaiþ jus þatei ik in attin meinamma jah jus in mis jah ik in izwis.
John 14 21 [CA] Saei habaid anabusnins meinos jah fastaiþ þos, sa ist saei frijoþ mik: jah þan saei frijoþ mik, frijoda fram attin meinamma, jah ik frijo ina jah gabairhtja imma mik silban.
John 14 22 [CA] þaruh qaþ imma Iudas, ni sa Iskarjotes: frauja, hva warþ, ei unsis munais gabairhtjan þuk silban, iþ þizai manasedai ni?

John 14 24 [CA] iþ saei ni frioþ mik, þo waurda meina ni fastaiþ; jah þata waurd þatei hauseiþ nist mein, ak þis sandjandins mik attins.
John 14 25 [CA] þata rodida izwis at izwis wisands.

John 14 27 [CA] gawairþi bileiþa izwis, gawairþi mein giba izwis; ni swaswe so manaseþs gibiþ, ik giba izwis. ni indrobnaina izwara hairtona nih faurhtjaina.
John 14 28 [CA] Hausideduþ ei ik qaþ izwis: galeiþa jah qima at izwis; jabai frijodedeiþ mik, aiþþau jus faginodedeiþ ei ik gagga du attin: unte atta meins maiza mis ist.

John 15 1 [CA] Ik im weinatriu þata sunjeino, jah atta meins waurstwja ist.
John 15 2 [CA] all taine in mis unbairandane akran goþ, usnimiþ ita: jah all akran bairandane, gahraineiþ ita, ei managizo akran bairaina.
John 15 3 [CA] ju jus hrainjai sijuþ in þis waurdis þatei rodida du izwis.
John 15 4 [CA] wisaiþ in mis jah ik in izwis. swe sa weinatains ni mag akran bairan af sis silbin, niba ist ana weinatriwa, swah nih jus, niba in mis sijuþ.
John 15 5 [CA] ik im þata weinatriu, iþ jus weinatainos; saei wisiþ in mis jah ik in imma, swa bairiþ akran manag, þatei inuh mik ni maguþ taujan ni waiht.
John 15 6 [CA] niba saei wisiþ in mis, uswairpada ut swe weinatains, jah gaþaursniþ jah galisada, jah in fon galagjand jah inbrannjada.
John 15 7 [CA] aþþan jabai sijuþ in mis, jah waurda meina in izwis sind, þatahvah þei wileiþ bidjiþ, jah wairþiþ izwis.
John 15 8 [CA] in þamma hauhiþs ist atta meins, ei akran manag bairaiþ jah wairþaiþ meinai siponjos.
John 15 9 [CA] swaswe frijoda mik atta, swah ik frijoda izwis; wisaiþ in friaþwai meinai.
John 15 10 [CA] jabai anabusnins meinos fastaid, sijuþ in friaþwai meinai, swaswe ik anabusnins attins meinis fastaida, jah wisa in friaþwai is.
John 15 11 [CA] þata rodida izwis, ei faheþs meina in izwis sijai, jah faheds izwara usfulljaidau.
John 15 12 [CA] þata ist anabusns meina, ei frijoþ izwis misso, swaswe ik frijoda izwis.
John 15 13 [CA] maizein þizai friaþwa[i] manna ni habaiþ, ei hvas saiwala seina lagjiþ faur frijonds seinans.
John 15 14 [CA] jus frijonds meinai sijuþ, jabai taujiþ þatei ik anabiuda izwis.
John 15 15 [CA] þanaseiþs izwis ni qiþa skalkans; unte skalks ni wait hva taujiþ is frauja, iþ ik izwis qaþ frijonds, unte all þatei hausida at attin meinamma, gakannida izwis.
John 15 16 [CA] ni jus mik gawalideduþ, ak ik gawalida izwis <jah gasatida izwis> ei jus sniwaiþ jah akran bairaiþ, jah akran izwar du aiwa sijai, ei þatahvah þei bidjaiþ attan in namin meinamma, gibiþ izwis.
John 15 17 [CA] þata anabiuda izwis ei frijoþ izwis misso.
John 15 18 [CA] jabai so manaseds izwis fijai, kunneiþ ei mik fruman izwis fijaida.
John 15 19 [CA] jabai þis fairhvaus weseiþ, aiþþau so manaseds swesans frijodedi; aþþan unte us þamma fairhvau ni sijuþ, ak ik gawalida izwis us þamma fairhvau, duþþe fijaid izwis so manaseþs.
John 15 20 [CA] gamuneiþ þis waurdis þatei ik qaþ du izwis: nist skalks maiza fraujin seinamma. jabai mik wrekun, jah izwis wrikand; jabai mein waurd fastaidedeina, jah izwar fastaina.
John 15 21 [CA] ak þata allata taujand izwis in namins meinis, unte ni kunnun þana sandjandan mik.
John 15 22 [CA] nih qemjau jah rodidedjau du im, frawaurht ni habaidedeina: iþ nu inilons ni haband bi frawaurht seina.
John 15 23 [CA] saei mik fijaiþ, jah attan meinana fijaiþ.
John 15 24 [CA] iþ þo waurstwa ni gatawidedjau in im þoei anþar ainshun ni gatawida, frawaurht ni habaidedeina; iþ nu jah gasehvun mik jah fijaidedun jah mik jah attan meinana.
John 15 25 [CA] ak ei usfullnodedi waurd þata gamelido in witoda ize: ei fijaidedun mik arwjo.
John 15 26 [CA] aþþan þan qimiþ parakletus þanei ik insandja izwis fram attin, ahman sunjos izei fram attin urrinniþ, sa weitwodeiþ bi mik.
John 15 27 [CA] jah þan jus weitwodeiþ, unte fram fruma miþ mis sijuþ.
John 16 1 [CA] Þata rodida izwis, ei ni afmarzjaindau.
John 16 2 [CA] us gaqumþim dreiband izwis; akei qimiþ hveila, ei sahvazuh izei usqimiþ izwis, þuggkeiþ hunsla saljan guda.
John 16 3 [CA] jah þata taujand, unte ni ufkunþedun attan nih mik.
John 16 4 [CA] akei þata rodida izwis, ei biþe qimai so hveila ize, gamuneiþ þize þatei ik qaþ izwis. iþ þata izwis fram fruma ni qaþ, unte miþ izwis was.
John 16 5 [CA] Iþ nu gagga du þamma sandjandin mik, jah ainshun us izwis ni fraihniþ mik: hvaþ gaggis?
John 16 6 [CA] akei unte þata rodida izwis, gauriþa gadaubida izwar hairto.
John 16 7 [CA] akei ik sunja izwis qiþa: batizo ist izwis ei ik galeiþau; unte jabai ik ni galeiþa, parakletus ni qimiþ at izwis; aþþan jabai gagga, sandja ina du izwis.
John 16 8 [CA] jah qimands is gasakiþ þo manaseþ bi frawaurht jah bi garaihtiþa jah bi staua;
John 16 9 [CA] bi frawaurht raihtis, [þata] þatei ni galaubjand du mis;
John 16 10 [CA] iþ bi garaihtiþa, þatei du attin meinamma gagga, jah ni þanaseiþs saihviþ mik;
John 16 11 [CA] iþ bi staua, þatei sa reiks þis fairhvaus afdomiþs warþ.
John 16 12 [CA] Nauh ganoh skal qiþan izwis, akei ni maguþ frabairan nu.
John 16 13 [CA] iþ þan qimiþ jains, ahma sunjos, briggiþ izwis in allai sunjai; nih þan rodeiþ af sis silbin ak swa filu swe hauseiþ rodeiþ, jah þata anawairþo gateihiþ izwis.
John 16 14 [CA] jains mik hauheiþ, unte us meinamma nimiþ jah gateihiþ izwis.
John 16 15 [CA] all þatei aih atta, mein ist; duhþe qaþ þatei us meinamma nimiþ jah gateihiþ izwis.
John 16 16 [CA] Leitil nauh jah ni saihviþ mik; jah aftra leitil jah gasaihviþ mik, unte ik gagga du attin.
John 16 17 [CA] þaruh qeþun us þaim siponjam <is> du sis misso: hva ist þata þatei qiþiþ unsis: leitil ei ni saihviþ mik, jah aftra leitil jah gasaihviþ mik, jah þatei ik gagga du attin?
John 16 18 [CA] qeþunuh: þata hva sijai þatei qiþiþ: leitil, ni witum hva qiþiþ.
John 16 19 [CA] iþ Iesus wissuh þatei wildedun ina fraihnan jah qaþ im: bi þata sokeiþ miþ izwis misso þatei qaþ: leitil jah ni saihviþ mik, jah aftra leitil jah gasaihviþ mik.
John 16 20 [CA] amen, amen, qiþa izwis þei greitiþ jah gaunoþ jus, iþ manaseþs faginoþ; jus saurgandans wairþiþ, akei so saurga izwara du fahedai wairþiþ.
John 16 21 [CA] qino, þan bairiþ, saurga habaid, unte qam hveila izos; iþ biþe gabauran ist barn, ni þanaseiþs ni gaman þizos aglons faura fahedai, unte gabaurans warþ manna in fairhvau.
John 16 22 [CA] jah þan jus auk nu saurga habaiþ, iþ aftra saihva izwis jah faginoþ izwar hairto, jah þo fahed izwara ni ainshun nimiþ af izwis.
John 16 23 [CA] jah in jainamma daga mik ni fraihniþ waihtais. amen amen, qiþa izwis þatei þishvah þei bidjiþ attan in namin meinamma, gibiþ izwis.
John 16 24 [CA] und hita ni beduþ ni waihtais in namin meinamma; bidjaiþ jah nimiþ, ei faheþs izwara sijai usfullida.
John 16 25 [CA] þata in gajukom rodida izwis; akei qimiþ hveila, þanuh izwis ni þanaseiþs in gajukom rodja, ak andaugiba bi attan gateiha izwis.
John 16 26 [CA] in jainamma daga in namin meinamma bidjiþ, jah ni qiþa izwis þei ik bidjau attan bi izwis;
John 16 27 [CA] ak silba atta frijoþ izwis, unte jus mik frijodeduþ jah galaubideduþ þatei ik fram guda urrann.
John 16 28 [CA] uzuhiddja fram attin jah atiddja in þana fairhvu; aftra bileiþa þamma fairhvau jah gagga du attin.
John 16 29 [CA] þaruh qeþun þai siponjos is: sai, nu andaugiba rodeis jah gajukono ni ainohun qiþis.
John 16 30 [CA] nu witum ei þu kant alla, jah ni þarft ei þuk hvas fraihnai; bi þamma galaubjam þatei þu fram guda urrant.
John 16 31 [CA] andhof im Iesus: nu galaubeiþ?
John 16 32 [CA] sai, qimiþ hveila jah nu qam, ei distahjada hvarjizuh du seinaim, jah mik ainana bileiþiþ; jah ni im ains, unte atta miþ mis ist.
John 16 33 [CA] þata rodida izwis, þei in mis gawairþi aigeiþ. in þamma fairhvau aglons habaid; akei þrafsteiþ izwis, ik gajiukaida þana fairhvu.
John 17 1 [CA] Þata rodida Iesus uzuhhof augona seina du himina jah qaþ: atta, qam hveila, hauhei þeinana sunu, ei sunus þeins hauhjai þuk;
John 17 2 [CA] swaswe atgaft imma waldufni allaize leike, ei all þatei atgaft imma, gibai im libain aiweinon.
John 17 3 [CA] soh þan ist so aiweino libains, ei kunneina þuk ainana sunjana guþ jah þanei insandides, Iesu Xristu.
John 17 4 [CA] ik þuk hauhida ana airþai; waurstw ustauh þatei atgaft mis du waurkjan.
John 17 5 [CA] jah nu hauhei mik, þu atta, at þus silbin þamma wulþau, þanei habaida at þus, faurþizei sa fairhvus wesi.
John 17 6 [CA] gabairhtida þeinata namo mannam þanzei atgaft mis us þamma fairhvau. þeinai wesun jah mis atgaft ins, jah þata waurd þeinata gafastaidedun.
John 17 7 [CA] nu ufkunþa ei alla þoei atgaft mis, at þus sind;
John 17 8 [CA] unte þo waurda þoei atgaft mis, atgaf im, jah eis nemun bi sunjai þatei fram þus urrann, jah galaubidedun þatei þu mik insandides.
John 17 9 [CA] ik bi ins bidja; ni bi þo manaseþ bidja, ak bi þans þanzei atgaft mis, unte þeinai sind.
John 17 10 [CA] jah meina alla þeina sind jah þeina meina, jah hauhiþs im in þaim.
John 17 11 [CA] ni þanaseiþs im in þamma fairhvau; iþ þai in þamma fairhvau sind, jah ik du þus gagga. atta weiha, fastai ins in namin þeinamma, þanzei atgaft mis, ei sijaina ain swaswe wit.
John 17 12 [CA] þan was miþ im in þamma fairhvau, ik fastaida ins in namin þeinamma. þanzei atgaft mis gafastaida, jah ainshun us im ni fraqistnoda, niba sa sunus fralustais, ei þata gamelido usfulliþ waurþi.
John 17 13 [CA] iþ nu du þus gagga, jah þata rodja in manasedai, ei habaina fahed meina usfullida in sis.
John 17 14 [CA] ik atgaf im waurd þeinata; jah so manaseþs fijaida ins, unte ni sind us þamma fairhvau, swaswe ik us þamma fairhvau ni im.
John 17 15 [CA] ni bidja ei usnimais ins us þamma fairhvau, ak ei bairgais im faura þamma unseljin.
John 17 16 [CA] us þamma fairhvau ni sind, swaswe ik us þamma fairhvau ni im.
John 17 17 [CA] weihai ins in sunjai; waurd þeinata sunja ist.
John 17 18 [CA] swaswe mik insandides in manaseþ, swah ik insandida ins in þo manased.
John 17 19 [CA] jah fram im ik weiha mik silban, ei sijaina jah eis weihai in sunjai.
John 17 20 [CA] aþþan ni bi þans bidja ainans, ak <jah> bi þans galaubjandans þairh waurda ize du mis,
John 17 21 [CA] ei allai ain sijaina, swaswe þu, atta, in mis jah ik in þus, ei jah þai in uggkis ain sijaina, ei so manaseþs galaubjai þatei þu mik insandides.
John 17 22 [CA] jah ik wulþu þanei gaft mis, gaf im, ei sijaina ain, swaswe wit ain siju.
John 17 23 [CA] ik in im jah þu in mis, ei sijaina ustauhanai du ainamma, jah kunnei so manaseþs þatei þu mik insandides jah frijodes ins, swaswe mik frijodes.
John 17 24 [CA] atta, þatei atgaft mis, wiljau ei þarei im ik, jah þai sijaina miþ mis, ei saihvaina wulþu meinana þanei gaft mis, unte frijodes mik faur gaskaft fairhvaus.
John 17 25 [CA] atta garaihta, jah so manaseþs þuk ni ufkunþa; iþ ik þuk kunþa. jah þai ufkunþedun þatei þu mik insandides.
John 17 26 [CA] jah gakannida im namo þeinata jah kannja, ei friaþwa þoei frijodes mik, in im sijai jah ik in im.
John 18 1 [CA] Þata qiþands Iesus usiddja miþ siponjam seinaim ufar rinnon þo Kaidron, þarei was aurtigards, in þanei galaiþ Iesus jah siponjos is.
John 18 2 [CA] wissuh þan jah Iudas sa galewjands ina þana stad, þatei ufta gaïddja Iesus jainar miþ siponjam seinaim.
John 18 3 [CA] iþ Iudas nam hansa jah þize gudjane jah Fareisaie andbahtans, iddjuh jaindwairþs miþ skeimam jah haizam jah wepnam.
John 18 4 [CA] iþ Iesus witands alla þoei qemun ana ina, usgaggands ut qaþ im: hvana sokeiþ?
John 18 5 [CA] andhafjandans imma qeþun: Iesu, þana Nazoraiu. þaruh qaþ im Iesus: ik im. stoþuh þan jah Iudas sa lewjands ina miþ im.
John 18 6 [CA] þaruh swe qaþ im þatei ik im, galiþun ibukai jah gadrusun dalaþ.
John 18 7 [CA] þaþroh þan ins aftra frah: hvana sokeiþ? iþ eis qeþun: Iesu, þana Nazoraiu.
John 18 8 [CA] andhof Iesus: qaþ izwis þatei ik im; jabai nu mik sokeiþ, letiþ þans gaggan.
John 18 9 [CA] ei usfullnodedi þata waurd þatei qaþ, ei þanzei atgaft mis, ni fraqistida ize ainummehun.
John 18 10 [CA] iþ Seimon Paitrus habands hairu, uslauk ina jah sloh þis auhumistins gudjins skalk jah afmaimait imma auso taihswo; sah þan haitans was namin Malkus.
John 18 11 [CA] þaruh qaþ Iesus du Paitrau: lagei þana hairu in fodr. stikl þanei gaf mis atta, niu drigkau þana?
John 18 12 [CA] þaruh hansa jah sa þusundifaþs jah andbahtos Iudaie undgripun Iesu jah gabundun ina,
John 18 13 [CA] jah gatauhun ina du Annin frumist; sa was auk swaihra Kajafin, saei was auhumists weiha þis ataþnjis.
John 18 14 [CA] wasuh þan Kajafa, saei garaginoda Iudaium þatei batizo ist ainana mannan fraqistjan faur managein.
John 18 15 [CA] þaruh laistida Iesu Seimon Paitrus jah anþar siponeis. sah þan siponeis was kunþs þamma gudjin jah miþinngalaiþ miþ Iesua in rohsn þis gudjins.
John 18 16 [CA] iþ Paitrus stoþ at daurom uta. þaruh usiddja ut sa siponeis anþar, saei was kunþs þamma gudjin, jah qaþ daurawardai jah attauh inn Paitru.
John 18 17 [CA] þaruh qaþ jaina þiwi, so daurawardo, du Paitrau: ibai jah þu þize siponje is þis mans? iþ is qaþ: ni im.
John 18 18 [CA] þaruh stoþun skalkos jah andbahtos haurja waurkjandans, unte kald was, jah warmidedun sik; jah þan was miþ im Paitrus standands jah warmjands sik.
John 18 19 [CA] iþ sa auhumista gudja frah Iesu bi siponjans is jah bi laisein is.
John 18 20 [CA] andhof imma Iesus: ik andaugjo rodida manasedai; ik sinteino laisida in gaqumþai jah in gudhusa, þarei sinteino Iudaieis gaqimand, jah þiubjo ni rodida waiht.
John 18 21 [CA] hvis mik fraihnis? fraihn þans hausjandans hva rodidedjau du im; sai, þai witun þatei qaþ ik.
John 18 22 [CA] iþ þata qiþandin imma, sums andbahte <at>standands gaf slah lofin Iesua qaþuh: swau andhafjis þamma reikistin gudjin?
John 18 23 [CA] andhof <imma> Iesus: jabai ubilaba rodida, weitwodei bi þata ubil, aiþþau jabai waila, duhve mik slahis?
John 18 24 [CA] þanuh insandida ina Annas gabundanana du Kajafin, þamma maistin gudjin.
John 18 25 [CA] iþ Seimon Paitrus was standands jah warmjands sik. þaruh qeþun du imma: niu jah þu þize siponje þis is? iþ is afaiaik jah qaþ: ne, ni im.
John 18 26 [CA] qaþ sums þize skalke þis maistins gudjins, sah niþjis was þammei afmaimait Paitrus auso: niu þuk sahv ik in aurtigarda miþ imma?
John 18 27 [CA] þaruh aftra afaiaik Paitrus, jah suns hana hrukida.
John 18 28 [CA] iþ eis tauhun Iesu fram Kajafin in praitoriaun. þanuh was maurgins. iþ eis ni iddjedun in praitoria<un>, ei ni bisaulnodedeina, ak matidedeina pasxa.
John 18 29 [CA] þaruh atiddja ut Peilatus du im jah qaþ: hvo wrohe bairiþ ana þana mannan?
John 18 30 [CA] andhofun jah qeþun du imma: nih wesi sa ubiltojis, ni þau weis atgebeima þus ina.
John 18 31 [CA] þaruh qaþ im Peilatus: nimiþ ina jus jah bi witoda izwaramma stojiþ ina. iþ eis qeþunuh du imma Iudaieis: unsis ni skuld ist usqiman manne ainummehun.
John 18 32 [CA] ei waurd fraujins usfullnodedi, þatei qaþ, bandwjands hvileikamma dauþau skulda gaswiltan.
John 18 33 [CA] <þaruh> galaiþ in praitauria aftra Peilatus jah wopida Iesu qaþuh imma: þu is þiudans Iudaie?
John 18 34 [CA] andhof Iesus: abu þus silbin þu þata qiþis þau anþarai þus qeþun bi mik?
John 18 35 [CA] andhof Peilatus: waitei ik Iudaius im? so þiuda þeina jah gudjans anafulhun þuk mis; hva gatawides?
John 18 36 [CA] andhof Iesus: þiudangardi meina nist us þamma fairhvau; iþ us þamma fairhvau wesi meina þiudangardi, aiþþau andbahtos meinai usdaudidedeina, ei ni galewiþs wesjau Iudaium. iþ nu þiudangardi meina nist þaþro.
John 18 37 [CA] þaruh qaþ imma Peilatus: an nuh þiudans is þu? andhafjands Iesus <qaþ>: þu qiþis ei þiudans im ik. ik du þamma gabaurans im jah du þamma qam in þamma fairhvau ei weitwodjau sunjai. hvazuh saei ist sunjos, hauseiþ stibnos meinaizos.
John 18 38 [CA] þanuh qaþ imma Peilatus: hva ist so sunja! jah þata qiþands <aftra> galaiþ ut du Iudaium jah qaþ im: ik ainohun fairino ni bigita in þamma.
John 18 39 [CA] iþ ist biuhti izwis ei ainana izwis fraletau in pasxa; wileidu nu ei fraletau izwis þana þiudan Iudaie?
John 18 40 [CA] iþ eis hropidedun aftra allai qiþandans: ne þana, ak Barabban; sah þan was sa Barabba waidedja.
John 19 1 [CA] Þanuh þan nam Peilatus Iesu jah usblaggw.
John 19 2 [CA] jah þai gadrauhteis uswundun wipja us þaurnum jah galagidedun imma ana haubid jah wastjai paurpurodai gawasidedun ina,
John 19 3 [CA] jah qeþun: hails þiudans Iudaie! jah gebun imma slahins lofin.
John 19 4 [CA] atiddja aftra ut Peilatus jah qaþ im: sai, attiuha izwis ina ut, ei witeiþ þatei in imma ni ainohun fairino bigat.
John 19 5 [CA] þaruh usiddja ut Iesus bairands þana þaurneinan waip jah þo paurpurodon wastja. jah qaþ im: <sai> sa ist sa manna.
John 19 6 [CA] þaruh biþe sehvun ina þai maistans gudjans jah andbahtos, hropidedun qiþandans: ushramei, ushramei ina! qaþ im Peilatus: nimiþ ina jus jah hramjiþ. iþ ik fairina in imma ni bigita.
John 19 7 [CA] andhofun imma Iudaieis: weis witoþ aihum, jah bi þamma witoda unsaramma skal gaswiltan, unte sik silban gudis sunu gatawida.
John 19 8 [CA] biþe gahausida Peilatus þata waurd, mais ohta sis.
John 19 9 [CA] jah galaiþ in praitauria<un> aftra jah qaþ du Iesua: hvaþro is þu? iþ Iesus andawaurdi ni gaf imma.
John 19 10 [CA] þaruh qaþ imma Peilatus: du mis ni rodeis? niu waist þatei waldufni aih ushramjan þuk jah waldufni aih fraletan þuk?
John 19 11 [CA] andhof Iesus: ni aihtedeis waldufnje ainhun ana mik, nih wesi þus atgiban iupaþro; duhþe sa galewjands mik þus maizein frawaurht habaid.
John 19 12 [CA] Framuh þamma sokida Peilatus fraletan ina. iþ Iudaieis hropidedun qiþandans: jabai þana fraletis, ni is frijonds kaisara; sahvazuh izei þiudan sik silban taujiþ, andstandiþ kaisara.

Romans 6 23 [A] þo auk launa frawaurhtais dauþus; iþ ansts gudis libains aiweino in Xristau Iesu, fraujin unsaramma.
Romans 7 1 [A] Þau niu wituþ, broþrjus kunnandam auk witoþ rodja, þatei witoþ fraujinoþ mann, s<wa> lagga hveila swe libaiþ?
Romans 7 2 [A] jah auk ufwaira qens at libandin abin gabundana ist witoda; aþþan jabai gaswiltiþ aba, galausjada af þamma witoda abins.
Romans 7 3 [A] þannu þan at libandin abin haitada horinondei, jabai wairþiþ waira anþaramma; (iþ) jabai gaswiltiþ wair, frija ist þis witodis, ei ni sijai horinondei waurþana abin anþaramma.
Romans 7 4 [A] swaei nu jah jus, broþrjus meinai, afdauþidai waurþuþ witoda þairh leik Xristaus, ei wairþaiþ anþaramma, þamma us dauþaim urreisandin, ei akran bairaima guda.
Romans 7 5 [A] þan auk wesum in leika, winnons frawaurhti þos þairh witoþ waurhtedun in liþum unsaraim du akran bairan dauþau;
Romans 7 6 [A] iþ nu, sai, andbundanai waurþum af witoda, gadauþnandans in þammei gahabaidai wesum, swaei skalkinoma in niujiþai ahmins jah ni fairniþai bokos.
Romans 7 7 [A] hva nu qiþam? witoþ frawaurhts ist? nis~sijai! ak frawaurht ni ufkunþedjau nih þairh witoþ, unte lustu nih wissedjau, nih witoþ qeþi: ni gairnjais.
Romans 7 8 [A] iþ lew nimandei frawaurhts þairh anabusn gawaurhta in mis allana lustu; unte inu witoþ frawaurhts was nawis.
Romans 7 9 [A] iþ ik qius <was> inu witoþ siml(e), iþ qimandein anabusnai frawaurhts gaqiunoda;
Romans 7 10 [A] iþ ik gadauþ(noda), jah bigitana warþ mis anabusns, sei was du libainai, wisan du dauþau.
Romans 7 11 [A] unte frawaurhts lew nimandei þairh anabusn uslutoda mik, jah þairh þo usqam.
Romans 7 12 [A] aþþan nu sweþauh witoþ weihata jah anabusns weiha jah garaihta jah þiuþeiga.
Romans 7 13 [A] þata nu þiuþeigo warþ mis dauþus? nis~sijai! ak frawaurhts ei uskunþa waurþi frawaurhts, þairh þata þiuþeigo mis gawaurkjandei dauþu, ei waurþi ufarassau frawaurhta frawaurhts þairh anabusn.
Romans 7 14 [A] witum auk þatei witoþ ahmein ist; iþ ik leikeins im, frabauhts uf frawaurht.
Romans 7 15 [A] þatei waurkja, ni fraþja; unte ni þatei wiljau tauja, ak þatei fija þata tauja.
Romans 7 16 [A] iþ jabai þatei ni wiljau þata tauja, gaqiss im witoda þatei goþ.
Romans 7 17 [A] iþ nu ju ni ik waurkja þata, ak so bauandei in mis frawaurhts.
Romans 7 18 [A] wait auk þatei ni bauiþ in mis, þat~ist in leika meinamma, þiuþ; unte wiljan atligiþ mis, iþ gawaurkjan goþ ni.
Romans 7 19 [A] unte ni þatei wiljau waurkja goþ, ak þatei ni wiljau ubil <þata> tauja.
Romans 7 20 [A] jabai nu þatei ni wiljau ik þata tauja, ju ni ik waurkja ita, ak sei bauiþ in mis frawaurhts.
Romans 7 21 [A] bigita nu witoþ, wiljandin mis goþ taujan, unte mis atist ubil.
Romans 7 22 [A] gawizneigs im auk witoda gudis bi þamma innumin mann;
Romans 7 23 [A] aþþan gasaihva anþar witoþ in liþum meinaim, andwaihando witoda ahmins meinis jah frahinþando mik in witoda frawaurhtais þamma wisandin in liþum meinaim.
Romans 7 24 [A] waina(h)s ik manna! hvas mik lauseiþ us þamma leika dauþaus þis?
Romans 7 25 [A] awiliudo guda þairh Iesu Xristu, fraujan unsarana; jau nu silba i(k) skalkino gahugdai witoda gudis, iþ leika witoda frawaurhtais.
Romans 8 1 [A] Ni waiht þannu nu wargiþos þaim in Xristau Iesu ni gaggandam bi leika.
Romans 8 2 [A] unte witoþ ahmins libainais in Xristau Iesu frijana brahta mik witodis frawaurhtais jah dauþaus.
Romans 8 3 [A] unte þata unmahteigo witodis, in þammei siuks was þairh leik, guþ seinana sunu insandjands in galeikja leikis frawaurhtais jah bi frawaurht gawargida frawaurht in leika,
Romans 8 4 [A] ei garaihtei witodis usfulljaidau in uns þaim ni bi leika gaggandam, ak bi ahmin.
Romans 8 5 [A] unte þai bi leika wisandans þo þoei leikis sind, mitond; iþ þai bi ahmin þo þoei ahmins.
Romans 8 6 [A] aþþan fraþi leikis dauþus, iþ fraþi ahmins libains jah gawairþi;
Romans 8 7 [A] unte fraþi leikis fijands du guda; witoda gudis ni ufhauseiþ, iþ ni mag:
Romans 8 8 [A] aþþan þai in leika wisandans guda galeikan ni magun.
Romans 8 9 [A] iþ jus ni sijuþ in leika, ak in ahmin, sweþauh jabai ahma gudis bauiþ in izwis. iþ jabai hvas ahman Xristaus ni habaiþ, sa nist is.
Romans 8 10 [A] jabai auk Xristus in izwis, leik raihtis . . . .

1 Corinthians 1 12 [A] . . . . ik im Pawlus, iþ ik Apaullons, iþ ik Kefins, iþ ik Xristaus.
1 Corinthians 1 13 [A] disdailiþs ist Xristus? ibai Pawlus ushramiþs warþ in izwara, aiþþau in namin Pawlus daupidai weseiþ?
1 Corinthians 1 14 [A] awiliudo guda ei ainnohun izwara ni daupida niba Krispu jah Gaïu,
1 Corinthians 1 15 [A] ei hvas ni qiþai þatei in meinamma namin daupidedjau.
1 Corinthians 1 16 [A] ik daupida auk jaþ~þans Staifanaus gadaukans; þata anþar ni wait ei ainnohun daupidedjau.
1 Corinthians 1 17 [A] niþ~þan insandida mik Xristus daupjan, ak wailamerjan; ni in snutrein waurdis, ei ni <us>lausjaidau galga Xristaus.
1 Corinthians 1 18 [A] unte þata waurd galgins þaim fralusnandam dwaliþa ist, iþ þaim ganisandam mahts gudis ist.
1 Corinthians 1 19 [A] gameliþ ist auk: fraqistja snutrein þize snutrane jah frodein þize frodane uskiusa.
1 Corinthians 1 20 [A] hvar handugs? hvar bokareis? hvar sokareis þis aiwis? nih dwala gatawida guþ handugein þis fairhvaus?
1 Corinthians 1 21 [A] unte auk in handugein gudis ni ufkunnaida sa fairhvus þairh handugein guþ, galeikaida guda þairh þo dwaliþa þizos wailamereinais ganasjan þans galaubjandans.
1 Corinthians 1 22 [A] unte Iudaieis taikne bidjand, iþ Krekos handugein sokjand;
1 Corinthians 1 23 [A] iþ weis merjam Iesu ushramidana, Iudaium gamarzein, iþ þiudom dwaliþa;
1 Corinthians 1 24 [A] iþ þaim galaþodam Iudaie jah þiudo Xristu, gudis maht jah gudis handugein.
1 Corinthians 1 25 [A] unte so dwaliþa gudis handugo(ze)i mannam . . . .

1 Corinthians 4 2 [A] . . . . ei hvas triggws bigitaidau.
1 Corinthians 4 3 [A] aþþan mis in minnistin ist, ei fram izwis ussokjaidau aiþþau fram manniskamma daga; akei nih mik silban ussokja.
1 Corinthians 4 4 [A] nih waiht auk mis silbin miþwait; akei ni in þamma garaihtiþs im, iþ saei ussokeiþ mik, frauja ist.
1 Corinthians 4 5 [A] þannu nu ei faur mel ni stojaiþ, unte qimai frauja, saei jah galiuhteiþ analaugn riqizis jah gabairhteiþ runos hairtane; jaþ~þan hazeins wairþiþ hvarjammeh fram guda.
1 Corinthians 4 6 [A] aþþan <þo>, broþrjus, þairhgaleiko[n]da in mis jah Apaullon in izwara, ei in ugkis ganimaiþ ni ufar þatei gameliþ ist fraþjan, ei ains faur ainana ana anþarana ufblesans ni sijai.
1 Corinthians 4 7 [A] hvas auk þuk ussokeiþ? hvauþ~þan habais þatei ni namt? aiþþau jabai andnamt, hva hvopis swe ni nemeis?
1 Corinthians 4 8 [A] ju sadai sijuþ, ju gabigai waurþuþ, inu uns þiudanodeduþ; jah wainei þiudanodedeiþ, ei jah weis izwis miþþiudanoma.
1 Corinthians 4 9 [A] man auk þei guþ uns apaustauluns spedistans ustaiknida, swaswe dauþubljans, unte fairweitl waurþum þizai manasedai jah aggilum jah mannam.
1 Corinthians 4 10 [A] weis dwalai in Xristaus, iþ jus frodai in Xristau; weizuþ~þan unmahteigai, iþ jus swinþai; juzuþ~þan wulþagai, iþ weis unswerai.
1 Corinthians 4 11 [A] und þo nu hveila jah huggridai jah þaursidai jah naqadai jah kaupatidai jah ungastoþai.

1 Corinthians 5 3 [A] . . . . ju gastauida swe andwairþs þana swa þata gataujandan,
1 Corinthians 5 4 [A] in namin fraujins unsaris Iesuis Xristaus, samaþ gagaggandam izwis jah meinamma ahmin, miþ mahtai fraujins unsaris Iesuis Xristaus,
1 Corinthians 5 5 [A] atgiban þana swaleikana unhulþin du qisteinai leikis, ei ahma ganisai in daga fraujins Iesuis.
1 Corinthians 5 6 [A] ni goda so hvoftuli izwara; niu wituþ þatei leitil beistis allana daig gabeisteiþ?
1 Corinthians 5 7 [A] ushraineiþ þata fairnjo beist, ei sijaiþ niujis daigs, swaswe sijaiþ unbeistjodai; jah auk paska unsara ufsniþans ist faur uns Xristus.
1 Corinthians 5 8 [A] þannu dulþjam ni in beista fairnjamma niþ~þan in beista balwaweseins jah unseleins, ak in unbeistein unwammeins jas~sunjos.
1 Corinthians 5 9 [A] gamelida izwis ana þizai aipistaulein: ni blandaiþ izwis horam,
1 Corinthians 5 10 [A] ni þaim horam þis fairhvaus, aiþþau [jabai] þaim faihufrikam jah wilwam aiþþau galiugam skalkinondam, unte skuldedeiþ þan us þamma fairhvau usgaggan.
1 Corinthians 5 11 [A] iþ nu gamelida izwis ni blandan, jabai hvas broþar namnids sijai hors aiþþau faihufriks aiþþau galiugam skalkinonds aiþþau ubilwaurds aiþþau afdrugkja aiþþau wilwa, þamma swaleikamma ni miþmatjan.
1 Corinthians 5 12 [A] hva mik jah þans uta stojan? niu þans inna jus stojiþ?
1 Corinthians 5 13 [A] iþ þans uta guþ stojiþ. usnimiþ þana ubilan us izwis silbam.

1 Corinthians 7 5 [A] . . . . izwara misso, niba þau us gaqissai hvo hveilo, ei uhteigai sijaiþ fastan jah bidan; þaþroþ~þan samaþ gawandjaiþ, ei ni fraisai izwara Satana in ungahobainais izwaraizos.
1 Corinthians 7 6 [A] þatuþ~þan qiþa gakunnands, ni bi haitjai.
1 Corinthians 7 7 [A] iþ wiljau allans mans wisan swe mik silban; akei hvarjizuh swesa giba habaiþ fram guda, sums swa, sumsuh swa.
1 Corinthians 7 8 [A] aþþan qiþa þaim unqenidam jah widuwom: goþ ist im, jabai sind swe ik.
1 Corinthians 7 9 [A] iþ jabai ni gahabaina sik, liugandau; batizo ist auk liugan þau intundnan.
1 Corinthians 7 10 [A] iþ þaim liugom haftam anabiuda, ni ik, ak frauja, qenai fairra abin ni skaidan.
1 Corinthians 7 11 [A] iþ jabai gaskaidnai, wisan unliugaida[i], aiþþau du abin seinamma aftra gagawairþjan, jah aban qen ni fraletan.
1 Corinthians 7 12 [A] iþ þaim anþaraim ik qiþa, ni frauja: jabai hvas broþar qen aigi ungalaubjandein, jah so gawilja ist bauan miþ imma, ni afletai þo qen;
1 Corinthians 7 13 [A] jah qens soei aigi aban ungalaubjandan, jah sa gawilja ist bauan miþ izai, ni afletai þana aban.
1 Corinthians 7 14 [A] weihaida ist qens so ungalaubjandei in abin, jah gaweihaids ist aba sa ungalaubjands in qenai; aiþþau barna izwara unhrainja weseina, iþ nu weiha sind.
1 Corinthians 7 15 [A] iþ jabai sa ungalaubjands skaidiþ sik, skaidai; nist gaþiwaids broþar aiþþau swistar in þaim swaleikaim; aþþan in gawairþja laþoda uns guþ.
1 Corinthians 7 16 [A] hva nuk~kannt þu, qino[n], ei aban ganasjais? aiþþau hva kannt, guma, þatei qen þeina ganasjais?
1 Corinthians 7 17 [A] ni ei, hvarjammeh swaswe gadailida guþ, ainhvarjatoh swaswe galaþoda guþ, swa gaggai; jah swa in allaim aikklesjom anabiuda.
1 Corinthians 7 18 [A] bimaitans galaþoda warþ hvas, ni ufrakjai; miþ faurafillja galaþoþs warþ hvas, ni bimaitai.
1 Corinthians 7 19 [A] þata bimait ni waihts ist jah þata faurafilli ni waihts ist, ak fastubnja anabusne gudis.
1 Corinthians 7 20 [A] hvarjizuh in laþonai þizaiei laþoþs was, in þizai sijai.
1 Corinthians 7 21 [A] skalks galaþoþs wast, ni karos; akei þauhjabai magt freis wairþan, mais brukei.
1 Corinthians 7 22 [A] saei auk in fraujin haitans ist skalks, fralets fraujins ist; samaleiko saei freis haitada, skalks ist Xristaus.
1 Corinthians 7 23 [A] wairþa galaubamma usbauhtai sijuþ; ni wairþaiþ skalkos mannam.
1 Corinthians 7 24 [A] hvarjizuh in þammei atlaþoþs was, broþrjus, in þamma gastandai at guda.
1 Corinthians 7 25 [A] aþþan bi maujos anabusn fraujins ni haba; iþ ragin giba swe gaarmaiþs fram fraujin du triggws wisan.
1 Corinthians 7 26 [A] man nu þata goþ wisan in þizos andwairþons þaurftais, þatei goþ ist mann swa wisan:
1 Corinthians 7 27 [A] gabundans is qenai, ni sokei lausjan; galausiþs is qenai, ni sokei qen.
1 Corinthians 7 28 [A] aþþan jabai nimis qen, ni frawaurhtes, jah jabai liugada mawi, ni frawaurhta, iþ aglon leikis gastaldand þo swaleika. iþ ik izwis freidja . . . .

1 Corinthians 8 9 [A] . . . . wairþai þaim unmahteigam.
1 Corinthians 8 10 [A] jabai auk hvas gasaihviþ þuk þana habandan kunþi in galiuge stada anakumbjandan, niu miþwissei is siukis wisandins timrjada du galiugagudam gasaliþ matjan?

1 Corinthians 9 19 [A] . . . . ei managizans gageigaidedjau.
1 Corinthians 9 20 [A] jah warþ Iudaium swe Judaius, ei Judaiuns gageigaid<edj>au; þaim uf witoda swe uf witoda, ni wisands silba uf witoda, ak uf anstai, ei þans uf witoda gageig[g]aidedjau;
1 Corinthians 9 21 [A] þaim witodalausam swe witodalaus, ni wisands witodis laus gudis, ak inwitoþ<s> Xristaus, ei gageig[g]<aidedj>au witodalausans.
1 Corinthians 9 22 [A] was þaim unmahteigam swe unmahteigs, ei unmahteigans gageig[g]aidedjau; allaim was all, ei hvaiwa sumans ganasjau.
1 Corinthians 9 23 [A] þatuþ~þan tauja in aiwaggeljis, ei gadaila is wairþau.

1 Corinthians 9 25 [A] iþ hvazuh saei haifstjan sniwiþ, allis sik gaþarb<a>iþ; aþþan eis, ei riurjana waip nimaina, iþ weis unriurjana.

1 Corinthians 10 15 [A] . . . . (fro)daim qiþa; domeiþ jus þatei qiþa.
1 Corinthians 10 16 [A] stikls þiuþiqissais þanei gaweiham, niu gamainduþs bloþis fraujins ist? hlaifs þanei brikam, niu gamainduþs leikis fraujins ist?
1 Corinthians 10 17 [A] unte ains hlaifs, ain leik þai managans sium, þaiei auk allai ainis hlaibis jah ainis stiklis brukjam.
1 Corinthians 10 18 [A] saihviþ Israel bi leika: niu þai matjandans hunsla gamainjandans hunslastada sind?
1 Corinthians 10 19 [A] hva nu qiþam? þatei þo galiugaguda hva sijaina aiþþau þatei galiugam saljada hva sijai?
1 Corinthians 10 20 [A] [ni þatei þo galiugaguda waihts sijaina,] ak þatei saljand þiudos, skohslam saljand, jan~ni guda. Ni wiljau auk izwis skohslam gadailans wairþan.
1 Corinthians 10 21 [A] ni maguþ stikl fraujins drigkan jah stikl skohsle; ni maguþ biudis fraujins fairaihan jab~biudis skohsle.
1 Corinthians 10 22 [A] þau inaljanom fraujin? ibai swinþozans imma sium?
1 Corinthians 10 23 [A] all binah, akei ni all daug; all mis binauht ist, akei ni all timreiþ.
1 Corinthians 10 24 [A] ni ainshun sein sokjai, ak anþaris hvarjizuh.
1 Corinthians 10 25 [A] all þatei at skiljam frabugjaidau matjaiþ, ni waiht andhruskandans in miþwisseins.
1 Corinthians 10 26 [A] fraujins ist auk airþa jah fullo izos.
1 Corinthians 10 27 [A] iþ jabai hvas laþo izwis þize ungalaubjandane jah wileiþ gaggan, all þatei faurlagjaidau izwis matjaiþ, ni waiht andsitandans bi gahugdai.
1 Corinthians 10 28 [A] iþ jabai hvas qiþai þatei galiugam gasaliþ ist, ni matjaiþ in ja(i)nis þis bandwjandins jah þuhta<us>: fraujins ist auk airþa jah fullo izos;
1 Corinthians 10 29 [A] þuhtuþ~þan qiþa ni silbins, ak anþaris. duhve auk frijei meina stojada þairh ungalaubjandins þuhtu?
1 Corinthians 10 30 [A] jabai ik anstai andnima, duhve anaqiþaidau in þize ik awiliudo?
1 Corinthians 10 31 [A] jaþþe nu matjaiþ jaþþe drigkaiþ jaþþe hva taujiþ, allata du wulþau gudis taujaiþ.

1 Corinthians 10 33 [A] swaswe ik allaim all leika, ni sokjands þatei mis bruk sijai, ak þatei þaim managam, ei ganisaina.

Philippians 4 3 [B] jai jah þuk waliso bidja gajuko, niþais þos þozei miþarbaididedun mis in aiwaggeljon miþ Klemaintau jah anþaraim gawaurstwam meinaim, þizeei namna sind in bokom libainais.
Philippians 4 4 [B] nunu nu faginoþ in fraujin sinteino; aftra qiþa, faginoþ!
Philippians 4 5 [B] anawilje izwara kunþa siai allaim mannam; frauja nehva ist.
Philippians 4 6 [B] ni waihtai maurnaiþ, ak in allai bidai jah aihtronai miþ awiliudam bidos izwaros kunþos sijaina at guda.
Philippians 4 7 [B] jah gawairþi gudis, þatei ufar ist all ahane, fastaiþ hairtona jah leika izwara in Xristau Iesu.
Philippians 4 8 [B] þata anþar, broþrjus, þishvah þatei ist sunjein, þishvah þatei gariud, þishvah þatei garaiht, þishvah þatei weih, þishvah þatei liubaleik, þishvah þatei wailameri, jabai hvo godeino, jabai hvo hazeino, þata mitoþ;
Philippians 4 9 [B] þatei jah galaisideduþ izwis jah ganemuþ jah gahausideduþ jah gasehvuþ in mis, þata taujaiþ, jah guþ gawairþeis sijai miþ izwis.
Philippians 4 10 [B] aþþan faginoda in fraujin mikilaba, unte ju hvan gaþaihuþ du faur mik fraþ(j)an, ana þammei jah froþuþ; aþþan analatidai waurþuþ.
Philippians 4 11 [B] ni þatei bi þarbai qiþau, unte ik galaisida mik in þaimei im ganohiþs wisan.
Philippians 4 12 [B] lais jah haunjan mik, lais jah ufarassu haban; in allamma jah in allaim usþroþiþs im, jah sads wairþan jah gredags, jah ufarassau haban jah þarbos þulan.
Philippians 4 13 [B] all mag in þamma inswinþjandin mik Xristau.
Philippians 4 14 [B] aþþan sweþauh waila gatawideduþ gamainja briggandans meina aglon.
Philippians 4 15 [B] aþþan wituþ jah jus, Filippisius, þatei in anastodeinai aiwaggeljons, þan usiddja af Makidonai, ni ain[n]ohun aikklesjono mis gamainida in raþjon gibos jah andanemis, alja jus ainai.
Philippians 4 16 [B] unte jah in Þaissalauneikai jah ainamma sinþa jah twaim andawizn mis insandideduþ.
Philippians 4 17 [B] ni þatei gasokjau giba, ak gasokja ak(ran) . . . .

Colossians 1 7 [B] swaswe ganemuþ at Aipafrin þamma liubin gaskalkja unsaramma, saei ist triggws faur izwis andbahts Xristaus Iesuis,
Colossians 1 8 [B] saei jah gakannida uns izwara friaþwa in ahmin.
Colossians 1 9 [B] duþþe jah weis, fram þamma daga ei hausidedum, ni hveilaidedum faur izwis bidjandans jah aihtrondans, ei fullnaiþ kunþjis wiljins is in allai handugein jah frodein ahmeinai;
Colossians 1 10 [B] ei gaggaiþ wairþaba fraujins in allamma þatei galeikai, in allamma waurstwe godaize akran bairandans jah wahsjandans in ufkunþja gu(dis),
Colossians 1 11 [B] in allai mahtai gaswinþidai bi mahtai wulþaus is, in allai usþulainai jah usbeisnai miþ fahedai,
Colossians 1 12 [B] awiliudondans attin saei laþoda izwis du dailai hlautis weihaize in liuhada,
Colossians 1 13 [B] saei galausida izwis us waldufnja riqizis jah atnam in þiudangardja sunaus friaþwos seinaizos,
Colossians 1 14 [B] in þammei habam faurbauht, fralet frawaurhte,
Colossians 1 15 [B] saei ist frisahts gudis ungasaihvanis, frumabaur allaizos gaskaftais;
Colossians 1 16 [B] unte in imma gaskapana waurþun alla in himinam jah ana airþai, þo gasaihvanona jah þo ungasaihvanona, jaþþe sitlos jaþþe fraujinassjus, jaþþe reikja jaþþe waldufnja, alla þairh ina jah in imma gaskapana sind.
Colossians 1 17 [B] jah is ist faura allaim jah alla in imma ussatida sind.
Colossians 1 18 [B] jah is ist haubiþ leikis, aikklesjons, saei ist anastodeins, frumabaur us dauþaim, ei sijai in allaim is frumadein habands;
Colossians 1 19 [B] unte in imma galeikaida alla fullon bauan,
Colossians 1 20 [B] jah þairh ina gafriþon alla in imma, gawairþi taujands þairh bloþ galgins is þairh ina, jaþþe þo ana airþai jaþþe þo ana himinam.
Colossians 1 21 [B] jah izwis simle wisandans framaþidans jah fijands gahugdai in waurstwam ubilaim, iþ nu gafriþodai
Colossians 1 22 [B] in leika mammons is þairh dauþu du atsatjan izwis weihans jah unwammans jah usfairinans faura imma,
Colossians 1 23 [B] jabai sweþauh þairhwisiþ in galaubeinai gaþwastidai jah gatulgidai jah ni afwagidai af wenai aiwaggeljons, þoei hausideduþ, sei merida ist in alla gaskaft þo uf himina, þizozei warþ ik Pawlus andbahts;
Colossians 1 24 [B] [saei] nu fagino in þaimei winna faur izwis jah usfullja gai<d>wa aglono Xristaus in leika meinamma faur leik is, þatei ist aikklesjo,
Colossians 1 25 [B] þizozei warþ ik andbahts bi ragina gudis, þatei giban ist mis in izwis du usfulljan waurd gudis,
Colossians 1 26 [B] runa sei gafulgina was fram aiwam jah fram aldim, iþ nu gaswikunþida warþ þaim weiham is,
Colossians 1 27 [B] þaimei wilda guþ gakannjan gabein wulþaus þizos runos in þiudom, þatei ist Xristus in izwis, wens wulþaus,
Colossians 1 28 [B] þanei weis gateiham talzjandans all manne jah laisjandans all manne in allai handugein, ei atsatjaima all manne fullawitan in Xristau Iesu,

Colossians 2 12 [B] miþ ganawistrodai imma in daupeinai, in þizaiei jah miþurrisuþ þairh galaubein waurstwis gudis, saei urraisida in(a) us dauþaim.
Colossians 2 13 [B] jah izwis dauþans wisandans missadedim jah unbimaita leikis izwaris miþgaqiwida miþ imma, fragibands uns allos missadedins,
Colossians 2 14 [B] afswairbands þos ana uns wadjabokos raginam seinaim, þatei was andaneiþo uns, jah þata usnam us midumai ganagljands ita du galgin,
Colossians 2 15 [B] andhamonds sik leika, reikja jah waldufnja gatarhida balþaba, gablauþjands þo bairhtaba in sis.
Colossians 2 16 [B] ni manna nu izwis bidomjai in mata aiþþau in draggka aiþþau in dailai dagis dulþais aiþþau fulliþe aiþþau sabbatum,
Colossians 2 17 [B] þatei ist skadus þize anawairþane, iþ leik Xristaus.
Colossians 2 18 [B] ni hvashun izwis gajiukai, wiljands in hauneinai jah blotinassau aggile þatei ni sahv ushafjands sik, sware ufblesans fram fraþja leikis seinis,
Colossians 2 19 [B] jah ni habands haubiþ, us þammei all leik þairh gawissins jah gabindos auknando jah þeihando wahseiþ du wahstau gudis.
Colossians 2 20 [B] jabai gaswultuþ miþ Xristau af stabim þis fairhvaus, hva þanaseiþs swe qiwai in þamma fairhvau urrediþ?
Colossians 2 21 [B] ni teikais, ni atsnarpjais, ni kausjais!
Colossians 2 22 [B] þatei ist all du riurein, þairh þatei is brukjaidau b(i) anabusnim jah laiseinim manne,
Colossians 2 23 [B] þoei sind sweþa(uh) waurd habandona handug(eins) [(þ)uhtaus] in fastubnja jah hauneinai hairtins jah unfreidei<nai> leikis, ni in sweriþo hvizai du soþa leikis.
Colossians 3 1 [B] Jabai nu miþurrisuþ Xristau, þoei iupa sind sokeiþ, þarei Xristus ist in taihswai gudis sitands.
Colossians 3 2 [B] þaimei iupa sind fraþjaiþ, ni þaim þoei ana airþai sind.
Colossians 3 3 [B] unte gadauþnodeduþ jah libains izwara gafulgina ist miþ Xristau in guda.
Colossians 3 4 [B] þan Xristus swikunþs wairþiþ, libains izwara, (þan)uh jah jus bairhtai wair(þiþ) miþ imma in wulþau.
Colossians 3 5 [B] da(uþ)eiþ nu liþuns izwarans, þans þaiei sind ana airþai, horinassu, unhrainein, winnon, lustu ubila(na) jah faihugeiron, sei ist galiuga(gu)de skalkinassus;
Colossians 3 6 [B] þairh þoei qimiþ hatis gudis ana sunum ungalaubeinais,
Colossians 3 7 [B] in þaimei jah jus iddjeduþ simle, þan libaideduþ in þaim.
Colossians 3 8 [B] iþ nu aflagjiþ jah jus þo alla, hatis, þwairhein, unselein, anaqiss, aglaitiwaurdein; us munþa izwaramma ni usgaggai.
Colossians 3 9 [B] ni liugaiþ izwis misso, afslaupjandans izwis þana fairnjan mannan miþ tojam is,
Colossians 3 10 [B] jah gahamoþ niujamma, þamma ananiwidin du ufkunþja (bi) (fr)isahtai þis, saei gaskop ina;
Colossians 3 11 [B] þarei nist Kreks jah Judaius, bimait jah faurafilli, barbar(us) (jah) (S)kwþus, skalks jah freis, ak alla jah in allaim Xristus.
Colossians 3 12 [B] gahamoþ izwis nu swe gawali(d)ai gudis, weihans jah walisans, brusts bleiþein<s>, [arma(hai)rtein], sele(in), haunein a(hins), qairrein, usbeisnein.
Colossians 3 13 [B] þulandans iz(wis) misso jah fragibandans s(ilban)s, jabai hvas wiþra hvana habai fairina; swaswe jah Xristus fragaf izwis, swa jah jus taujaiþ.
Colossians 3 14 [B] aþþan ufar alla <þo> friaþwa, sei ist gabindi ainamundiþos.
Colossians 3 15 [B] jah gawairþi gudis swignjai[þ] i(n) hairtam izwaraim, in þammei jah laþodai wesuþ in ainamma leika, jah awiliudondans wairþaiþ.
Colossians 3 16 [B] waurd Xristaus bauai in izwis gabigaba, in allai handugein jah frodein ah(mei)nai laisjandans jah talz(ja)ndans izwis silbans psalmom, hazeinim, saggwim ahmeinaim, in (an)stai sigg(w)andans in hair(t)am izwaraim f(raujin).
Colossians 3 17 [B] all þishvah þatei tau(jai)þ in waur(da) aiþþau in waurstwa, (a)ll in namin fraujins Iesuis, awiliudondans guda attin þairh ina.
Colossians 3 18 [B] jus qinons, ufhausjaiþ wairam izwaraim, swe gaqimiþ in fraujin.
Colossians 3 19 [B] wairos, frijoþ qenins izwaros jah ni sijaiþ baitrai (w)iþra þos.
Colossians 3 20 [B] barna, ufhausjaiþ fadreinam bi all; unte þata waila galeikaiþ ist in fraujin.
Colossians 3 21 [B] jus attans, ni gramjaiþ barna izwara du þwairhein, ei ni wairþaina in unlustau.
Colossians 3 22 [B] þewisa, ufhausjaiþ bi all <þaim bi> leika fraujam, ni in augam skalkinondans, swe mannam samjandans, ak in ainfalþein hairtins, ogandans guþ.
Colossians 3 23 [B] þishvah þatei taujaiþ, us saiwalai waurkjaiþ swe fraujin, ni mannam,
Colossians 3 24 [B] witandans þatei af fraujin nimiþ andalauni arbjis; unte fraujin Xristau skalkinoþ.
Colossians 3 25 [B] sa auk skaþaila andnimiþ þatei skoþ, jah nist wiljahalþein at guda.
Colossians 4 1 [B] Jus fraujans, garaiht jah ibnassu þewisam atkunnaiþ, witandans þatei aihuþ jah jus fraujan in himinam.
Colossians 4 2 [B] bidai ha(f)tjandans izwis, wakandans in izai in awiliudam;
Colossians 4 3 [B] bidjandans samana jah bi uns ei guþ uslukai unsis haurd waurdis du rodjan runa Xristaus, in þizozei jah gabundans im,
Colossians 4 4 [B] ei gabairhtjau þo, swaswe skuljau rodjan.
Colossians 4 5 [B] in handugein gaggaiþ du þaim uta, þata mel usbugjandans.
Colossians 4 6 [B] waurd izwar sinteino in anstai salta gasupoþ siai, ei witeiþ hvaiwa skuleiþ ainhvarjammeh andhafjan.
Colossians 4 7 [B] þatei bi mik ist, all gakanneiþ izwis Twkekus, sa liuba broþar jah triggwa andbahts jah gaskalki in fraujin,
Colossians 4 8 [B] þanei insandida du izwis duþþe ei kunnjai hva bi izwis ist, jah gaþrafstjai hairtona izwara,
Colossians 4 9 [B] miþ Aunisimau þamma liubin jah triggwin broþr, saei ist us izwis, þaiei all izwis gakannjand þatei her ist.
Colossians 4 10 [B] goleiþ izwis Areistarkus, sa miþfrahunþana mis, jah Markus gadiliggs Barnabins, bi þanei nemuþ anabusnins, ei jabai qimai at izwis, andnimaiþ ina;
Colossians 4 11 [B] jah Iesus, saei haitada Justus, þaiei sind us bimaita. þai ainai gawaurstwans sind þiudangardjos gudis, þaiei wesun mis du gaþrafsteinai.
Colossians 4 12 [B] goleiþ izwis Aipafras, sa us izwis, skalks Xristaus Iesuis, sinteino usdaudjands bi izwis in bidom, ei standaiþ allawaurstwans jah fullawitans in allamma wiljin gudis.
Colossians 4 13 [B] weitwodja auk imma þatei habaiþ manag aljan bi izwis jah bi þans þaiei sind in Laudeikaia jah Iairaupaulein.
Colossians 4 14 [B] goleiþ izwis Lukas, leikeis sa liuba.
Colossians 4 15 [B] goleiþ þans in Laudeikaia broþruns jah Nwmfan jah þo ingardjon is aikklesjon.
Colossians 4 16 [B] jah þan ussiggwaidau at izwis so aipistaule, taujaiþ ei jah in Laudekaion aikklesjon ussiggwaidau, jah þoei ist us Laudeikaion, jus ussiggwaid.
Colossians 4 17 [B] jah qiþaiþ Arkippau: saihv þata andbahti þatei andnamt in fraujin, ei ita usfulljais.
Colossians 4 18 [B] du Kaulaussaium ustauh.
