1 Thessalonians 2 10 [B] . . . . jah guþ, hvaiwa weihaba jah garaihtaba jah unfairinodaba izwis þaim galaubjandam wesum,
1 Thessalonians 2 11 [B] swaswe wituþ ainhvarjanoh izwara, swe atta barna seina, bidjandans izwis jah gaþlaihandans,
1 Thessalonians 2 12 [B] jah weitwodjandans du gaggan izwis wairþaba gudis, saei laþoda izwis du seinai þiudangardjai jah wulþau.
1 Thessalonians 2 13 [B] duþe jah weis awiliudom guda unsweibandans, unte nimandans at uns waurd hauseinais gudis andnemuþ ni swaswe waurd manne, ak swaswe ist sunjaba waurd gudis, þatei jah waurkei<þ> in izwis juzei galaubeiþ.
1 Thessalonians 2 14 [B] jus auk galeikondans waurþuþ, broþrjus, aikklesjom gudis þaim wisandeim in Iudaia in Xristau Iesu, unte þata samo wunnuþ jah jus fram izwaraim inkunjam swaswe jah weis fram Iudaium,
1 Thessalonians 2 15 [B] þaiei jah fraujin usqemun Iesua jah swesaim praufetum jah uns frawrekun jah guda ni galeikandans jah allaim mannam andaneiþans sind,
1 Thessalonians 2 16 [B] warjandans uns du þiudom rodjan ei ganisaina, akei du usfulljan seinos frawaurhtins sinteino; aþþan snauh ana ins hatis gudis und andi.
1 Thessalonians 2 17 [B] aþþan weis, broþrjus, gaain[an]aidai af izwis du mela hveilos, andwairþja ni hairtin, ufarassau sniumidedum andaugi izwar[a] gasaihvan in managamma lustau.
1 Thessalonians 2 18 [B] unte wildedum qiman at izwis, ik raihtis Pawlus jah ainamma sinþa jah twaim, jah analatida uns Satana.
1 Thessalonians 2 19 [B] hva auk ist unsara wens aiþþau faheþs aiþþau waips hvoftuljos, niu jus in andwairþja fraujins unsaris Iesuis Xristaus in is quma?
1 Thessalonians 2 20 [B] jus auk siuþ wulþus unsar jah faheþs.
1 Thessalonians 3 1 [B] In þizei ju ni usþulandans þanamais, galeikaida uns ei biliþanai weseima in Aþeinim ainai.
1 Thessalonians 3 2 [B] jah insandidedum Teimauþaiu, broþar unsarana jah andbaht gudis in aiwaggeljon Xristaus, ei izwis gatulgjai jah bidjai bi galaubein izwara,
1 Thessalonians 3 3 [B] ei ni ainshun afagjaidau in þaim aggwiþom; silbans auk wituþ þatei du þamma satidai sijum.
1 Thessalonians 3 4 [B] jah auk þan wesum at izwis, fauraqeþum izwis þatei anawairþ was uns du winnan agliþos, swaswe jah warþ jah wituþ.
1 Thessalonians 3 5 [B] duþþe jah ik ju ni usþulan<d>s insandida du ufkunnan galaubein izwara, ibai aufto usfaifraisi izwis sa fraisands jah sware wairþai arbaiþs unsara.
1 Thessalonians 3 6 [B] aþþan nu at qimandin Teimauþaiu at unsis fram izwis jah gateihandin uns galaubein <jah> friaþwa izwara, jah þatei gaminþi unsar habaiþ god sinteino, gairnjandans uns gasaihvan, swaswe jah weis izwis,
1 Thessalonians 3 7 [B] inuh þis gaþrafstidai sijum, broþrjus, fram izwis ana allai nauþai jah aglon unsarai in izwaraizos galaubeinais;
1 Thessalonians 3 8 [B] unte sai libam, jabai jus gastandiþ in fraujin.
1 Thessalonians 3 9 [B] hva auk awiliude magum usgildan [fraujin] guda bi izwis ana allai fahedai þizaiei faginom in izwara faura guda unsaramma,
1 Thessalonians 3 10 [B] naht jah daga ufarassau bidjandans ei gasaihvaima andwairþja izwara jah ustiuhaima waninassu galaubeinais izwaraizos?
1 Thessalonians 3 11 [B] aþþan silba guþ jah atta unsar jah frauja unsar Iesus Xristus garaihtjai wig unsarana du izwis.
1 Thessalonians 3 12 [B] aþþan izwis frauja managjai jah ganohnan gataujai friaþwai in izwis misso jah allans swaswe jah weis in izwis,
1 Thessalonians 3 13 [B] du tulgjan hairtona izwara u(n)fairinona in weihiþai faura guda jah attin unsaramma in quma fraujins unsaris Iesuis Xristaus miþ allaim þaim weiham seinaim.
1 Thessalonians 4 1 [B] Þannu nu, broþrjus, anahaitam bidai izwis jah bidjam in fraujin Iesua, ei swaswe andnemuþ at uns hvaiwa skuluþ gaggan jah galeikan guda, swa[swe] jah gaggaiþ jah gaaukaiþ mais.
1 Thessalonians 4 2 [B] wituþ auk hvarjos anabusnins atgebum izwis þairh fraujan Iesu Xristu.
1 Thessalonians 4 3 [B] þata auk ist wilja gudis, weihiþa izwara, ei gahabaiþ izwis af kalkinassau[s],
1 Thessalonians 4 4 [B] ei witi hvarjizuh izwara gastaldan sein kas in weihiþai jah sweriþai,
1 Thessalonians 4 5 [B] ni in gairunja lustaus, swaswe jah þiudos þozei ni kunnun guþ,
1 Thessalonians 4 6 [B] ei hvas ni ufargaggai nih bi faihu _ol_ broþar seinana, unte fraweitands frauja ist allaize, swaswe jah fauraqeþum izwis jah weitwodidedum.
1 Thessalonians 4 7 [B] unte ni laþoda uns guþ du unhrainiþai, ak in weihiþa.
1 Thessalonians 4 8 [B] inuh þis nu saei ufbrikiþ, ni mann ufbrikiþ, ak guda, saei gaf ahman seinana weihana izwis.

Philemon 1 17 [A] jabai nu mik habais du gamana, andnim þana swe mik.
Philemon 1 18 [A] iþ jabai hva gaskoþ þus aiþþau skula ist, þata mis rahnei.
Philemon 1 19 [A] ik Pawlus gamelida meinai handau: ik usgiba; ei ni qiþau þus þatei jaþ~þuk silban mis skula is.
Philemon 1 20 [A] jai, broþar, ik þeina niutau in fraujin; anaþrafstei meinos brusts in Xristau.
Philemon 1 21 [A] gatrauands ufhauseinai þeinai gamelida þus, witands þatei jah ufar þatei qiþa taujis.
Philemon 1 22 [A] bijandzuþ~þan manwei mis saliþwos; wenja auk ei þairh bidos izwaros fragibaidau izwis.
Philemon 1 23 [A] goleiþ þuk Aipafras, sa miþfrahunþana mis in Xristau Iesu . . . .
